# cs.AR [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [HGQ-LUT: Fast LUT-Aware Training and Efficient Architectures for DNN Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22293)
*Chang Sun,Zhiqiang Que,Bakhtiar Zadeh,Qibin Liu,Kevin H. Alvarez,Wayne Luk,Maria Spiropulu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出 HGQ-LUT，一种新型查找表感知训练（LUT-aware training, LAT）方法，通过引入基于常规高效张量运算的 LUT-Dense 和 LUT-Conv 层，结合细粒度异构量化与资源代理函数，在 FPGA 上实现超低延迟和卓越硬件效率，同时将训练速度提升超过 100 倍，并集成到开源工具链以支持端到端工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于查找表（Lookup-table, LUT）的神经网络在 FPGA 上可实现超低延迟和出色的硬件效率，但当前的 LUT 感知训练（LUT-aware training, LAT）方法存在三大缺陷：训练速度比传统网络慢数个数量级、需要大量手动调参以实现硬件效率、缺乏端到端工作流，难以在实际中应用。

Method: HGQ-LUT 提出了 LUT-Dense 和 LUT-Conv 层，这些层在训练时使用常规的、对加速器高效（accelerator-efficient）的张量运算实现，训练完成后被编译为逻辑查找表（logic LUT）映射到硬件。同时，该方法结合了细粒度的元素级异构量化（element-wise heterogeneous quantization，包括零比特剪枝）以及一个 LUT 感知的资源代理函数（LUT-aware resource surrogate），从而在没有人工位宽调参的情况下自动探索精度与资源的权衡。

Result: HGQ-LUT 在达到最先进的硬件效率的同时，在现代 GPU 上将训练速度提升了超过 100 倍。该方法被集成到开源工具链中，支持混合架构（混合 LUT 基与常规算术模块）的统一设计、编译和比特精确验证（bit-exact verification）。

Conclusion: HGQ-LUT 使基于 LAT 的深度神经网络（DNN）在实际部署中变得可行，例如应用于欧洲核子研究中心（CERN）大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）的实验场景。

Abstract: Lookup-table (LUT) based neural networks can deliver ultra-low latency and excellent hardware efficiency on FPGAs by mapping arithmetic operations directly onto the logic primitives. However, state-of-the-art LUT-aware training (LAT) approaches remain difficult to use in practice: they are often orders of magnitude slower to train than conventional networks, require non-trivial manual tuning for hardware efficiency, and lack an end-to-end workflow. This work presents HGQ-LUT, integrated in https://github.com/calad0i/HGQ2, a new LAT approach that achieves state-of-the-art hardware efficiency while accelerating training by over 100 times on modern GPUs. HGQ-LUT introduces LUT-Dense and LUT-Conv layers that are implemented with regular, accelerator-efficient tensor operations during training, which are then compiled into logic LUTs for hardware. By combining these layers with fine-grained, element-wise heterogeneous quantization (including zero-bit pruning) and a LUT-aware resource surrogate, HGQ-LUT enables the automatic exploration of accuracy-resource trade-offs without manual bit-width tuning. We further integrate HGQ-LUT into open-source toolchains, enabling unified design, compilation, and bit-exact verification of hybrid architectures that mix LUT-based with conventional arithmetic blocks. These features make LAT-based DNNs practical for real-world deployment, such as at the CERN Large Hadron Collider's experiments.

</details>


<div id='physics.class-ph'></div>

# physics.class-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [How the Hahn-Banach Theorem Sheds Bright Light on Fundamental Questions in Classical Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22717)
*Martin Feinberg,Richard B. Lavine*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了哈恩-巴拿赫定理（Hahn-Banach Theorem）与热力学第二定律（Second Law of Thermodynamics）之间的深刻联系，指出该定理能够从开尔文-普朗克（Kelvin-Planck）形式的第二定律直接导出熵（entropy）和热力学温度（thermodynamic-temperature）函数，并满足克劳修斯-杜海姆不等式（Clausius-Duhem inequality），且无需将定义域限制于平衡态；但唯一性要求每个状态均可通过可逆过程（reversible process）达到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在阐明哈恩-巴拿赫定理与热力学第二定律之间显著但尚未被广泛认识的数学-物理关联，使热力学学者和数学家都能理解这一交叉领域的核心结果。

Method: 以开尔文-普朗克版本的第二定律为出发点，应用哈恩-巴拿赫定理直接导出熵和热力学温度函数，并检验克劳修斯-杜海姆不等式的满足性；同时通过该定理分析函数存在性与唯一性所需的条件。

Result: 对于任意可能过程，哈恩-巴拿赫定理能够立即且同时给出局部材料状态下的熵和热力学温度函数，使其满足克劳修斯-杜海姆不等式，且无需局限于平衡态（equilibrium）；但该函数的全局唯一性要求状态空间中每一个状态都必须被某个可逆过程所访问。

Conclusion: 哈恩-巴拿赫定理是热力学第二定律的自然数学伴侣，其存在性结果不依赖平衡态假设，但唯一性受限于可逆过程的覆盖性；该综述旨在促进两个领域之间的交叉理解。

Abstract: The Hahn-Banach Theorem, a cornerstone of modern functional analysis, is a natural companion of the Second Law of Thermodynamics. From a Kelvin-Planck version of the Second Law, the Hahn-Banach Theorem delivers, immediately and simultaneously, entropy and thermodynamic-temperature functions of the local material state such that the Clausius-Duhem inequality is satisfied for every process a particular material might admit. For \emph{existence} of such functions there is no need at all to require that their domain be restricted to states of equilibrium. However, the Hahn-Banach Theorem also indicates that for \emph{uniqueness} of such a pair of functions across the entire state-space domain, every state must be visited by a reversible process. This review is intended to help make accessible to both thermodynamics scholars and mathematicians the remarkable interplay of the Hahn-Banach Theorem and the Second Law.

</details>

# math.CA [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Skew-orthogonal polynomials for a quartic Freud weight: two classes of quasi-orthogonal polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22616)
*Costanza Benassi,Marta Dell'Atti*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了关于四次Freud权重的斜正交多项式（skew-orthogonal polynomials），提出一种显式方法将任意次斜正交多项式表示为正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials）的线性组合，并通过新的递推关系计算组合系数。进一步发现，奇次和偶次斜正交多项式分别构成关于两类不同半经典Laguerre权重的准正交多项式（quasi-orthogonal polynomials），并首次给出了仅涉及斜正交多项式自身的闭合递推关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 斜正交多项式在随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）和可积系统（integrable systems）中具有重要应用，但关于四次Freud权重的斜正交多项式的系统分析方法尚不充分，缺乏显式构造和高效递推机制。

Method: 提出一种显式方法，将任意次的斜正交多项式构造为正交多项式的线性组合；通过新颖的递推关系（recursive relations）计算组合系数；并识别奇次和偶次斜正交多项式分别对应于两类不同半经典Laguerre权重的准正交多项式。

Result: 成功实现了斜正交多项式任意次数的显式表达；给出了组合系数的递推计算公式；发现了奇次和偶次斜正交多项式与两类半经典Laguerre权重下的准正交多项式之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 首次建立了仅涉及斜正交多项式自身的闭合递推关系，为相关领域（如随机矩阵理论、可积系统）中基于四次Freud权重的分析提供了有效的代数工具。

Abstract: This work is a thorough investigation of skew-orthogonal polynomials with respect to a quartic Freud weight. We provide an explicit method to evaluate skew-orthogonal polynomials of any degree as linear combinations of orthogonal polynomials. The coefficients of these combinations can be evaluated via novel recursive relations. Moreover, we observe that skew-orthogonal polynomials with even and odd degree constitute two families of quasi-orthogonal polynomials with respect to two different semi-classical Laguerre weights, and we provide the first instance of closed recursive relations involving skew-orthogonal polynomials only.

</details>


<div id='math.DG'></div>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Multiplicative Ehresmann connections for Lie groupoid fibrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22394)
*Matthijs Lau,Ioan Mărcuţ*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文引入李群胚（Lie groupoid）上满射淹没（surjective submersion）的乘法Ehresmann联络（multiplicative Ehresmann connection），推广了纤维丛上的经典Ehresmann联络与李群胚扩张上的乘法联络。研究了此类联络的存在性，指出其对一般李群胚（包括proper李群胚）可能不存在，但在Morita淹没、均匀李群胚纤维化（uniform Lie groupoid fibration）等情形下存在正结果。主要结果聚焦于完备性：对于李群胚纤维化，乘法联络的完备性由核丛诱导联络及基联络决定；对于源-proper李群胚族，局部平凡性与完备乘法Ehresmann联络的存在性等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Ehresmann联络（Ehresmann connection）是纤维丛几何的核心工具，近年来被推广为李群胚扩张（Lie groupoid extension）上的乘法联络（multiplicative connection）。本文旨在将这两种概念统一为更一般的框架，系统研究李群胚满射淹没上的乘法Ehresmann联络的存在性与完备性条件。

Method: 采用定义—存在性—完备性的递进结构。首先定义李群胚满射淹没上的乘法Ehresmann联络；然后通过构造反例与正例，系统考察其在各类李群胚（proper、Morita淹没、均匀纤维化等）上的存在性；最后分别针对李群胚纤维化（Lie groupoid fibration）与源-proper李群胚族（families of source-proper Lie groupoids）分析完备性条件。

Result: 存在性方面：一般情形（包括proper李群胚）下此类联络可能不存在；但在Morita淹没（Morita submersion）、均匀李群胚纤维化（uniform Lie groupoid fibration）、局部平凡李群胚族（locally trivial families of Lie groupoids）及proper李群胚族上存在正结果。完备性方面：对于李群胚纤维化，完备性由核丛（kernel bundle）上的诱导联络以及（在连通性假设下）基联络共同决定；对于源-proper李群胚族，局部平凡性与完备乘法Ehresmann联络的存在性等价。

Conclusion: 本文建立的乘法Ehresmann联络框架统一了纤维丛与李群胚扩张中的联络理论，揭示了其在广泛几何结构中的存在性与完备性条件，为李群胚的几何与拓扑研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: We introduce multiplicative Ehresmann connections on surjective submersions of Lie groupoids, extending both the classical notion of Ehresmann connections on fibre bundles and the more recent notion of multiplicative connections on Lie groupoid extensions. We investigate the existence of such connections, showing that, in general, they may fail to exist even for proper Lie groupoids. In contrast, positive results hold for Morita submersions, uniform Lie groupoid fibrations, locally trivial families of Lie groupoids, and proper families of Lie groupoids. Our main results concern completeness. For Lie groupoid fibrations, we prove that the completeness of a multiplicative connection is governed by the induced connection on the kernel bundle and, under connectivity assumptions, by the base connection. For families of source-proper Lie groupoids, we prove the equivalence between local triviality and the existence of complete multiplicative Ehresmann connections.

</details>


### [5] [Timelike Ricci curvature lower bounds via optimal transport for Orlicz-type Lorentzian costs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22538)
*Argam Ohanyan,Marta Sálamo Candal*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文在全局双曲时空上研究了与Orlicz型Lorentzian代价函数相关联的最优输运问题，将已有的$p \in (0,1)$和$p<0$情形推广到更一般的单调递增凹函数$u$；通过引入$u$-分离性质并证明强对偶性，最终利用Orlicz型最优输运沿测地线的相对熵凸性刻画出类时Ricci曲率下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的Lorentzian最优输运问题仅考虑了幂函数形式的代价函数$u_p(x) = p^{-1}x^p$，覆盖了$p \in (0,1)$以及较新的$p<0$情形。本文旨在将这些特例统一并推广到更广泛的Orlicz型代价函数族，从而建立更一般的理论框架。

Method: 本文采用由单调递增凹函数$u$与时间分离函数$\ell$复合而成的Orlicz型Lorentzian代价函数$u \circ \ell$；引入了测度对之间的$u$-分离（$u$-separation）性质，该性质推广了McCann的$p$-分离（$p$-separation），并基于此证明了对完整的Orlicz型优化问题的强对偶性（strong duality）。

Result: 类时Ricci曲率（timelike Ricci curvature）的下界可以通过Orlicz型最优输运沿测地线的相对熵（relative entropy）凸性来刻画，这是McCann在$u = u_p$（$p \in (0,1)$）情形下开创性工作的深远推广。

Conclusion: 通过引入更一般的代价函数和$u$-分离概念，本文成功将Lorentzian最优输运与Ricci曲率下界的等价刻画从幂函数情形推广至Orlicz型函数族，为广义相对论和几何分析中的曲率-输运联系提供了更具包容性的理论工具。

Abstract: We study the optimal transport problem on globally hyperbolic spacetimes associated with Orlicz-type Lorentzian cost functions of the form $u \circ \ell$, where $u$ is a suitable monotonically increasing and concave function, and $\ell$ is the time separation. Our work encompasses and generalises the case $u(x) = u_p(x) = p^{-1}x^p$ for $p \in (0,1)$, as well as the more recent $p < 0$, which have been the only examples considered so far in the literature. A fundamental notion for our purposes is the property of $u$-separation for a pair of measures, which generalises McCann's $p$-separation and for which we are able to obtain strong duality to the full Orlicz-type optimization problem. In our main results, we characterise timelike Ricci curvature lower bounds via the convexity of the relative entropy along geodesics arising from the Orlicz-type optimal transport with cost $u \circ \ell$, which is a far-reaching generalization of McCann's seminal work in the case $u = u_p$, $p \in (0,1)$.

</details>


<div id='gr-qc'></div>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Perturbation Dynamics and Structure Formation in Extended Proca-Nuevo Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21962)
*N. S. Kavya,Avik De,Tee-How Loo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对扩展Proca-Nuevo（EPN）框架——一种包含有质量自旋-1场的矢量-张量广义相对论扩展理论——建立了宇宙学微扰与结构形成的完整分析框架，推导了规范不变的线性微扰方程，讨论了稳定性条件，为后续观测检验奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在矢量-张量修正引力理论中，EPN框架作为广义相对论（General Relativity）的推广，其宇宙学层面的微扰理论和结构形成机制尚未被系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，为该理论提供与宇宙学观测对接的理论基础。

Method: 在假设最小物质耦合（minimal matter coupling）的前提下，采用规范不变形式（gauge-invariant form）导出线性微扰方程；通过分析EPN扇区引入的有效各向异性应力（effective anisotropic stress）以及单个传播标量模式与度规势的耦合，研究物质不均匀性的增长过程。

Result: EPN框架中，矢量场通过代数约束（algebraic constraint）修改背景膨胀，产生一种在ΛCDM极限之间插值并在中间红移处引入偏差的特征性哈勃演化。物质增长方程形式上保持广义相对论（GR）的形式，但其膨胀历史被修改。完整标量微扰系统已给出，稳定性条件得到讨论。

Conclusion: 本文的分析为利用当前及未来的宇宙学观测检验EPN框架提供了理论基础与计算工具。

Abstract: A comprehensive analysis of cosmological perturbations and structure formation is presented for the Extended Proca-Nuevo (EPN) framework, a vector-tensor extension of General Relativity with a massive spin-1 field. In this scenario, the vector field modifies the background expansion through an algebraic constraint, leading to a characteristic Hubble evolution that interpolates between $Λ$CDM limits while introducing deviations at intermediate redshifts. Assuming minimal matter coupling, the linear perturbation equations are derived in gauge-invariant form and the resulting growth of matter inhomogeneities is analyzed. The EPN sector induces effective anisotropic stress and couples a single propagating scalar mode to the metric potentials, leaving the matter growth equation in its GR form but with a modified expansion history. The full scalar perturbation system is presented, stability conditions are discussed, and the results provide a foundation for testing the EPN framework against current and future cosmological observations.

</details>


### [7] [A New Spin on Dissipative Tides: First-Post-Newtonian Effects in Compact Binary Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21990)
*Anand Balivada,Abhishek Hegade K. R.,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发展了自旋致密双星中耗散性电四极潮汐力的次领头阶后牛顿（post-Newtonian）描述，推导了质心运动方程、广义能量平衡律以及准圆轨道下的傅里叶相位修正。研究表明，自旋诱导的潮汐耗散在2.5后牛顿阶进入引力波（gravitational wave）相位，并携带对数频率依赖，不会与并合相位简并。对于双黑洞系统，该耗散流在极端质量比极限下重现了视界吸收，并指出了等质量情况下的红移相关修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋致密双星在旋近晚期，潮汐耗散会对引力波信号（gravitational-wave signal）产生特征修正。现有模型缺乏次领头阶精度的耗散性潮汐描述，亟需发展更精确的理论框架来满足高信噪比时代对引力波波形的精密建模需求。

Method: 采用最一般的、与旋转对称性（rotational symmetry）兼容的低频线性潮汐响应理论，在次领头阶后牛顿框架下推导自旋致密双星中耗散性电四极潮汐（electric-quadrupolar tides）的质心运动方程、广义能量平衡律（generalized energy-balance law），以及自旋与轨道角动量对齐或反对齐准圆轨道对应的傅里叶相位修正（Fourier-phase correction）。

Result: 自旋诱导的潮汐耗散在2.5后牛顿阶（post-Newtonian order）进入引力波相位，并携带对数频率依赖（logarithmic frequency dependence），因此不与并合相位（coalescence phase）简并。对于双黑洞（binary black holes），该耗散流在极端质量比极限下重现了视界吸收（horizon absorption），并指出等质量情况下的红移相关修正（redshift-related correction）可能未包含在近期某些世界线有效场论（worldline effective field theory）计算中。

Conclusion: 这些结果为高信噪比时代自旋致密双星的精密波形建模提供了新的波形要素（waveform ingredients），有助于提升对引力波信号的解读精度。

Abstract: Tidal dissipation in spinning compact binaries imprints characteristic corrections on the late-inspiral gravitational-wave signal. We develop a next-to-leading order post-Newtonian description of dissipative, electric-quadrupolar tides in spinning compact binaries, deriving the center-of-mass equations of motion, a generalized energy-balance law, and the corresponding Fourier-phase correction for quasi-circular orbits with spins aligned or anti-aligned with the orbital angular momentum. Using the most general, low-frequency, linear tidal response compatible with rotational symmetry, we show that spin-induced tidal dissipation enters the gravitational-wave phase at 2.5 post-Newtonian order and carries a logarithmic frequency dependence, so it is not degenerate with the coalescence phase. For binary black holes, our dissipative flux reproduces horizon absorption in the extreme-mass-ratio limit and points to a redshift-related correction in the comparable-mass case potentially not included in certain recent worldline effective field theory calculations. These results provide new waveform ingredients for precision modeling of spinning compact binaries in the high-signal-to-noise era.

</details>


### [8] [Data-Driven Acceleration of Eccentricity Reduction for Binary Black Hole Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22021)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟中降低轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）是构建天体物理相关引力波模型的关键。现有迭代方案需要四次或更多试模拟才能达到目标偏心率阈值，每次试模拟增加约10%的运行时间（总长达数周至数月），计算成本极高。

Method: 采用数据驱动方法，利用高斯过程回归（Gaussian Process Regression）模型，基于已有偏心率降低的数值相对论模拟存档进行训练。模型学习初始轨道频率（Omega_0）和径向速度（adot_0）的最优取值，直接为新的模拟配置提供低偏心率的初始参数。

Result: 在所有测试的配置中，训练后的模型一致地将所需偏心率降低迭代次数减少至仅0次或1次，相较于基于后牛顿（post-Newtonian）初始猜测的传统方法，显著降低了计算成本。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，数据驱动方法能够有效加速昂贵的数值相对论模拟，为双黑洞引力波建模提供了更高效的计算路径。

Abstract: Reducing orbital eccentricity in numerical relativity simulations of binary black holes is essential for producing astrophysically relevant gravitational wave models, as many of these systems are expected to be near-circular in nature. Standard eccentricity reduction procedures rely on iterative schemes, often requiring four or more trial simulations to achieve desired thresholds. This approach is computationally expensive because each trial simulation adds ~10% to the total simulation run time of multiple weeks to months. We introduce a data-driven approach that accelerates this process by learning the values of the initial orbital frequency, Omega_0, and radial velocity, adot_0, that yield an evolution with small eccentricity. This is done using a Gaussian Process Regression model trained on an archive of previously eccentricity-reduced numerical relativity simulations. For all configurations tested, using the trained model consistently reduces the number of required eccentricity reduction iterations to just zero or one, significantly lowering computational costs relative to post-Newtonian initial guesses. These results demonstrate the power of data-driven methods in accelerating expensive numerical relativity simulations.

### [9] [Shadow dependent phenomenology framework for rotating black hole metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22181)
*Nikko John Leo S. Lobos,Emmanuel T. Rodulfo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个热力学-光学对偶（thermodynamic-optical duality），将黑洞的半经典量子蒸发与其经典宏观几何直接联系起来。通过微分同胚反演，将无法观测的裸质量重新参数化为可观测的阴影半径，从而绕过裸质量直接表述经典弱偏转角、霍金温度（Hawking temperature）和半经典积分光度。应用于标准Kerr、Kerr-MOG和旋转Horndeski时空后，该对偶揭示了模型特有的现象学特征，并能在事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测约束下有效检验Kerr假设并探测修改引力中的基本场。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微分同胚反演（diffeomorphic inversion），将黑洞内禀质量完全重新参数化为可观测的阴影半径；进而基于该映射构建经典的弱偏转角、霍金温度及半经典积分光度的表达式，完全绕过不可观测的裸质量；将该方法应用于标准Kerr、Kerr-MOG和旋转Horndeski三种时空模型。

Result: 标准Kerr几何在统计固定的阴影半径下产生基线光度标度律 $L \propto R_{sh}^{-2}$。MOG排斥矢量场增强经典偏转并严格抑制量子光度；Horndeski标量毛发在引力透镜中引入独特的对数增广，并在当前EHT限制下导致霍金辐射出现约52%的偏差。

Conclusion: 该框架通过将理论可观测量严格锚定于经验干涉测量边界，提供了一条计算高效的途径来检验Kerr假设并探测强场引力中的基本场。

Abstract: We establish a thermodynamic-optical duality that directly bridges the semiclassical quantum evaporation of black holes with their classical macroscopic geometry. By employing a diffeomorphic inversion, we re-parameterize the intrinsic black hole mass entirely in terms of the observable shadow radius $R_{sh}$. This mapping allows the formulation of the classical weak deflection angle, Hawking temperature, and integrated semiclassical luminosity, bypassing the unobservable bare mass. Applying this methodology to the standard Kerr, Kerr-MOG, and rotating Horndeski spacetimes, we reveal distinct, model-specific phenomenological signatures. For a statistically fixed shadow radius constrained by Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observations of M87*, the standard Kerr geometry yields a baseline luminosity scaling of $L \propto R_{sh}^{-2}$. In modified gravity regimes, the duality breaks the degeneracy between bare mass and modified field strengths: the MOG repulsive vector field enhances classical deflection while strictly suppressing quantum luminosity, whereas Horndeski scalar hair introduces a unique logarithmic augmentation to astrometric lensing and drives up to a $\sim 52\%$ deviation in Hawking emission under current EHT limits. By strictly anchoring theoretical observables to empirical interferometric boundaries, this framework provides a computationally efficient avenue for testing the Kerr hypothesis and probing fundamental fields in strong-field gravity.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证此前工作中得到的势函数是否为平坦FLRW宇宙中标量场Eisenhart提升背景下允许非平凡共形Killing矢量的最一般局域势，并检验先前采用的ansatz是否完备。

Method: 分析共形Killing方程的可积性条件（integrability conditions），将延长后的共形Killing方程的行列式条件约化为关于h=V'/V的非线性二阶微分方程，并对其局域求解。

Result: 行列式条件约化为非线性二阶微分方程，局域求解得到两个分支：正则分支（regular branch）精确复现了此前得到的势函数族；奇异分支（singular branch）位于行列式方程无法以h''为正常形式局域写出的奇异点集上，且与完整共形Killing方程不相容。

Conclusion: 先前工作中使用的ansatz是完备的（exhaustive），所得到的势函数已是该框架下最一般的局域势形式。

Abstract: We study the integrability conditions of the conformal Killing equations for the Eisenhart lift of a scalar field in a flat Friedmann-Lema\^ıtre-Robertson-Walker universe. We show that the potential found in our earlier work is already the most general local potential that admits a non-trivial conformal Killing vector in the sector independent of the cyclic Eisenhart coordinate. The determinant condition of the prolonged conformal Killing equations reduces to a nonlinear second-order differential equation for $h=V'/V$. We solve this equation locally and find two branches. The regular branch reproduces exactly the family of potentials obtained before, while the singular branch lies on the locus where the determinant equation cannot be written locally in normal form with respect to $h''$ and is incompatible with the full conformal Killing equations. Hence the ansatz used in our earlier work is exhaustive.

Abstract: We investigate the spacetime geometry of a black hole solution coupled to a nonlinear Born-Infeld-type electrodynamics of the Kruglov form, taking into account the effective geometry governing photon propagation. Our analysis focuses on the role of parameter $q$, which controls deviations from Maxwell electrodynamics. We study observational signatures including light deflection, the black holes shadow, and images of a thin accretion disk. We find that the effective photon geometry induces significant modifications to null trajectories, leading to systematic $q$-dependent shifts in the deflection angle, shadow radius, and lensing observables. In particular, smaller positive values of $q$ enhance light bending, while negative values produce the opposite trend. Moreover, the efective geometry admits stable photon orbits outside the event horizon in certain regions of parameter space, together with nonstandard (reversal direction of) angular behavior of photon trajectories. These features leave distinct imprints on accretion disk images, especially in the structure and visibility of photon rings.

### [12] [Simulation-based Inference for Gravitational Waves from Binary Neutron Stars: Application of Summary Data from Heterodyning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22380)
*Masaki Iwaya,Vivien Raymond,Soichiro Morisaki,Kazuki Takada*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星（BNS）系统的引力波参数估计因信号持续时间长（可达数分钟）而面临严峻计算挑战；神经后验估计（NPE）虽能大幅加速，但需要有效的高维输入数据降维。

Method: 基于相对分箱（relative binning）形式化，利用后牛顿近似（post-Newtonian approximation）的频带（frequency banding）构建波形比的多项式近似，生成似然导向汇总统计量（likelihood-oriented summary statistics），将原始频域数据压缩为汇总数据，仅需约O(1000)个波形采样点。

Result: 训练后的NPE网络在1024次BNS注入测试中，对照传统嵌套抽样（nested sampling）方法，所有源参数的后验分布均良好校准；大部分参数的Jensen-Shannon散度（JSD）与数值噪声一致，但当前配置下最不一致参数的中位JSD超过10^{-2}比特。

Conclusion: 所提压缩策略使训练与存储成本均较已有BNS推理网络更高效，展示了快速参数估计的潜力。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave parameter estimation for binary neutron star (BNS) systems poses severe computational challenges due to the extended signal duration, which can reach several minutes in current detectors. Neural posterior estimation (NPE), a simulation-based inference approach, offers dramatic speedups but requires effective dimensionality reduction of the high-dimensional input data. We present a novel compression strategy based on likelihood-oriented summary statistics derived from the relative binning formalism of Zackay et al. (2018), which compresses raw frequency-domain data into the summary data. The summary data is based on a polynomial approximation of the waveform ratio using frequency banding grounded in post-Newtonian approximation, and directly evaluated with only $O(1000)$ sample points of the waveform. As a result, both the training and storage cost become more efficient than previously reported networks for BNS inference. We train a set of NPE networks on these summary statistics and validate a network against traditional nested sampling over 1024 BNS injections. The network produces well-calibrated posteriors across all source parameters we consider, with Jensen-Shannon divergences (JSD) consistent with numerical noise for most parameters. Although we find that the median JSD for the most inconsistent parameter exceeds $10^{-2}$ bits with current configurations, our results show potential for rapid parameter estimation of the BNS signal.

### [13] [Kahler decoupling for Kerr perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22424)
*Stephen R. Green,Kirill Krasnov,Adam Shaw*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Euclidean Kerr度规与Kähler度规之间的两种共形等价关系，并证明了这种隐藏的Kähler结构为曲率标量（如Teukolsky方程）中解耦方程的存在提供了几何解释。解耦机制源于Kähler背景上自对偶2-形式在自然协变导数下的平行性质，从而保持了微分算子的分解且不混合分量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Teukolsky方程等解耦方程的存在提供几何解释，阐明其与Kähler几何的内在联系。

Method: 通过分析Euclidean Kerr度规与Kähler度规的两种共形等价关系，利用Kähler背景上自对偶2-形式（self-dual 2-forms）在自然协变导数下的平行性质，推导解耦机制；并分别通过自旋-k（spin-k）Teukolsky算子的相似变换以及电磁扰动的共形不变性两种方式对该机制进行显式展示。

Result: 证明了自旋-k Teukolsky算子可通过相似变换从Kähler度规相关的Laplace型算子得到；对于电磁扰动，利用Maxwell方程的共形不变性，推导出自动解耦的方程，其极端分量与自旋-1 Teukolsky方程一致。

Conclusion: Kerr度规中曲率标量的解耦方程是Kähler几何结构的直接结果，而非巧合。

Abstract: The Euclidean Kerr metric is conformal, in two distinct ways, to a Kahler metric, with conformal factors determined by the repeated eigenvalue of the two chiral halves of the Weyl curvature. A Lorentzian analogue holds, where the conformally related metric is complex but retains key features of Kahler geometry. We show that this hidden Kahler structure provides a geometric explanation for the existence of decoupled equations for curvature scalars, such as the Teukolsky equations. The essential mechanism is that, on a Kahler background, self-dual 2-forms are parallel with respect to a natural covariant derivative, so differential operators acting on them preserve their decomposition and do not mix components. In this way, decoupling is seen to be a direct consequence of Kahler geometry. We make this mechanism explicit in two ways. First, we show that the spin-k Teukolsky operator can be obtained from a Laplace-type operator associated with the Kahler metric by a similarity transformation. Second, for electromagnetic perturbations, we use the conformal invariance of Maxwell's equations delta F = 0 to show that they imply d delta F = 0, where delta is the co-differential of the Kahler metric. This operator automatically decouples, and the resulting equations for the extremal components coincide with the spin-one Teukolsky equations.

### [14] [Spontaneous spherical symmetry breaking of black holes with resonant hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22437)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现，带有共振毛的黑洞解在非球对称动力学下是不稳定的。根据所选解的类型，不稳定性会触发两种不同的衰变通道：通过裂变分裂为一个玻色子团和一个无毛黑洞，或通过吸收坍缩为后者。第二种自相互作用模型的结果表明，这种不稳定性可能对不同类别的自相互作用具有普遍性。

Conclusion: 带有共振毛的黑洞解是动力学不稳定的，其最终命运要么通过裂变分裂为玻色子团和无毛黑洞，要么通过吸收坍缩为无毛黑洞。在这两种情况下，非球对称动力学（non-spherical dynamics）都是关键因素。

Abstract: Black holes with resonant hair are static, spherical, electrically charged solutions of the Einstein-Maxwell-(gauged-)scalar system. Scalar self-interactions are mandatory for their existence. Initial dynamical studies restricted to spherical symmetry suggested stability; more recently, fully non-spherical dynamical studies revealed instabilities, at least for a particular class of self-interactions. Here, we provide a more detailed study of this instability together with a different decay channel, depending on the chosen solutions. Moreover, considering a second model, we provide evidence that the instabilities may be generic for different classes of self-interactions. We conclude these solutions are dynamically unstable and split into a bosonic lump and a bald black hole (via fission) or implode to the latter (via absorption). In both cases, the non-spherical dynamics seems to be key.

Conclusion: 基于Rényi熵修正的Friedmann方程模型能够成功描述晚期宇宙加速膨胀，统计比较、能量条件（energy conditions）评估及稳定性分析均支持其作为标准宇宙学模型（ΛCDM）的一个稳健替代方案。

Abstract: We explore a cosmological model based on Rényi entropic corrections to the Friedmann equations and constrain it using DESI, P-BAO, CC, and gravitational-wave observations. Unlike earlier works, we obtain a direct and stringent constraint on the Rényi parameter $λ$ from late-time cosmic acceleration, with the resulting value even satisfying recent Big Bang Nucleosynthesis and baryogenesis bounds. The model predicts values of $H_0$ and $Ω_{m0}$ that are consistent with current observational data. It provides a successful description of late-time acceleration with a quintessence-like behavior, smoothly approaching the $Λ$CDM limit without crossing the phantom divide. Furthermore, the statical comparisons along with the evaluation of energy conditions and stability analyses reinforce its viability as a robust alternative to the standard cosmological model.

</details>


### [16] [Preserving the Energy-Momentum Tensor in f(R, Matter) Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22623)
*Szőllősi Tamás-Géza*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Herglotz变分原理（Herglotz variational principle）的f(R, Matter)引力理论扩展，通过将物质-几何非最小耦合导致的能量-动量张量非守恒解释为有效耗散过程，并证明在适当的Herglotz贡献下，该扩展理论可恢复能量-动量张量的协变守恒（covariant conservation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将能量-动量张量的非守恒性解释为有效耗散过程（effective dissipative process），并采用Herglotz变分原理（Herglotz variational principle）来构建f(R, Matter)引力理论的一般性框架。该变分原理专门适用于耗散系统（dissipative systems）。

Result: 通过对Herglotz贡献项进行适当选择，所得到的Herglotz扩展形式下的f(R, Matter)引力能够恢复能量-动量张量的协变守恒（covariant conservation）。

Conclusion: Herglotz变分原理为处理修正引力中的非守恒问题提供了一种有效的变分方法，能够在保持理论框架一致性的前提下恢复守恒律。

Abstract: In certain modified theories of gravity, non-minimal couplings between matter and geometry lead to the nonconservation of the energy-momentum tensor. By interpreting this as an effective dissipative process, we formulate a general class of f(R, Matter) theories with the Herglotz variational principle, a variational approach designed for dissipative systems. We demonstrate that, for an appropriate choice of the Herglotz contribution, the resulting Herglotz extension of f(R, Matter) gravity restores the covariant conservation of the energy-momentum tensor.

### [17] [Quasinormal Modes and Neutrino Energy Deposition for a Magnetically Charged Black Hole in a Hernquist Dark Matter Halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22684)
*Ali Ovgun,Reggie C. Pantig,Joel Saavedra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在携带非线性电动力学（NED）磁荷且嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕的静态球对称黑洞背景下，系统研究了拟正则模、阴影观测量、弱引力透镜以及中微子-反中微子湮灭过程。发现磁荷与暗物质晕对各项观测量的影响方向相反，在一定参数下可部分抵消，揭示出近视界磁结构与延展暗物质环境之间的竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常单独考虑黑洞内部结构（如磁荷）或外部环境（如暗物质晕）对可观测量的影响，缺乏同时纳入两者的统一解析框架。本文旨在构建一个同时包含非线性电动力学磁荷与Hernquist暗物质晕的简单解析黑洞模型，以便系统比较磁结构与暗物质环境对引力波、成像、透镜和高能中微子湮灭过程的竞争性贡献。

Method: 采用静态球对称黑洞度规，由质量M、磁荷g和暗晕参数(α,β)共同控制。推导标量、电磁和轴向引力主方程，利用高阶WKB展开结合Padé求和计算拟正则模谱。通过eikonal近似建立拟正则谱与光子球及阴影半径的联系。针对中微子-反中微子湮灭，计算包含角因子、Tolman红移T^9核、积分沉积率和约化壳层轮廓的完整公式。

Result: 磁荷提高实部振荡频率并略微增大阻尼率，而Hernquist暗晕产生相反方向的谱移，适当参数下两者可部分抵消。在固定渐近质量M=M+α下，NED和暗晕集中项的残余效应使阴影和弱偏转角在首个非平凡阶上小于Schwarzschild情形。磁荷抑制中微子湮灭效率，暗晕通过降低lapse函数增强该效率。

Conclusion: 环down（ringdown）、成像、透镜和高能沉积观测从不同权重探测同一物理竞争——近视界磁结构与延展暗物质环境之间的相互作用。该模型为同时研究致密天体内部和环境形变提供了简单的解析平台。

Abstract: We investigate quasinormal modes, shadow observables, weak gravitational lensing, and neutrino--antineutrino annihilation for a static, spherically symmetric black hole that carries a nonlinear-electrodynamics magnetic charge and is embedded in a Hernquist dark-matter halo. The geometry is controlled by the black-hole mass $M$, magnetic charge $g$, and halo parameters $(α,β)$, and provides a simple analytic setting in which compact-object and environmental deformations can be studied simultaneously. We derive the scalar, electromagnetic, and axial gravitational master equations and compute the corresponding quasinormal spectra using a high-order WKB expansion supplemented by Pade resummation. The magnetic charge raises the real oscillation frequency and slightly increases the damping rate, whereas the Hernquist halo shifts the spectrum in the opposite direction; for suitable parameters the two effects partially cancel at the level of individual modes. We then connect the eikonal spectrum with the photon sphere and shadow radius, emphasizing the distinction between comparisons performed at fixed bare mass and at fixed asymptotic mass $\mathcal{M}=M+α$. At fixed asymptotic mass, the residual NED and halo-concentration terms reduce the shadow and the weak-deflection angle relative to Schwarzschild at the first nontrivial order. Finally, we formulate neutrino-pair annihilation in the same background, including the angular factor, Tolman-redshifted $T^9$ kernel, integrated deposition rate, and reduced shell profile. The magnetic sector suppresses the annihilation efficiency, while the halo sector enhances it through its lowering of the lapse. These results show that ringdown, imaging, lensing, and high-energy deposition probe the same underlying competition between near-horizon magnetic structure and extended dark-matter environment, but with different parameter weights.

</details>


### [18] [Gauge-independent approach to inflation in quadratic gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22725)
*Adrian Palomares,Ying-li Zhang,Jinsu Kim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了二次引力（quadratic gravity）中线性宇宙学扰动的标量部分。通过在爱因斯坦帧（Einstein frame）中采用规范无关的方法，推导出运动方程并用三组规范不变变量（gauge-invariant variables）表达。在超视界极限（superhorizon limit）下，发现牛顿规范（Newtonian gauge）中的度规扰动呈现指数增长（exponential growth），但这种表观不稳定性是规范依赖的（gauge-dependent），在其他规范中扰动行为良好。该不稳定性被识别为规范赝像（gauge artefact），而非理论本身的病态。同时，分析了规范不变变量在帧变换（frame transformation）下的演化行为变化，并厘清了乔丹帧（Jordan frame）与爱因斯坦帧结果之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次引力中的宇宙学扰动稳定性问题尚需澄清，特别是需要区分真正的物理效应与规范赝像（gauge artefacts），并评估不同规范下扰动行为的可靠性。

Method: 在爱因斯坦帧中采用规范无关的方式推导线性宇宙学标量扰动的运动方程，使用三组规范不变变量（gauge-invariant variables）来区分物理效应与规范赝像；在超视界极限（superhorizon limit）下分析变量的主导行为，并对比多种常用规范（gauges）下的扰动演化。

Result: 牛顿规范（Newtonian gauge）中出现了度规扰动的指数增长（exponential growth），表现为表观不稳定性；然而该不稳定性在其他规范中不出现，扰动在微扰区间内保持良好行为。该增长被证实为非普遍且规范依赖的（gauge-dependent），属于规范赝像（gauge artefact）而非理论本身的病态。

Conclusion: 二次引力中的宇宙学扰动在物理上是稳定的，表观不稳定性源于规范选择（gauge choice）而非理论内在缺陷；物理可观测量可一致地计算。研究还阐明了规范不变变量在帧变换（frame transformation）下的演化行为变化，并明确了乔丹帧（Jordan frame）与爱因斯坦帧结果之间的关系。

Abstract: We investigate the scalar sector of linear cosmological perturbations in quadratic gravity. Working in the Einstein frame, we derive the equations of motion in a gauge-independent manner and express them in terms of three sets of gauge-invariant variables. This approach allows us to distinguish genuine physical effects from gauge artefacts, which is particularly relevant for assessing the stability of perturbations in this theory. In the superhorizon limit, we obtain the leading-order behaviour of the relevant gauge-invariant variables and analyse the perturbations in several commonly used gauges. We find that the Newtonian gauge exhibits an apparent instability, characterised by the exponential growth of the metric perturbations. However, this growth is non-generic and gauge-dependent; in the other gauges analysed in this work, the perturbations remain well behaved within the perturbative regime. Physical observables can thus be consistently computed, and the apparent instability is identified as a gauge artefact rather than a pathology of the theory. Our analysis also demonstrates how the evolution behaviour of a gauge-invariant variable changes under the frame transformation and clarifies the relation between results obtained in the Jordan and Einstein frames.

</details>


### [19] [Radiation outer boundary conditions and near-to-far field signal transformations for the Bardeen-Press equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22734)
*Som Dev Bishoyi,Scott E. Field,Stephen R. Lau*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对极端质量比旋进等天体物理问题中Teukolsky方程的时间域求解，开发并实现了精确的辐射外边界条件与近远场传送核，使人工边界透明、消除非物理的长时增长，并通过指数求和近似保证计算效率与误差可控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限计算域上数值求解自旋权重$s=-2$的Teukolsky方程（Teukolsky equation）时，引入的人工外边界若施加不精确的边界条件，会产生虚假反射（spurious reflections）和缓慢增长的非物理模，污染长时演化结果。因此需要构造精确的辐射外边界条件以消除这些人为误差。

Method: 基于Bardeen-Press方程（Bardeen-Press equation，$a=0$的Teukolsky方程在调和矩下的形式），推导并实现了精确辐射外边界条件（exact radiation outer boundary conditions），使任意有限半径处的人工边界透明。同时构建了近远场传送核（near-to-far field teleportation kernels），将有限半径$r_1$处的场数据映射到$r_2>r_1$处的数据，包括$r_2=\infty$对应渐进波形到未来零无穷（future null infinity）的传播。边界核与传送核均通过指数求和（exponential sums）进行良好近似并附有误差界（error bounds）。

Result: 在时间域求解器中实现了基于核的边界条件后，消除了非物理的晚时增长（unphysical late-time growth），获得了正确的晚时衰减率（correct late-time decay rates），从而能够高效进行长时程模拟。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于指数求和近似的边界条件与传送核方法为引力波波形建模及相关黑洞摄动计算（blackhole perturbation calculations）提供了一种高效、精确的长时程模拟方案。

Abstract: Several theoretical and astrophysical problems - including gravitational-wave modeling for extreme mass-ratio inspirals - require accurate time-domain solutions of the spin-weight $s=-2$ Teukolsky equation in Boyer-Lindquist coordinates. Because such simulations are performed on finite computational domains, they typically introduce an artificial outer boundary where nontrivial boundary conditions must be imposed. If these conditions are inaccurate, then spurious reflections and slowly-growing unphysical modes may corrupt long-time evolutions. We develop and implement exact radiation outer boundary conditions for the Bardeen-Press equation (a harmonic moment of the $a=0$ Teukolsky equation), making the artificial boundary transparent at any finite radius. We also construct near-to-far field teleportation kernels that map field data recorded at finite radius $r_1$ to the data reaching $r_2 > r_1$. The possible choice $r_2 = \infty$ corresponds to asymptotic waveform evaluation, that is propagation of the data to future null infinity. We show that both boundary and teleportation kernels are well approximated by exponential sums, with associated error bounds. Implemented in a time-domain solver, our kernel-based boundary conditions eliminate unphysical late-time growth and give the correct late-time decay rates, affording efficient long-duration simulations for waveform modeling and related blackhole perturbation calculations.

</details>

### [20] [Signature of paraparticles: a minimal Gedankenexperiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22178)
*Francesco Toppan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对置换群（permutation group）交换的准粒子（paraparticles），提出一个最小化理论测试方案（Gedankenexperiment），将该类准粒子的检测与工程化问题映射为手征性测试（chirality test），为实验实现提供操作流程图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然任意子（anyons）已在实验中探测到，但通过置换群交换的准粒子（permutation-group parastatistics）尚未被实验验证。近期理论工作表明，在某些情况下可回避长期存在的“统计惯例性（conventionality of parastatistics）”论证，故亟需一个最小实验方案来指导实验检测或工程化实现这类准粒子。

Method: 本文提供一个思想实验（Gedankenexperiment），本质上是逻辑运算的流程图；该方案是2021年发表的两个理论测试的简化版本。检测与工程化被映射为手征性测试，数学基础基于Z₂×Z₂阶化色彩李（超）代数（Z₂×Z₂-graded color Lie (super)algebras）及其衍生数学结构。

Result: 该最小化方案展示了如何在实验室中模拟或实现检测步骤，可能通过操控qudit（多能级量子比特）来完成。关键结果是，置换群准粒子的探测可归结为对手征性这一可观测特征的检验。

Conclusion: 本文为实验物理学家提供了实现置换群统计（permutation-group parastatistics）准粒子检测或工程化的必要步骤，填补了理论预言与实验实现之间的空白。

Abstract: Paraparticles beyond bosons and fermions can be exchanged via either the braid group (anyons, existing up to $D=2$ space dimensions) or the permutation group; in the latter case the space dimensions are not limited. Besides being predicted, anyons have been experimentally detected. The situation differs for paraparticles exchanged via the permutation group ("permutation-group parastatistics").The first test to detect their theoretical signature was published in 2021 (for $Z_2\times Z_2$-graded parafermions; it was soon followed by a second paper proving the detectability of $Z_2\times Z_2$-graded parabosons). Later on, two further papers proved theoretical signatures of permutation-group parastatistics. These works demonstrate that, in certain situations, a long-held belief on the "conventionality of parastatistics" argument can be evaded: some measurements of permutation-group paraparticles cannot be recovered from ordinary bosons/fermions. The main question now is how to experimentally detect or engineer in the laboratory such paraparticles. For this aim a minimal setup for the theoretical test is here provided: a Gedankenexperiment (a simplified version of the two tests published in 2021) which, essentially, is a flow chart of logical operations. The key point is to present, to experimentalists, the necessary steps to be simulated/realized in the laboratory (possibly, by manipulating qudits). In this minimal setup, the detection/engineering of paraparticles is mapped into a chirality test. The mathematical setting is based on $Z_2\times Z_2$-graded color Lie (super)algebras and derived mathematical structures.

</details>


### [21] [On truncations of hierarchical equations of motion for finite-dimensional systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22568)
*Vasilii Vadimov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了对于有限维开放量子系统，采用舒尔补型终结子（Schur-complement type of terminator）对分级运动方程（HEOM）进行截断近似时，其谱会收敛到完整HEOM的谱，且不会产生虚假不稳定模式（spectral pollution）。并以自旋-玻色子模型（spin-boson model）进行了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于有限维开放量子系统（finite-dimensional open quantum systems），分级运动方程（hierarchical equations of motion, HEOM）的截断近似在数值模拟中广泛应用，但其截断深度的收敛性以及是否会产生虚假谱污染（spectral pollution）尚未得到严格证明。

Method: 采用基于舒尔补型终结子（Schur-complement type of terminator）构建有限维近似的方法，从谱分析（spectral analysis）角度对截断后的HEOM进行了理论证明。

Result: 证明了随着截断深度增加，有限维近似的谱收敛到完整HEOM的谱；同时证明了若精确HEOM是稳定的，足够深的截断不会产生虚假不稳定模式（spurious unstable modes）。

Conclusion: 所提出的舒尔补型截断方案在理论上保证了谱收敛性和无谱污染特性，并通过自旋-玻色子模型（spin-boson model）进行了数值验证。

Abstract: We study truncations of hierarchical equations of motion (HEOM) for finite-dimensional open quantum systems. We prove that for finite-dimensional approximations constructed with a Schur-complement type of terminator, the spectrum converges to that of the full HEOM as the truncation depth increases. We also prove that this approximation is free of spectral pollution: sufficiently deep truncations do not produce spurious unstable modes, provided the exact HEOM is stable. We illustrate the results for the spin-boson model.

</details>


### [22] [Two flavor neutrino oscillations in presence of non-Hermitian dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22421)
*Kritika Rushiya,Gaurav Hajong,Bhabani Prasad Mandal,Poonam Mehta*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为非厄米动力学下的中微子振荡建立了统一的数学框架，比较了正定度量算子（$\mathcal{G}$-metric）与Brody-Graefe密度矩阵方案，发现$\mathcal{G}$-度量方案在$\mathcal{PT}$-对称情形下（包括$\mathcal{PT}$-未破缺和破缺区域）概率不守恒，而密度矩阵方案能给出正半定映射，且在稳态极限下概率不等于$1/2$，表明系统呈现非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为非厄米动力学下两味中微子振荡（two flavor neutrino oscillations）提供一致的数学框架，并比较不同方案的有效性。

Method: 采用两种方案：(a) 基于正定度量算子 $\mathcal{G}$ 定义的双正交内积（bi-orthonormal inner product）；(b) Brody和Graefe提出的密度矩阵方案（density matrix prescription），后者是一个正半定映射（positive semi-definite map）。

Result: 在$\mathcal{PT}$-对称（$\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric）情形下，$\mathcal{G}$-度量方案在$\mathcal{PT}$-未破缺和$\mathcal{PT}$-破缺区域均不适用（概率不守恒）；密度矩阵方案在稳态极限（steady state limit）下的概率不一定等于$1/2$，表明存在非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）行为。

Conclusion: 对于非厄米动力学下的中微子振荡，密度矩阵方案优于$\mathcal{G}$-度量方案，且系统表现出非马尔可夫行为，这挑战了传统马尔可夫近似下的中微子振荡模型。

Abstract: We develop a consistent mathematical framework for studying two flavor neutrino oscillations in presence of non-Hermitian dynamics. We consider two approaches : (a) bi-orthonormal inner product defined by a positive-definite metric operator $\mathcal{G}$ and (b) the density matrix prescription by Brody and Graefe [Phys. Rev. Lett. 109, 230405 (2012)]. For the $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric case, we show that the $\mathcal{G}$ metric approach does not work well (probabilities are not conserved) both in $\mathcal{PT}$-unbroken as well as $\mathcal{PT}$-broken regime. Hence, we adopt the density matrix prescription by Brody and Graefe which is a positive semi-definite map. In the density matrix prescription, we note that probability in the steady state limit is not necessarily $1/2$ thereby indicating non-Markovian behavior.

</details>


### [23] [Entanglement and information scrambling in long-range measurement-only circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22022)
*Abigail McClain Gomez,Fiona Abney-McPeek,Hong-Ye Hu,Susanne F. Yelin,Ceren B. Dağ*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模克利福德（Clifford）模拟，研究一维纯测量（measurement-only）电路中长程两量子比特奇偶校验（parity check）导致的纠缠与信息相变，揭示了超出纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）分类的新型物相，并将轨迹平均纠缠熵映射至二维统计力学（statistical mechanics）模型，建立了从体积律（volume-law）到亚体积律（sub-volume-law）纠缠相变与连续对称性破缺相及临界XY相边界之间的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯测量电路为多体纠缠的产生与调控提供了最小化设置，可能展现出无幺正类比（unitary counterpart）的动力学相变。现有研究对长程测量协议下的相图尚未充分理解，需要超越纠缠熵的探针进行系统性分类。

Method: 采用一维测量-only克利福德电路，引入长程两量子比特奇偶校验测量，通过随机基（random-basis）与单基（single-basis）两种协议进行大规模克利福德模拟。扩展基于副本（replica）的方法将轨迹平均纠缠熵映射至二维统计力学模型，并在连续时间极限下得到稳态有效长程XX哈密顿量。

Result: 通过调节测量范围（measurement range）与每层密度，发现需借助互信息（mutual information）、三方互信息（tripartite mutual information）、辅助比特纯化（purification from an ancilla）及贝尔簇统计（Bell-cluster statistics）等探针才能完整分类的多种物相。在随机基电路中，体积律到亚体积律的纠缠相变对应于连续对称性破缺相与临界XY相之间的边界。在结构化单基电路中，发现一类新相：体积律与长程纠缠共存，同时辅助比特实现快速、与系统尺寸无关的纯化，且无置乱（scrambling）现象。

Conclusion: 纯测量电路为高效制备高度纠缠且具有技术实用价值的量子态提供了新途径，其丰富的相行为超越了传统幺正电路框架下的分类体系。

Abstract: Measurement-only circuits provide a minimal setting in which repeated local projections can either generate or suppress many-body entanglement, giving rise to measurement-induced phase transitions and dynamical regimes, that might have no unitary counterpart. Here we investigate entanglement and information transitions in one-dimensional measurement-only Clifford circuits with long-range two-qubit parity checks. By tuning both the measurement range and density per layer, we uncover a broad set of phases whose classification requires probes beyond entanglement entropy, such as mutual information, tripartite mutual information, purification from an ancilla, and Bell-cluster statistics. We map phase diagrams using large-scale Clifford simulations for two protocols: a random-basis design in which each measurement is randomly chosen from $\lbrace XX,YY,ZZ \rbrace$, and a single-basis design in which the basis is fixed within each layer but varies between layers, hence introducing more structure to the circuit.
  We map the trajectory-averaged entanglement entropy to a two-dimensional statistical mechanics model by extending a replica-based method to random-basis measurement-only circuits, and show that a continuous-time limit yields an effective long-range XX hamiltonian in the steady state. This connection links the observed volume-law to sub-volume-law entanglement transition to the boundary between a continuous symmetry broken phase and a critical XY phase. Strikingly, in structured (single-basis) circuits we find a phase in which volume-law and long-range entanglement coexists with rapid, size-independent purification of an ancilla qubit, and the absence of scrambling, highlighting measurement-only circuits as a promising route to efficiently preparing highly entangled and technologically useful quantum states.

</details>


### [24] [Tantalum Damascene Coplanar Waveguide Resonators Fabricated Using 300 mm Scale Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22086)
*Ekta Bhatia,Yingge Du,Krishna P Koirala,Chung Kow,Mingzhao Liu,Juan Macy,Tharanga R. Nanayakkara,Francisco Ponce,Satyavolu S. Papa Rao,Drew J. Rebar,Peter V. Sushko,Brent A VanDevender,Chongmin Wang,Marvin G. Warner,Zhihao Xiao*

Motivation: 超导transmon器件中的表面氧化物会引起损耗，导致器件性能下降。因此，寻找一种有效方法减少或替代这些氧化物，以提高器件性能，是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 采用大马士革工艺（damascene process），将器件的侧壁本征氧化物替换为金属/基底界面。在 fabrication 过程中埋入氧化层，以此模拟侧壁的氧化情况。

Result: 对比两种类型器件，观察到适度的性能改进，表明表面参与比（surface participation ratio）可能有所降低。

Conclusion: 大马士革工艺可能通过降低表面参与比来减少超导transmon器件的表面损耗，从而提升器件性能。

Abstract: Surface oxides contribute to losses in superconducting transmon devices resulting in degraded performance. We explore the use of the damascene process to replace the sidewall native oxide of a device with a metal/substrate interface. We simulate sidewall oxidation by burying an oxide layer during fabrication. We observe a modest improvement between the two types of devices, which is suggestive of a reduction in the surface participation ratio.

### [25] [No-Go Theorem for Quantum Heat Engines Powered Purely by Quantum Measurements in the Steady Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22376)
*Kenta Koshihara,Kazuya Yuasa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了纯粹由量子测量（quantum measurement）反作用注入能量驱动的热力学引擎，并证明在稳态循环中，缺乏反馈控制（feedback control）或热接触（thermal contact）等熵减过程时，无法从该引擎提取功（work）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究仅由量子测量反作用（measurement backaction）驱动的引擎是否能在稳态循环中持续做功，从而揭示量子测量在热力学循环（thermodynamic cycle）中的能量注入与功提取的极限。

Method: 采用有限维工作物质（finite-dimensional working substance）的量子热力学模型，基于一般量子信道（quantum channel）的庞加莱式回归定理（Poincaré-like recurrence theorem），对纯由量子测量驱动的引擎进行稳态分析。

Result: 证明了在稳态（steady regime）下，量子测量变为非扰动的（nondisturbing），不再向工作物质注入能量，因此无法提取功。

Conclusion: 稳态循环的测量驱动引擎若要实现功提取，必须引入反馈控制或热接触等熵减过程（entropy-decreasing process）。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics of a quantum measurement-powered engine that converts energy injected by measurement backaction into work. We consider an engine with a finite-dimensional working substance, driven purely by quantum measurements, i.e., by bare quantum measurements, without feedback control or thermal contact in the thermodynamic cycle. On the basis of a Poincaré-like recurrence theorem for general quantum channels, we prove a no-go result for work extraction from such an engine in the steady regime. In the steady regime, quantum measurements become nondisturbing and do not inject energy into the working substance. Consequently, no work can be extracted. This result reveals the necessity of an entropy-decreasing process, such as feedback control or thermal contact, for work extraction in steady-cycle measurement-powered engines.

### [26] [Quantum limits on squeezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22500)
*Xin Zhou,Francesco Massel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明玻色子模式网络中的正则对易关系（canonical commutation relations）对输入模式与内部模式的系数施加约束，基于此推导出储层工程（reservoir-engineered）压缩方案中总稳态压缩（steady-state squeezing）的下界，并揭示独立参量驱动（parametric driving）可改变量子噪声-增益平衡，从而获得更优的压缩界。此外，该约束还可将三模玻色子系统的Duan不可分离性判据（Duan inseparability criterion）重新表述为单一参数依赖的品质因子（figure of merit）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示正则对易关系对玻色子模式网络在压缩动力学中所施加的基本约束，从而推导储层工程压缩方案的性能极限，并探究该约束能否推广至多模不可分离性判据的简化表达。

Method: 基于正则对易关系对输入模式与内部模式间系数的约束，推导稳态正交方差（quadrature variances）归一化总和的下界；考虑独立参量驱动项时重新分析量子噪声-增益平衡，获得不同的最优界；将相同约束应用于三模系统的Duan判据，构造参数依赖的品质因子。

Result: 仅由正则对易关系与稳定性导出的下界在强耦合极限（strong-coupling limit）下饱和于1；加入独立参量驱动后最优界趋近1/2。三模玻色子系统的Duan不可分离性判据可被简化为单一参数依赖的品质因子。

Conclusion: 所得下界具有普遍性，适用于当前机电和纳米力学实验（electromechanical and nanomechanical experiments），且两模压缩界即使在室温条件下也具备实验可达性。

Abstract: In our work, we show how, for a network of bosonic modes, canonical commutation relations constrain the coefficients relating input and internal modes. Based on these constraints, we derive a lower bound on the total steady-state squeezing achievable in reservoir-engineered (dissipative) squeezing schemes, quantified by the sum of mode-optimal quadrature variances normalized to its corresponding input variance. The bound follows solely from canonical commutation relations and stability, and is saturated in the strong-coupling limit at 1. Furthermore, we show that adding independent parametric driving terms for each mode changes the quantum noise-gain balance and yields a distinct optimum bound, approaching 1/2. In addition, we show how these constraints allow us to reformulate the Duan inseparability criterion for a three-mode bosonic system in terms of a single parameter-dependent figure of merit. Our results apply directly to current electromechanical and nanomechanical experiments and indicate that the two-mode bounds can be experimentally approached even at room temperature.

### [27] [Decohered color code and emerging mixed toric code by anyon proliferation: Topological entanglement negativity perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22521)
*Keisuke Kataoka,Yoshihito Kuno,Takahiro Orito,Ikuo Ichinose*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究颜色码（color code）在退相干（decoherence）作用下如何产生一种内在混合态拓扑序（intrinsic mixed-state topological order, imTO），该相在局域有能隙哈密顿量的纯基态中没有对应物。通过规范固定（gauging）方法和拓扑纠缠负性（topological entanglement negativity, TEN）分析，发现退相干后的混合态类似于单个环面码（toric code），且TEN随退相干强度出现平滑交叉与方差峰值，揭示了基于负性（negativity）的量可作为探测退相干诱导混合态拓扑序的有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索颜色码在退相干下能否涌现出纯基态中不存在的内在混合态拓扑序，并建立相应的表征与探测方法。

Method: 利用针对混合稳定子态（mixed stabilizer states）的规范固定过程；计算拓扑纠缠负性（TEN）；进行高效的稳定子形式（stabilizer-formalism）模拟。

Result: 纯颜色码的TEN为2 ln 2，最大退相干态降至ln 2，表明涌现出单个环面码；TEN随退相干强度出现平滑交叉，其方差呈现显著且几乎与系统尺寸无关的峰值；负性仅在与涌现环面码的三角晶格（triangular lattice）相称的子区域划分下表现出特征标度（characteristic scaling）。

Conclusion: 退相干可以诱导出纯基态中不存在的内在混合态拓扑序，且基于负性的量是探测该类拓扑序的有力探针。

Abstract: We study how the color code under decoherence gives rise to an intrinsic mixed-state topological order (imTO), which has no counterpart in pure ground states of local gapped Hamiltonians. For decoherence induced by XX-type operators on red links of the honeycomb lattice, we show that the resulting mixed state inherits half of the topological properties of the color code, including anyon content, logical operators, and topological entanglement structure. Using a gauging procedure for mixed stabilizer states, we identify the emergent phase as closely related to a single toric code. We characterize this phase by topological entanglement negativity (TEN) and perform efficient stabilizer-formalism simulations. While the pure color code has ${\rm TEN} = 2 \ln 2$, the maximally decohered state has ${\rm TEN} = \ln 2$, indicating emergence of a single toric code. By tuning the decoherence strength, we find a smooth crossover in TEN accompanied by a pronounced, nearly system-size-independent peak in its variance. We further show that the negativity exhibits characteristic scaling only for subsystem partitions commensurate with the triangular lattice of the emergent toric code. Our results demonstrate that negativity-based quantities provide powerful probes of mixed-state topological order generated by decoherence.

### [28] [Stability Thresholds for Gravitationally Induced Entanglement in Shielded Setups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22593)
*Jan Bulling,Marit O. E. Steiner,Julen S. Pedernales,Martin B. Plenio*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了引力诱导纠缠（GIE）实验中残余粒子-屏蔽相互作用带来的噪声源，指出Casimir力和磁偶极相互作用会通过相位积累、退相干以及屏蔽热振动导致的假纠缠信号严重限制GIE实验的有效性，并提出了抑制这些噪声的定量阈值与缓解策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在引力诱导纠缠（gravitationally induced entanglement, GIE）实验中，通常使用法拉第屏蔽层（Faraday shield）来抑制两个大质量粒子之间的直接电磁相互作用。然而，对于超导粒子，其巨大抗磁性（diamagnetism）需要额外磁屏蔽来抑制磁偶极相互作用。因此，有必要系统分析残余的粒子-屏蔽相互作用对GIE实验的潜在影响。

Method: 本文通过理论分析，分别研究了Casimir相互作用和磁偶极相互作用（magnetic-dipole interactions）在粒子与屏蔽层之间残余耦合下的效应；定量评估了实验装置各元件（包括屏蔽层、俘获势阱和探测器）的位置与取向的逐次运行涨落如何将这些相位转化为有效退相干（decoherence）；并进一步将屏蔽层的振动模式进行量子力学处理，分析其热振动对粒子-屏蔽关联以及假纠缠信号的影响。

Result: 研究结果表明，Casimir力和磁偶极相互作用均会通过印刻大相位严重限制GIE测试；运行间的涨落会将这些相位转化为有效退相干，大幅降低可探测的双粒子纠缠信号。特别地，超导屏蔽层与粒子之间的磁相互作用构成了主要噪声源。屏蔽层的热振动不仅会产生持久的粒子-屏蔽关联，还可能介导类引力信号的粒子-粒子假纠缠。

Conclusion: 本文推导了观测真实GIE信号所需的最大可容忍位置与取向涨落的定量阈值，并提出了包括几何结构优化和屏蔽层冷却在内的缓解策略（mitigation strategies），以保留真实的引力诱导纠缠特征。

Abstract: Proposed experiments for gravitationally induced entanglement (GIE) typically suppress direct electromagnetic interactions between two massive particles by inserting a conducting Faraday shield. For superconducting particles, their large diamagnetism requires additional magnetic shielding to screen magnetic dipolar interactions. Here, we analyze the effect of residual particle-shield interactions and show that both Casimir and magnetic-dipole interactions can severely limit GIE tests by imprinting large phases. We quantify how run-to-run positional and orientational fluctuations of the setup elements, including the shield, trapping potentials, and detectors, convert these phases into effective decoherence, strongly reducing the detectable bipartite entanglement. In particular, we show that magnetic interactions between the particles and a superconducting shield constitute a major noise source, especially relevant for levitated superconducting particles. Treating the vibrational modes of the shield quantum mechanically, we further find that thermal vibrations generate persistent particle-shield correlations and can even mediate particle-particle entanglement that can mimic a gravitational signal. Finally, we derive quantitative thresholds on the maximum tolerable positional and orientational fluctuations of the setup elements required to observe entanglement, and propose mitigation strategies including geometry optimization and shield cooling to preserve a genuine GIE signature.

</details>


### [29] [Approaching the Limit of Quantum Clock Precision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22704)
*Chad Nelmes,Emanuel Schwarzhans,Tony Apollaro,Timothy Spiller,Irene D'Amico*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由时间无关相互作用控制的量子钟（quantum clock）蓝图，通过在耗散自旋链（dissipative spin chains）中设计相干输运，达到了精度-分辨率权衡基本界限的标度指数，并引入了一种快速淬火协议（sudden-quench protocol），该协议对分离时机不精确具有鲁棒性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确且自主的钟在基础研究和实际应用中都具有重要意义，因此需要设计一种在物理上可实现且实验上可触及的高精度量子钟系统。

Method: 采用精心设计的相干输运方法在耗散自旋链中实现时间无关的相互作用；引入快速淬火协议，通过简单的初始化和分离机制实现反复操作。

Result: 在精度-分辨率权衡基本界限上达到了标度指数（scaling exponent）；所提出的协议对分离时机的不精确具有鲁棒性，意味着即使由精度较低的时钟驱动也能实现高精度计时。

Conclusion: 该量子钟蓝图在物理现实和实验可及系统中具有可行性，其鲁棒性特征为高精度计时提供了实用前景。

Abstract: Precise and autonomous clocks are of fundamental interest and central importance to both foundational studies and practical applications. Here, we construct a blueprint for a quantum clock governed by time-independent interactions. By carefully-engineered coherent transport in dissipative spin chains, we achieve a scaling exponent at the precision-resolution trade-off fundamental bound, bringing this within reach of physically realistic and experimentally accessible systems. We further introduce a sudden-quench protocol that enables repeated operation through a simple initialization and detachment mechanism. Remarkably, the protocol is robust to imprecise detachment timing, implying that high-precision timekeeping can be achieved even when driven by a clock with much lower precision.

### [30] [D-branes and fractional instantons on a twisted four torus: the moduli space as an N=2 supersymmetric Higgs branch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21980)
*Erich Poppitz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过D膜世界体积理论，将带't Hooft扭曲的四环面上SU(N)杨-米尔斯理论中拓扑荷Q=r/N的自对偶瞬子嵌入其中，构建了缠绕交叉膜结构。研究发现该模空间局部等价于N=2超对称理论的希格斯支，具有显式的超凯勒结构，旨在帮助理解Q<1及Q≥1瞬子的模空间全局结构与时空依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解带't Hooft扭曲的四环面上SU(N)杨-米尔斯理论中拓扑荷Q=r/N的瞬子（instanton）模空间全局结构尚不明确，尤其是当所有模被激发时瞬子的时空依赖性。本文旨在通过D膜方法简化对该模空间的描述，并为最终与ADHM解在无穷体积极限下的匹配提供线索。

Method: 通过将自对偶瞬子嵌入D膜的（D-brane）世界体积理论（worldvolume theory），构建与一般常场强瞬子背景对偶的缠绕交叉膜构型（wrapped intersecting brane configuration），并利用N=2超对称理论（supersymmetric theory）的希格斯支（Higgs branch）局部描述模空间。

Result: 模空间局部可被识别为N=2超对称理论的希格斯支，该参数化与近期场论结果等价，但构造更为简洁并具有显式的超凯勒（hyper-Kähler）结构。对于整数Q，预期在适当无穷体积极限下与ADHM解（ADHM solution）一致。

Conclusion: D膜视角为带扭曲的四环面上瞬子模空间提供了更高效的描述，有望帮助理解Q<1瞬子（全部模被激发后具有时空依赖性）以及Q≥1瞬子的模空间全局结构，并提示整数Q瞬子可在无穷体积极限下与ADHM解匹配。

Abstract: We study self-dual instantons of topological charge $Q=r/N$, for any natural $r$, in $SU(N)$ Yang-Mills theory on a four torus with 't Hooft twists, by embedding them into worldvolume theories of $D$-branes. To study their moduli, we construct the wrapped intersecting brane configurations dual to general constant field strength instanton backgrounds. We show that, locally, the moduli space is identified with the Higgs branch of an $N=2$ supersymmetric theory. This parameterization of the moduli space is equivalent to one recently found in field theory, but is obtained with significantly less effort and has manifest hyper-K\" ahler structure. Our hope is that combining different perspectives on instantons on the twisted torus will help understand the still unknown global structure of the moduli space for general solutions with $Q=r/N$ as well as the nature of instantons with all moduli turned on -- when some $Q<1$ and all $Q \ge 1$ instantons become space-time dependent. For integer $Q$, these are expected to match the ADHM solution in an appropriately taken infinite volume limit.

### [31] [A Physicist's Visit to Exotic Spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21997)
*Tancredi Schettini Gherardini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文利用理论物理中的解析与计算工具（包括纤维丛、瞬子、扭曲自对偶性、Kaluza-Klein假设及机器学习），研究了与普通7维球面同胚但不微分同胚的奇异7维球面（exotic 7-spheres），特别是Gromoll-Meyer球面的几何与拓扑性质，并提出了一个基于机器学习的黎曼爱因斯坦度量数值算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异球面是微分拓扑与广义相对论交叉领域的重要研究对象。本文旨在通过理论物理工具，深入理解Gromoll-Meyer球面的几何结构，并探索奇异球面与广义相对论的联系。

Method: 回顾了纤维丛（fibre bundles）与瞬子（instantons）理论及其与杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）的关系，推广了自对偶性（self-duality）至扭曲自对偶性（twisted self-duality）。通过束论论证驱动的Kaluza-Klein假设，推导了Gromoll-Meyer球面上的黎曼度量族，并将其重写为四元数值对象（quaternionic-valued objects）进行几何分析。此外，提出了一个基于机器学习、高度可推广的数值算法，用于在任意流形上寻找黎曼爱因斯坦度量（Riemannian Einstein metrics）。

Result: 推导了Gromoll-Meyer球面上一个黎曼度量族的解析表达式；识别出具有最大等距群（maximal isometry）的度量，并研究了其曲率性质及相关的能量条件（energy conditions）。讨论了奇异7维球面与普通球面之间同胚映射（homeomorphism）的显式实现及其在广义相对论中的可能解释。展示了基于机器学习的爱因斯坦度量算法的当前应用进展。

Conclusion: 论文提供了奇异球面几何与拓扑的跨学科视角，结合微分拓扑与广义相对论给出了新诠释。所提出的机器学习算法具有高度可推广性，为在奇异球面上寻找爱因斯坦度量提供了新工具。最后讨论了多项未来研究方向。

Abstract: This thesis discusses exotic 7-spheres, i.e. manifolds that are homeomorphic but not diffeomorphic to the ordinary 7-sphere, using a set of analytical and computational tools from theoretical physics. The theory of fibre bundles and instantons, together with their relation to Yang-Mills theory, are reviewed, before presenting a generalisation of self-duality to twisted self-duality. The formalism required to derive and geometrically interpret some solutions to twisted-self-duality is relevant to the main subject of this thesis: investigating the geometry of the Gromoll-Meyer sphere. Through a Kaluza-Klein ansatz, motivated by bundle-theoretic arguments, an analytic expression for a family of Riemannian metrics on the Gromoll-Meyer sphere is derived. After a detailed study of its geometric constituents, recast as quaternionic-valued objects, the metric with maximal isometry is identified. Its curvature properties are also studied and the associated energy conditions are assessed. Then, an up-to-date and broader overview on the current work concerning exotic spheres and exotic manifolds in general is offered, before focusing again on the Gromoll-Meyer sphere, but this time under the lens of differential topology. Some explicit realisations of the homeomorphism between an exotic 7-sphere and an ordinary one are discussed, together with their possible interpretations in the context of general relativity. Finally, a numerical algorithm for finding Riemannian Einstein metrics on arbitrary manifolds is presented; it is based on machine learning, and highly generalisable in many directions. The current work on implementing its application to exotic spheres is also discussed. The thesis ends with an ample discussion of possible future directions.

</details>


### [32] [Black Hole Response Theory and its Exact Shockwave Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22009)
*Lara Bohnenblust,Carl Jordan Eriksen,Jitze Hoogeveen,Gustav Uhre Jakobsen,Jan Plefka*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了适用于引力自力（gravitational self-force）展开的世界线量子场论（WQFT）的黑洞响应形式化，通过整合世界线和引力子涨落得到关联的引力子响应函数，并以Aichelburg-Sexl冲击波为例展示了该框架如何精确求和到冲击波度规，并精确计算了离壳引力子两点响应函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界线量子场论（WQFT）方法在黑洞引力自力（gravitational self-force）展开中的应用尚不充分，缺少一个系统的响应函数形式化来连接世界线自由度与引力子涨落，从而为高阶后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）计算提供基础框架。

Method: 通过将世界线和引力子涨落积分掉（integrating out），定义了零阶响应（zeroth response）一点函数、一阶响应（first response）两点函数及更高阶的有效顶点，构建了引力自力（gravitational self-force）展开的系统框架；对质量为零的主源（对应Aichelburg-Sexl冲击波），通过重求和（resummation）获得精确的冲击波度规和测地线，并精确计算了离壳引力子两点响应函数。

Result: 一点响应重求和得到精确的冲击波度规；重求和的探针顶点再现了该背景中的精确测地线；离壳引力子两点响应函数在引力耦合常数G上精确求出；对于在壳外引力子，得到了包含反冲的引力波散射精确转移矩阵（transfer matrix）；后闵可夫斯基展开指数化为紧凑形式，其中Born项被包含Weinberg相位在内的整体相位所修饰。

Conclusion: 该黑洞响应形式化为未来在超高能区（ultra high-energy regime）进行一阶自力（1SF）水平上的可观测量（如脉冲和波形）计算提供了基本的WQFT工具。

Abstract: We develop a black hole response formulation of worldline quantum field theory (WQFT) adapted to the gravitational self-force expansion. Integrating out the worldline and graviton fluctuations yields connected graviton response functions: the "zeroth response" one-point function encodes the exact background metric, the "first response" two-point function describes the scattering of a gravitational wave off the black hole, and higher-point functions provide effective vertices for a systematic gravitational self-force (SF) expansion. As a first application, we consider a massless primary source, corresponding to the Aichelburg-Sexl shockwave or an ultra-boosted black hole. We show that the one-point response resums to the exact shockwave metric and that the resummed probe vertices reproduce the exact geodesics in this background. We then compute the off-shell graviton two-point response exactly in the gravitational coupling $G$ by resumming the full post-Minkowskian series. For on-shell external gravitons this yields the exact transfer matrix for gravitational-wave scattering off the shockwave, including recoil. The PM expansion exponentiates to a compact form in which the Born term is dressed by an overall phase which includes the Weinberg phase. Our results provide the basic WQFT ingredients for future 1SF computations of observables such as the impulse and waveform in the ultra high-energy regime.

### [33] [Minisuperspace Double Copy in Lifshitz Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22066)
*Mehmet Kemal Gümüş*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文针对各向异性Lifshitz时空，建立了一种经典双重复制（classical double copy）的迷你超空间（minisuperspace）表述，将引力系统约化为有效一维径向问题，并识别出可直接从约化引力动力学中复制麦克斯韦算子（Maxwell operator）的径向算子，同时证明了该框架在更高曲率理论中的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典双重复制旨在建立引力理论与规范理论之间的对偶关系，但现有框架在处理各向异性（anisotropic）时空结构时面临困难。本文旨在为非相对论性Lifshitz时空提供一种系统化的经典双重复制构造方法。

Method: 通过在作用量层面施加静态对称性（static symmetries），将引力系统约化为具有普适结构的有效一维径向问题，所有理论依赖由单个势函数（potential）捕获。识别出一种径向算子（radial operator），其无需借助运动方程即可从约化引力动力学直接复制出单副本场（single-copy field）时间分量的麦克斯韦算子。

Result: 对于非相对论性Lifshitz背景，该关系因一个编码偏离最大对称性（maximal symmetry）的额外贡献而发生修正；该修正项源自各向异性标度（anisotropic scaling）和视界几何（horizon geometry），并在相对论极限下光滑消失。哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）施加后，物质扇区生成相应的源项（source term），在Kerr-Schild描述存在时复现已知的单副本电荷密度，并可推广至超出该描述的范畴。该机制在更高曲率理论中同样成立，此时有效势被替换为其高阶推广，算子结构保持不变。

Conclusion: 通过显式的Lifshitz黑洞解以及爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力（Einstein–Gauss–Bonnet gravity）中带电荷反德西特（charged AdS）解的相对论极限验证，确认了该形式体系的一致性。该框架为各向异性时空中的经典双重复制提供了统一且普适的构造途径。

Abstract: We develop a minisuperspace formulation of the classical double copy for anisotropic Lifshitz spacetimes in arbitrary dimension. By imposing static symmetries at the level of the action, the gravitational system reduces to an effective one-dimensional radial problem with a universal structure, in which all theory dependence is captured by a single potential. Within this framework, we identify a radial operator that reproduces the Maxwell operator for the temporal component of the single-copy field directly from the reduced gravitational dynamics, without using the equations of motion.
  For non-relativistic Lifshitz backgrounds, this relation is modified by an additional contribution that encodes the deviation from maximal symmetry. We show that this term has a universal origin, determined by anisotropic scaling and horizon geometry, and that it vanishes smoothly in the relativistic limit. After imposing the Hamiltonian constraint, the matter sector generates the corresponding source term, reproducing known single-copy charge densities when a Kerr--Schild description exists and extending them beyond this setting.
  We further demonstrate that the same mechanism persists in higher-curvature theories, where the effective potential is replaced by its higher-order generalization while preserving the operator structure. Explicit Lifshitz black hole solutions illustrate how matter content and horizon topology enter the construction. As an additional check, we verify the consistency of the formalism in the relativistic limit using a charged AdS solution in Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet gravity.

TL;DR: 本文研究二维环面上带量子化磁通量 M 的复标量场的真空期望值。发现存在临界面积：当环面超过此面积时真空期望值非零，且该期望值必然依赖于环面坐标。通过最低模近似，M=1 时得到单一真空构型，M=2 和 M=3 时分别得到两个和六个简并真空构型，并分析了这些构型的对称性保持或自发破缺行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究带量子化磁通量（quantized magnetic flux）的二维环面上复标量场（complex scalar field）的真空期望值（vacuum expectation value）行为，特别是临界面积的存在性以及真空构型的简并与对称性性质。

Method: 采用最低模近似（lowest-mode approximation）方法，对二维环面上具有量子化磁通量 M 的复标量场系统进行分析，分别计算不同磁通量子数下的真空构型数量。

Result: 发现了临界面积（critical area）：当环面面积超过该临界值时，真空期望值变为非零。此外，任何非零真空期望值都必然非平凡地依赖于环面坐标。在 M=1 时存在单一真空构型，M=2 时存在两个简并真空构型，M=3 时存在六个简并真空构型。

Conclusion: 确定了不同磁通量子数下真空构型的简并度，并分析了这些构型的对称性保持（preserve）或自发破缺（spontaneously break）行为。

Abstract: We investigate the vacuum expectation value of a complex scalar field on a two-dimensional torus with quantized magnetic flux $M$. A characteristic feature of this system is the emergence of a critical area: when the area of the torus exceeds this critical value, the vacuum expectation value becomes nonvanishing. Furthermore, any nonzero vacuum expectation value necessarily exhibits nontrivial dependence on the coordinates of the torus. Employing the lowest-mode approximation, we find a single vacuum configuration for $M=1$, whereas two and six degenerate vacuum configurations arise for $M=2$ and $M=3$, respectively. We then analyze the symmetry properties of these vacuum configurations and determine whether they preserve or spontaneously break the symmetry of the underlying system.

### [35] [Multiple Mellin-Barnes integrals in Schwinger-DeWitt technique](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22299)

TL;DR: 本文研究弯曲时空背景下拉普拉斯型算子（Laplace-type operators）积分核的非对角渐近级数（off-diagonal asymptotic series），通过积分变换将热核（heat kernel）的DeWitt级数转化为DeWitt型级数，其系数（称为基核，basis kernels）为包含Synge世界函数（Synge world function）的超几何型函数。文章研究了对应Mellin-Barnes积分的非共振（non-resonant）与共振（resonant）情形的级数表示，并基于算子函数的紫外（UV）与红外（IR）性质给出了物理诠释。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对拉普拉斯型算子的热核DeWitt级数施加积分变换，得到一类DeWitt型非对角渐近展开；在此基础上，对先前工作中出现的N重Mellin-Barnes积分进行级数展开分析，分别处理非共振情形与共振情形。

Result: 得到了Mellin-Barnes积分在非共振与共振两种情形下的级数表示形式；指出该级数与算子函数的紫外（UV）和红外（IR）行为存在内在关联，从而赋予展开式以明确的物理意义。

Conclusion: 本文建立了弯曲背景下算子函数非对角渐近级数的一般框架，将数学上不同类型的级数（共振与非共振）统一纳入物理诠释，为分析量子场论中的有效作用量（effective action）和短距/长距行为提供了新工具。

Abstract: We consider off-diagonal asymptotic series for integral kernels of functions of Laplace-type operators on curved backgrounds. These expansions are obtained by applying integral transforms to the DeWitt series for the heat kernel of the corresponding operator and thus represent a DeWitt-type series in the heat kernel coefficients with the coefficients of this expansion (which we call basis kernels) being some hypergeometric-type functions of the Synge world function. Basis kernels of a certain class of operator functions were found previously in terms of $N$-fold Mellin-Barnes integrals. In this paper we study series representations of the corresponding Mellin-Barnes integrals in both non-resonant and resonant cases and suggest a physical interpretation for the emerging series, which is related to the UV and IR properties of operator functions.

### [36] [Five benefits of grand unified $SU(5)$ brane world scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22311)
*Masato Arai,Filip Blaschke,Minoru Eto,Masaki Kawaguchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在五维时空的畴壁（domain wall）上构造了一个 $SU(5)$ 大统一理论（Grand Unified Theory, GUT），通过一个伴随标量场（adjoint scalar field）和一个单态场（singlet）同时实现畴壁解、手征费米子零模局域化、规范对称性自发破缺、规范场束缚以及希格斯场的局域化，并提供了一种解决双重态-三重态分裂问题（doublet-triplet splitting problem）的新方案。通过重整化群（renormalization group）分析，证明可从五维汤川耦合（Yukawa coupling）再现弱标度下的标准模型汤川耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统大统一理论在四维时空框架下面临若干难题，包括如何解释规范对称性破缺的动力学机制、如何自然地解决双重态-三重态分裂问题，以及如何将不同性质的场（费米子、规范场、希格斯场）有效局域化在同一个膜世界（brane-world）上。本文旨在利用五维时空中的畴壁解，构建一个尽可能经济的大统一理论模型。

Method: 方法上，作者在五维时空引入一个伴随标量场和一个单态标量场，两者共同形成五个畴壁解（domain-wall solutions），构成动力学膜世界。通过Jackiw-Rebbi机制局域化手征费米子零模（chiral fermion zero modes），借助几何希格斯机制（geometric Higgs mechanism）将 $SU(5)$ 破缺至标准模型规范群，并利用场依赖的规范动能项（field-dependent gauge kinetic term）束缚规范场。希格斯场通过同一标量场构型实现局域化，从而解决双重态-三重态分裂问题。文中还提出了两种希格斯扇区的具体实现方式，并导出了四维有效理论（four-dimensional effective theory）。

Result: 该模型仅用一个伴随标量场和一个单态标量场便实现了大统一理论所需的全部核心要素，包括费米子零模局域化、规范对称性破缺、规范场束缚、希格斯场局域化及双重态-三重态分裂问题的解决。通过重整化群分析，在合适的参数选择下，五维汤川耦合能够再现弱能标处的标准模型汤川耦合。

Conclusion: 本文提出的五维畴壁上的 $SU(5)$ 大统一理论模型在结构上非常经济，为膜世界框架下的大统一理论构建提供了一条新途径，并为双重态-三重态分裂问题提供了新颖的解决方案。

Abstract: We construct an $SU(5)$ Grand Unified Theory on domain walls in the five-dimensional space-time. In this setup, we introduce an adjoint scalar field and a singlet that together form a set of five domain-wall solutions, realizing a dynamical brane-world. The same scalar fields also localize chiral fermion zero modes around the walls via the Jackiw-Rebbi mechanism, break $SU(5)$ down to the Standard Model gauge group via geometric Higgs mechanism and simultaneously trap gauge fields through a field-dependent gauge kinetic term. Furthermore, they enable localization of the Higgs field, providing a novel solution to the doublet-triplet splitting problem. As a result, all essential ingredients of the model are realized by a single adjoint scalar field and a singlet, making the construction very economical. We propose two realizations of the Higgs sector, derive the four-dimensional effective theory, and demonstrate that the Standard Model Yukawa couplings at the weak scale can be reproduced from the five-dimensional Yukawa couplings by the renormalization group analysis with a suitable choice of parameters.

### [37] [Graviton propagation in ghost-free massive gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22418)
*Claudia de Rham,Jan Kożuszek,Andrew J. Tolley,Toby Wiseman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明在 dRGT 有质量引力（massive gravity）中，对应 helicity-2 模式的两个自由度在任何背景下的高频极限中始终沿度量光锥（metric lightcone）传播，这对该理论当前及未来的观测检验具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: dRGT 有质量引力存在五个引力自由度，其中 helicity-1 和 helicity-0 模的特征（characteristics）在一般背景下不同于度量光锥，因此需要严格澄清 helicity-2 模的传播行为是否始终遵循度量光锥，以便为观测检验提供理论依据。

Method: 作者在 dRGT 有质量引力的框架下，保留两个质量项，在高频极限下对一般背景进行理论分析，严格证明 helicity-2 模式对应的两个自由度始终沿度量光锥传播。

Result: 研究证明，在任何一般背景下，helicity-2 模的两个自由度在高频极限下均沿度量光锥传播，不受背景结构的影响。

Conclusion: 该结论对于当前及未来对 dRGT 有质量引力的观测检验具有重要参考价值，因为它确保了 helicity-2 模的传播特性在不同背景下保持一致，从而简化了理论与观测结果的对照。

Abstract: We consider the ghost-free dRGT massive gravity with two of its three possible mass terms. This theory has five gravitational degrees of freedom. On Minkowski spacetime these modes have helicity-2, -1 and -0 and propagate on the Minkowski lightcone in the high-frequency limit. However for a general background the degrees of freedom corresponding to the helicity-1 and -0 modes have characteristics different to that of the metric lightcone. Here we prove in all generality, that the two degrees of freedom corresponding to the helicity-2 mode always propagate on the metric lightcone for any background in the high-frequency limit, which has significant relevance for current and future observational tests of the theory.
