### [38] [On a quantization of deformed reducible gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22466)
*A. A. Averianov,A. O. Barvinsky,I. L. Buchbinder,V. A. Krykhtin,D. V. Nesterov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过Stueckelberg型过程将可约化规范理论（reducible gauge theory）中的破缺规范对称性恢复为严格规范不变性的方法，并完成了其一般性量子化，最终将其应用于AdS空间中大规模费米子全反对称张量场模型的单圈量子有效作用量计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 处理由质量项和/或相互作用项破坏规范不变性（gauge invariance）的一般可约化规范理论，使其能够纳入协变Schwinger-DeWitt技术可处理的最小波算子（minimal wave operators）形式主义中。

Method: 利用Stueckelberg型过程（Stueckelberg-type procedure）将破缺的规范对称性恢复为精确的规范不变性；在规范变换生成元（generators of gauge transformations）具有第一和第二阶段可约化性（reducibility）的一般情形下进行量子化（quantization），通过泛函积分（functional integral）导出包含所有对应鬼场（ghost fields）的配分函数（partition function）。

Result: 成功将阿贝尔情形（Abelian case）下破缺规范对称性的理论转化为严格规范不变的理论；将该方法应用于AdS空间（$AdS$ space）中大规模费米子全反对称张量场模型（massive fermionic totally antisymmetric tensor field models），得到单圈量子有效作用量（one-loop quantum effective action）表示为不同维度下特殊狄拉克型微分算子（special Dirac-type differential operators）的泛函行列式（functional determinants）形式。

Conclusion: 所提出的Stueckelberg型恢复规范对称性方法及量子化方案在可约化规范理论框架下是有效的，并成功推广至弯曲时空（AdS空间）中的大规模张量场模型，为这类模型的量子效应计算提供了系统化路径。

Abstract: We consider a general reducible gauge theory deformed by mass or/and interaction terms violating gauge invariance. It is shown that in the Abelian case, by using the Stueckelberg-type procedure, this theory with broken gauge symmetry can be converted into exactly gauge-invariant theory which under a suitable choice of gauge conditions can be treated within the formalism of minimal wave operators manageable by the covariant Schwinger-DeWitt technique. We carry out quantization of such a theory in general terms when the initial generators of gauge transformations are of the first and second stages of reducibility and derive its partition function in terms of the functional integral with all corresponding ghost fields. This method is applied to quantization of massive fermionic totally antisymmetric tensor field models in $AdS$ space. One-loop quantum effective action for these models is derived in the form of the functional determinants of special Dirac-type differential operators in various dimensions.

</details>


### [39] [Carrollian ABJM: Fermions and Supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22582)
*Arjun Bagchi,Arthur Lipstein,Saikat Mondal,Alex Jiayi Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将AdS/CFT对应中的ABJM理论取平直空间极限（$c \to 0$），构建了一类Carrollian超共形场论，并证明了该理论可用Carrollian Dirac矩阵重新表述，具有无限维Carrollian超共形对称性，其玻色子子代数为扩展BMS$_4$代数，为构造平直空间中的M理论Carrollian规范对偶提供了具体起点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平直空间全息对偶（flat space holography）的构造是重要的理论问题。一个自然的方法是从已充分理解的AdS/CFT例子（如AdS$_4$与ABJM理论的对应）出发，取其平直空间极限。然而，该极限在费米子情形下实施困难，因为Dirac代数依赖于时空度规，在Carrollian时空与闵氏时空中形式不同。

Method: 本研究从ABJM理论出发，将平直空间极限视为边界理论中光速$c$趋于零的极限，从而得到Carrollian超共形理论。针对费米子，论文系统分析了Carrollian Dirac代数的四种可能实现方式，其中一种恰好对应相对论性费米子在$c \to 0$极限下的领头阶行为。在三维情形下，论文指出Carrollian Dirac代数的最小实现需要$4\times4$矩阵而非通常的$2\times2$矩阵，并基于此将ABJM理论的极限重新表述为Carrollian形式。

Result: 结果表明，$c \to 0$极限下的ABJM理论可以用Carrollian Dirac矩阵重新表述，并具有无限维Carrollian超共形对称性。该对称性的玻色子子代数为扩展BMS$_4$代数（extended BMS$_4$ algebra），该代数正是四维闵氏时空渐近对称性的代数描述。

Conclusion: 该工作为构造平直空间中与M理论对偶的Carrollian规范场论提供了具体的出发点，从而推进了平直空间全息对偶框架的建立。

Abstract: A natural approach for constructing a concrete example of flat space holography is to take the flat space limit of a well-understood example of AdS/CFT, such as the one relating M-theory in AdS$_4$ times an orbifolded 7-sphere to a certain three dimensional superconformal Chern-Simons-matter theory known as the ABJM theory living in the boundary of AdS$_4$. In particular, taking the flat space limit of the bulk corresponds to taking the speed of light $c$ to zero in the boundary, giving rise to a Carrollian superconformal theory. This limit is subtle to implement for fermions, however, since the Dirac algebra is sensitive to the spacetime metric and therefore takes a different form in Carrollian spacetimes than it does in Minkowski space. In fact, we show that there are four possible ways of realising Carrollian fermions, one of which arises at leading order in the $c\rightarrow0$ limit of relativistic fermions. In three dimensions, there is an additional complication that the minimal realisation of the Carrollian Dirac algebra requires $4\times4$ matrices rather than $2\times 2$ matrices familiar from the relativistic case. Nevertheless, we show that the $c\rightarrow0$ limit of the ABJM theory can be recast in terms of Carrollian Dirac matrices and enjoys and infinite-dimensional Carrollian superconformal symmetry whose bosonic subsector is the extended BMS$_4$ algebra encoding the asymptotic symmetries of four dimensional Minkowski space. This provides a concrete starting point for constructing a Carrollian gauge theory dual to M-theory in flat space.

</details>


### [40] [Generalized Entanglement Wedges and the Connected Wedge Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22612)
*Athira Arayath,Sabrina Pasterski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用广义纠缠楔（generalized entanglement wedges）框架重新审视了连通楔定理（connected wedge theorem, CWT），将其重新表述为体区域纠缠熵的关系，建立了边界决策区域互信息的新上下界，并证明非空散射构型必然对应连通的纠缠楔，且该推广适用于渐近平直时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对连通楔定理（CWT）进行推广与重新表述，将其从边界区域的纠缠楔语言转化为体区域（bulk regions）的纠缠熵（entanglement entropies）语言，以揭示散射构型（scattering configuration）与纠缠楔连通性之间的更深层关系。

Method: 采用广义纠缠楔（generalized entanglement wedges）框架，将CWT重新表述为体区域纠缠熵之间的关系；通过定义与散射构型相关联的体决策区域（bulk decision regions），建立边界决策区域互信息（mutual information）的上下界。

Result: 得到了边界决策区域互信息在体区域熵下的新上下界；证明了非空散射构型必然意味着连通的纠缠楔（connected entanglement wedge）。

Conclusion: 该工作将连通楔定理推广到了渐近平直时空（asymptotically flat spacetimes），表明CWT不仅限于AdS/CFT对偶框架，具有更广泛的适用范围。

Abstract: We use the framework of generalized entanglement wedges to revisit the connected wedge theorem (CWT). This construction identifies an entanglement wedge associated for any bulk region and allows us to rephrase the CWT in terms of the entanglement entropies of bulk regions. We establish new upper and lower bounds on the mutual information of boundary decision regions in terms of the entropies of certain bulk regions associated with a scattering configuration. We then define new bulk decision regions for which we show that a non-empty scattering configuration implies a connected entanglement wedge. This generalization of the CWT extends to asymptotically flat spacetimes.

### [41] [Generalised Symmetries and Swampland-Type Constraints from Charge Quantisation via Rational Homotopy Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22656)
*Luigi Alfonsi,Hyungrok Kim,William G. A. Luciani*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对电荷量子化（charge quantisation）的同伦类型（homotopy type）$\mathcal A$ 假设进行了精炼，将之与物质流及高规范理论（higher gauge theory）相联系，并论证了$\mathcal A$的同伦群（homotopy groups）分类膜电荷（brane charges）、同调群（homology groups）分类可逆高形式对称性（invertible higher-form symmetries），同时指出该假设施加了与沼泽地猜想（swampland conjectures）类似的约束，且量子引力理论中的$\mathcal A$必须是可缩的（contractible）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sati 与 Schreiber 此前提出量子场论和弦理论中的电荷量子化由同伦类型 $\mathcal A$ 支配，摘要旨在对这一假设进行精炼与扩展，将其与物质流及高规范理论的调整相结合，并探讨其与沼泽地猜想之间的深层联系。

Method: 通过引入对 $\mathcal A$ 的确定方法，将其与高规范理论（higher gauge theory）中的调整机制相连接，并分别利用同伦群与同调群对膜电荷和可逆高形式对称性进行分类，借此推导出对量子场论的非平凡约束。

Result: 研究发现：$\mathcal A$ 的同伦群分类可能的膜电荷，而同调群分类可逆高形式对称性；电荷量子化假设排除了非紧致规范群（noncompact gauge groups）以及构成非幂零李代数（non-nilpotent Lie algebra）的单形式场强（one-form field strengths）；此外，量子引力理论中的 $\mathcal A$ 必须是可缩的，这符合沼泽地猜想中关于全局广义对称性缺失与荷谱完备性的要求，并在 Type I 弦论中得到了具体验证。

Conclusion: 电荷量子化的同伦类型假设是一个有效的理论框架，它不仅能够统一分类膜电荷与高形式对称性，还对量子场论施加了与沼泽地猜想一致的强约束，尤其预言了量子引力中 $\mathcal A$ 的可缩性。

Abstract: Sati and Schreiber [arXiv:2402.18473, arXiv:2512.12431] have proposed that charge quantisation in quantum field theory and string theory is governed by a homotopy type $\mathcal A$. We provide a refinement of this postulate, incorporating other currents including matter, connecting it to adjustments in higher gauge theory and providing a prescription for determining $\mathcal A$, and show that, while the homotopy groups of $\mathcal A$ classify the possible brane charges, the homology groups of $\mathcal A$ classify the invertible higher-form symmetries. Furthermore, we show that the charge-quantisation postulate implies a number of non-trivial constraints on quantum field theories similar to those implied by swampland conjectures; in particular, it rules out noncompact gauge groups and one-form field strengths that form a non-nilpotent Lie algebra. Finally, we argue that for theories of quantum gravity the space $\mathcal A$ must be contractible, in accordance with the swampland conjectures on the absence of global generalised symmetries and the completeness of the spectrum of charges, and explain how this explicitly arises in the case of Type I string theory.

### [42] [Landau Analysis of One-Cycle Negative Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22683)

Method: 采用几何Landau分析（geometric Landau analysis），通过递归方式分析相关的朗道图（Landau diagrams），推导奇点结构。

Result: 证明该量在所有圈数下（to all loop orders）的奇点仅出现在$z=-1,0$和$\infty$三个位置。

Conclusion: 该结果是在循环展开（expansion over cycles）的次领头阶（next-to-leading order）实现该量非微扰重求和的第一步。

Abstract: We use geometric Landau analysis to determine the singularity structure of four-point, one-cycle negative geometries in $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory, which represent certain contributions to the logarithm of the four-point amplitude or equivalently the normalized quadrangular Wilson loop with a Lagrangian insertion. By analyzing the relevant Landau diagrams recursively, we prove that this quantity has singularities only at $z=-1,0$ and $\infty$ to all loop orders. This represents a first step towards obtaining a non-perturbative resummation for this quantity at next-to-leading order in the expansion over cycles.

### [43] [Carrollian quantum states and flat space holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22745)
*Stefan Fredenhagen,Stefan Prohazka,Robert Tiefenbacher*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从代数视角研究自由Carrollian量子场论，构造了电型和磁型Carrollian Weyl代数，分析了真空态和热态等量子态的性质，并探讨了这些结果对平面对偶（flat space holography）中红外自由度的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Carrollian量子场论的代数结构与态空间性质，特别是不同量子化方案下真空态和热态的存在性与正则性，进而揭示这些结果对平面对偶理论的边界理论中红外自由度的含义。

Method: 通过取相对论性标量场的Carroll极限（Carroll limit），构造电型和磁型Carrollian Weyl代数；随后分析这些代数下的真空态（vacuum state）、KMS态（KMS state）以及空间均匀的准自由纯态（spatially homogeneous quasifree pure state）和Sorkin-Johnston态等不同类别的量子态。

Result: 有质量电型理论存在正则的Carroll不变真空态和正则的KMS态，构成自洽的Carrollian热力学系统；无质量电型和磁型理论则更加微妙，取决于量子化方案，可能不存在正则的优选的真空态，或仅存在非正则的Carroll不变基态，但仍支持非正则的热态。此外，构造了一个适用于Carrollian全息（Carrollian holography）的良定义的准自由态，其Hilbert空间表示分解为标准Fock扇区（standard Fock sector）和不可分的零模扇区（nonseparable zero-mode sector）。

Conclusion: Carrollian量子场论在不同质量与量子化方案下展现出丰富的态空间结构，其中零模扇区的不可分性凸显了边界理论中红外自由度（infrared degrees of freedom）在平面对偶中的关键作用。

Abstract: We study free Carrollian quantum field theories from an algebraic perspective and explore their implications for flat space holography. As explicit examples, we construct the electric and magnetic Carrollian Weyl algebras obtained from Carroll limits of the relativistic scalar field and analyze their states, including vacuum and thermal configurations. For the massive electric theory, we find a regular Carroll-invariant vacuum state and a regular KMS state, yielding a consistent Carrollian thermodynamic system. By contrast, the massless electric and magnetic theories are more subtle: depending on the quantization, they admit either no regular distinguished vacuum or only nonregular Carroll-invariant ground states, while still supporting nonregular thermal states. We further analyze alternative classes of states in the massless electric theory, including spatially homogeneous quasifree pure states and Sorkin--Johnston states.Motivated by these results, we discuss consequences for flat space holography. We construct a well-defined quasifree state relevant for Carrollian holography whose Hilbert-space representation factorizes into a standard Fock sector and a nonseparable zero-mode sector, thereby highlighting the role of infrared degrees of freedom in the boundary theory.

Method: 将关联测量（correlation measurement）和局域磁化率测量（local susceptibility measurement）的实验数据，与动态自旋关联（dynamic spin correlations）的理论高温展开方法（high-temperature expansion method）相结合，构建测温方案。

Abstract: We propose an accurate thermometry approach for Rydberg atom tweezer arrays combining data from correlation and local susceptibility measurements with a theoretical high-temperature expansion method for dynamic spin correlations. We apply our approach to a recent quantum simulation experiment [Bornet et al., arXiv 2602.14323] realizing an anti-ferromagnetic dipolar spin-1/2 XY model on the Kagome lattice. We obtain T=0.55J and S/N=0.67 ln2 for temperature and entropy respectively, showing that further experimental efforts are required to reach the putative quantum spin liquid regime.

### [45] [Downward ultra-high-energy neutrino detection in the air with radio antennas at ground-based observatories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22083)
*Baobiao Yue,Karl-Heinz Kampert,Julian Rautenberg*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用地面无线电天线阵列识别超高能中微子（UHE neutrinos）的方法，基于辐射最大值（\(X^{\text{radio}}_{\text{max}}\)）的重构算法可以区分中微子引发的深层大气簇射与背景宇宙射线。模拟结果表明，该技术在1 EeV以上能显著增强对陡峭倾斜簇射的灵敏度，并具有良好的可扩展性，适用于GRAND等未来射电天文台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超高能中微子（UHE neutrinos）是穿越宇宙距离几乎不被衰减的独特宇宙信使，能够直接揭示宇宙中最剧烈的能量过程。传统的粒子探测器在探测超高能中微子方面存在局限，而无线电探测（radio detection）因其大气对无线电信号衰减极小、重构精度高且暴露范围大，具有显著优势。本研究旨在利用地面无线电天线阵列开发一种识别超高能中微子的有效方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于辐射最大值（\(X^{\text{radio}}_{\text{max}}\)）的重构算法，用于区分深层发展的中微子诱导簇射（neutrino-induced showers）与背景宇宙射线。通过对电子中微子带电电流相互作用（\(ν_e\)-CC）诱导的大气簇射进行模拟，评估了触发效率（trigger efficiency）、重构性能（reconstruction performance）以及参考阵列的有效面积和孔径（effective area and aperture prediction）。

Result: 模拟结果显示，无线电探测方法在1 EeV以上能显著提升对陡峭倾斜簇射（highly inclined showers）的探测灵敏度，可有效补充传统表面探测器（surface detectors）的不足。该技术具有高度可扩展性（highly scalable），可用于GRAND等未来射电天文台。

Conclusion: 所提出的重构与识别策略为实现探测超高能中微子所需的灵敏度提供了一条可行路径，证实了无线电探测技术在未来中微子天体物理学中的潜力。

Abstract: Ultra-high-energy (UHE) neutrinos are unique cosmic messengers that can traverse cosmological distances unattenuated, providing direct insight into the most energetic processes in the universe. Radio detection offers significant advantages for detecting highly inclined air showers induced by UHE neutrinos. This is due to a larger exposure range compared to particle detectors, which is a result of minimal atmospheric attenuation of radio signals combined with good reconstruction precision. Furthermore, this technique improves the air shower longitudinal reconstruction, which can be used to identify neutrinos with their first interaction far below the top of the atmosphere. In this work, we present a method for identifying UHE neutrinos using ground-based radio antennas. A reconstruction algorithm is introduced based on the radio emission maximum ($X^{\text{radio}}_{\text{max}}$), which demonstrates its power in distinguishing deeply developing neutrino-induced showers from background cosmic rays. Using simulations of $ν_e$-CC-induced air showers, we evaluate the trigger efficiency, reconstruction performance, and resulting effective area and aperture prediction for a reference array. Our results show that radio detection significantly enhances the sensitivity to very inclined showers above 1 EeV, complementing traditional surface detectors. This technique is highly scalable and applicable to future radio observatories, such as GRAND. The proposed reconstruction and identification strategy provides a pathway toward achieving the sensitivity required to detect UHE neutrinos.

### [46] [Testing solitonic boson star interpretations of Sagittarius A* with near-infrared flare astrometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21883)
*Xiangyu Wang,Zhenyu Zhang,Hai-Qing Zhang,Minyong Guo,Bin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用GRAVITY近红外（NIR）耀斑天体测量数据，通过对比五种不同有效半径的孤子玻色子星（solitonic boson star）模型与施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）对Sagittarius A*的拟合效果，发现玻色子星模型推断的质量均高于已确立的4.3×10^6 M⊙，从而对Sagittarius A*作为孤子玻色子星的解释施加了严格约束，但并未完全排除这一可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Sagittarius A*是否可能是一个孤子玻色子星（solitonic boson star），而非传统的施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole），从而为银河系中心致密天体的本质提供新的理论视角。

Method: 采用五种不同有效半径的球对称孤子玻色子星模型，以施瓦西黑洞为对照，将耀斑（flares）视为在圆形赤道轨道上运动的热点（hot spots），分析其质心运动（centroid motions）与成像特征，并分别使用χ²分析与马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法进行参数拟合。

Result: 两种拟合方法结果一致：玻色子星模型推断出的质量均系统性地高于已确立的4.3×10^6 M⊙；扩散性更强的玻色子星成像特性更接近黑洞，其质量估计也相应更接近已确立值。

Conclusion: 研究结果对Sagittarius A*作为孤子玻色子星（solitonic boson star）的解释施加了严格约束（stringent constraints），但并未完全排除这一可能性。

Abstract: We use GRAVITY near-infrared (NIR) flare astrometry to test whether Sagittarius A* could be a solitonic boson star. We consider five spherically symmetric solitonic boson-star models with different effective radii, together with the Schwarzschild black hole. Treating the flares as hot spots on circular equatorial orbits, we analyze their centroid motions and images in these spacetimes and use them for parameter fitting. We perform the fitting using both $χ^2$ analysis and Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods, which yield consistent results: the inferred masses of boson-star models are systematically larger than the established value of $4.3\times10^6M_\odot$. Notably, more diffusive boson stars exhibit imaging properties closer to those of a black hole, leading to mass estimates that are correspondingly closer to the established value. Overall, our results place stringent constraints on solitonic boson star interpretations of Sagittarius A*, although do not completely rule them out.

</details>


### [47] [Signature of iron line profile from a Kerr-like wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22268)
*Cheng Liu,Hoongwah Siew,Hong-Xuan Jiang,Yosuke Mizuno,Tao Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文为区分克尔类虫洞（Kerr-like wormholes）与克尔黑洞（Kerr black holes）的X射线铁线（Fe Kα）光谱特征提供了相对论性反射（relativistic reflection）建模框架，并基于模拟的NuSTAR光谱展示了大型喉径虫洞在高品质光谱中可通过全自洽的反射模型加以检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 吸积黑洞的X射线光谱中观测到的宽且不对称的铁Kα发射线（broad, skewed Fe Kα emission lines）是探测内盘时空几何的关键探针。然而，可穿越的类克尔虫洞（traversable Kerr-like wormholes）等无视界替代天体可以模拟克尔度规（Kerr metric）的许多信号特征，对现有数据解读构成挑战。因此，有必要建立一个区分虫洞喉径（wormhole throat）与事件视界（event horizon）的光谱判别框架。

Method: 作者发展了一个包含克尔类虫洞几何的相对论性反射框架，利用自定义射线追踪子程序（ray-tracing subroutine），在XSPEC中实现两个模块：kwline（δ-函数线型）和kwconv（全反射谱），参数包括自旋（spin）、喉径半径（throat radius）和形状函数系数（shape-function coefficients）。通过计算密集网格的线型并生成具有真实响应矩阵的合成NuSTAR光谱，再使用标准克尔模型（canonical Kerr models）对模拟数据进行拟合，量化虫洞几何造成的光谱偏差。

Result: 随着喉径参数λ（throat parameter λ）增大，克尔类虫洞产生的Fe Kα线更窄，红翼（red wings）受到抑制。在50 ks的NuSTAR模拟中（λ=0.9, a_*=0.998），简单卷积模型（kerrconv）可勉强拟合虫洞光谱，但自洽模型（如relxillCp）统计失败，产生结构化残差（structured residuals）和非物理解释参数锁定（如发射率q_in→10）。

Conclusion: 当使用全自洽的反射模型（fully consistent reflection models）而非后处理近似（post-processing approximations）进行分析时，大喉径虫洞在高品质X射线光谱中是可检测的。

Abstract: Broad, skewed iron K$α$ emission lines in the X-ray spectra of accreting black holes encode key information about the spacetime geometry of the innermost disk. While the Kerr metric is standard for spin measurements, horizonless alternatives like traversable "Kerr-like" wormholes can mimic many black hole signatures, challenging current data interpretations. We develop a relativistic reflection framework incorporating Kerr-like wormhole geometries to predict iron line distortions and assess the feasibility of distinguishing event horizons from wormhole throats.Using a custom ray-tracing subroutine, we implement two \textsc{XSPEC} modules: \texttt{kwline} for $δ$-function profiles and \texttt{kwconv} for full reflection spectra, parameterized by spin, throat radius, and shape-function coefficients. We compute a dense grid of line profiles and generate synthetic \textit{NuSTAR} spectra with realistic response matrices. By fitting these simulations with canonical Kerr models, we quantify deviations attributable to wormhole geometries.We find that Kerr-like wormholes produce narrower Fe K$α$ lines with suppressed red wings as the throat parameter $λ$ increases. In 50 ks \textit{NuSTAR} simulations ($λ=0.9, a_*=0.998$), simple convolutional models (\texttt{kerrconv}) can mimic the wormhole spectrum. However, self-consistent models like \texttt{relxillCp} result in statistical failure, yielding structured residuals and unphysical parameter pegging (e.g., emissivity $q_{\rm in} \to 10$). We conclude that large-throat wormholes are detectable in high-quality X-ray spectra if analyzed with fully consistent reflection models rather than post-processing approximations.

### [48] [How lonely are the Binary Compact Objects Detected by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22441)
*Devesh Giri,Suvodip Mukherjee*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文基于引力波观测数据，针对双致密星并合（CBC）过程中可能发生的三体相遇扰动，构建了包含牛顿三体动力学和领头阶辐射反作用（2.5PN）的物理模型，并在LVK GWTC-4目录的三个高信噪比事件中未发现统计显著偏差，从而首次给出了这些引力波事件附近中等质量黑洞（>10² M☉）的上限约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的引力波（gravitational wave, GW）观测解释均假设双星系统（compact binary coalescence, CBC）在孤立环境中演化，但真实天体物理环境中存在短暂的三体相遇（three-body encounter）可能扰动双星轨道并影响辐射的引力波信号，现有研究缺乏对这一效应的物理建模。

Method: 建立基于牛顿三体动力学并补充领头阶（2.5阶后牛顿，2.5PN）辐射反作用（radiation-reaction）的物理模型，从LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）GWTC-4目录中选取GW170817、GW190814和GW230627_015337三个高信噪比（high SNR）、带内持续时间≥10秒的事件进行搜索分析。

Result: 数据中未发现统计显著的偏差，转化为对这三个双星附近约10⁻¹ AU范围内、质量高于~10² M☉的中等质量黑洞（intermediate-mass black hole, IMBH）的约束；基于飞越相互作用（fly-by interaction）会动力学破坏双星这一直接排除机制，首次给出了这些引力波事件附近中等质量黑洞的上限。

Conclusion: 该方法可直接排除特定中等质量黑洞的存在，且不依赖于波形建模（waveform modelling）；未来借助长持续时间引力波信号，可探测更远距离（>1 AU）处与更轻致密天体的相遇，为探测致密环境（如星系中心和稠密球状星团）中的天体物理或原初（primordial）致密天体打开新窗口。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave (GW) observations of compact binary coalescences (CBCs) are traditionally interpreted under the assumption that the binary evolves in isolation. However, in realistic astrophysical environments, brief three-body encounters may perturb the binary's orbital evolution and imprint deviations on the emitted GWs. We develop a physically motivated model for such interactions, retaining Newtonian three-body dynamics supplemented by leading-order ($2.5$PN) radiation-reaction within the binary. We show that such encounters produce a distinctive morphology of dephasing and amplitude modulation in GWs. We search for this kind of distortion from the LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA (LVK) GW catalog GWTC-4 on three events: GW170817, GW190814, and GW230627\_015337, chosen based on high SNR and in-band duration $\gtrsim 10~\mathrm{s}$. We find no statistically significant deviation in the data, which translates into constraints on the absence of any intermediate-mass black hole in the mass range above $\sim 10^2$ M$_\odot$ in the vicinity of these binaries of radius approximately $10^{-1}~\mathrm{AU}$. This arises from robust exclusions arising from fly-by interactions that would dynamically disrupt the binary and are directly ruled out independent of waveform modelling, placing the first upper bound on intermediate-mass black holes near these GW events. In future, with the availability of long-duration GW signals, this new avenue can probe encounters of the binary GW sources with compact objects of lighter masses at distances farther away than 1 AU and hence opens a new window to probe the population of individual compact objects of both astrophysical and primordial origin in astrophysical systems of dense environments ranging from galactic centers to dense globular clusters.

### [49] [Caustic Skeleton and the Local Cosmic Web: the Coma Cluster node and the Pisces-Perseus ridge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22213)
*Amelie Read,Job Feldbrugge,Celine Boehm,Rien van de Weygaert,Benjamin Hertzsch*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文应用尖点骨架理论（caustic skeleton theory）于Manticore-Local模拟（对本地宇宙的贝叶斯约束重建），提取了后发座星系团（Coma Cluster）和双鱼-英仙座脊（Pisces-Perseus ridge）这两个典型网状结构的三维多尺度尖点骨架。研究发现该理论能准确再现红移空间中星系的观测大尺度组织，并预测两种拓扑上不同的纤维状结构类型（A₄ swallowtail与D₄ umbilic尖点），其中D₄型纤维在小尺度上愈发重要，双鱼-英仙超星系团尤为D₄主导，从而为邻近宇宙中最受研究的纤维复合体提供了新的拓扑刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有结构识别方法难以区分形态相似但拓扑起源不同的纤维状结构，亟需一种能够揭示大尺度环境中尖点（caustic）奇异点层级结构并建立多尺度分类的理论工具。

Method: 将尖点骨架理论应用于Manticore-Local模拟（基于2M++星系目录的贝叶斯约束重建），从两个典型网状结构（后发座星系团与双鱼-英仙座脊）中提取三维多尺度尖点骨架网络。

Result: 尖点骨架网络准确再现了红移空间中星系的观测大尺度组织；该理论预测了两种拓扑不同的纤维类别——A₄ swallowtail尖点与D₄ umbilic尖点，它们在形态上相似但折叠历史根本不同；D₄型纤维在小尺度上影响增大，双鱼-英仙超星系团呈明显D₄主导，而后发座星系团周围的Stickman结构则相反。

Conclusion: 尖点骨架理论为邻近宇宙中广泛研究的纤维复合体提供了一种新颖的拓扑表征（topological characterisation），揭示了常规结构识别器容易忽略的拓扑分异。

Abstract: We apply caustic skeleton theory to the Manticore-Local simulations, which are Bayesian constrained reconstructions of the Local Universe from the 2M++ galaxy catalogue, and extract the three-dimensional multi-scale caustic skeleton of two canonical weblike structures in our Local Universe, namely the Coma Cluster and the Pisces-Perseus ridge as they represent the most prominent cluster node and filamentary artery in the nearby Universe. We show that the Caustic Skeleton network of caustic singularities accurately reproduces the observed large-scale organisation of galaxies in redshift space for one of the Manticore realisations. The hierarchy of caustic features allows us to establish a multi-scale classification of the large-scale environment in which observed 2M++ galaxies reside. One of the most interesting aspects of the theory is that it predicts two topologically distinct classes of filaments (A_4 swallowtail and D_4 umbilic caustics) that form through fundamentally different folding histories yet appear morphologically similar enough, on the surface, to be overlooked by conventional structure identifiers. We find that the influence of D_4 filaments only becomes increasingly relevant towards smaller scales, and the Pisces-Perseus Supercluster in particular is revealed to be a distinctly D_4-dominated structure compared to the extended Stickman structure around the Coma Cluster. In other words, caustic skeleton theory enables a novel topological characterisation of one of the most studied filamentary complexes in the nearby Universe. [Shortened]

### [50] [Precision Analysis for $\boldsymbol{H_0}$ Using Upcoming Multi-band Gravitational Wave Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22731)
*Setabuddin,Md Riajul Haque,Ratna Koley,Supratik Pal*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文研究了利用原初黑洞（PBHs）作为引力波（GW）源，通过多波段引力波观测来约束哈勃参数（$H_0$）不确定性的可行性。结合标量诱导和并合诱导两类引力波信号，对将来平方公里阵列（SKA）和爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）的联合观测进行统计预测，发现当PBH参数测量精度达到1%时，可将$H_0$的不确定性控制在约0.1 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹量级，表明多波段引力波观测是一种独立于宇宙距离阶梯的互补性方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈勃参数（$H_0$）的测量在宇宙学中仍存在显著争议，传统方法依赖于宇宙距离阶梯（cosmic distance ladder），迫切需要独立、互补的新观测约束途径。

Method: 论文提出一个统一的框架，将原初黑洞（PBHs）产生的两类引力波——标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced GWs）与并合诱导引力波（merger-induced GWs）相结合；利用平方公里阵列（SKA）和爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）两个未来探测器进行多波段分析；通过信噪比（SNR）估计和Fisher矩阵分析（Fisher matrix analysis）对PBH参数（$M_{\rm PBH}$和$f_{\rm PBH}$）进行统计预测。

Result: 在信噪比SNR ≥ 1条件下识别出可探测的PBH参数空间；保守估计下，当参数相对不确定度$δθ_i/θ_i \leq 0.1$时，$H_0$的不确定性$δH_0 \lesssim 2~{\rm km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$；乐观精密测量下，当$δθ_i/θ_i \leq 0.01$时，$δH_0 \lesssim \mathcal{O}(0.1)~{\rm km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$。结果对$H_0$的初始取值不敏感，仅对PBH坍缩效率（collapse efficiency）有中等依赖。

Conclusion: 多波段引力波观测能够为约束$H_0$的不确定性提供一种独立且互补的方法，有潜力成为不依赖宇宙距离阶梯的哈勃参数新测量手段。

Abstract: We investigate how multi-band gravitational wave (GW) observations can constrain the uncertainties in the Hubble parameter ($H_0$) using primordial black holes (PBHs) as possible sources. Our framework combines scalar-induced and merger-induced GWs from PBHs, and forecasts on a combination of two future detectors Square Kilometre Array (SKA) and the Einstein Telescope (ET), enabling a multi-band analysis. We perform a statistical forecast of the PBH parameters, $M_{\rm PBH}$ and $f_{\rm PBH}$, using signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) estimates and Fisher matrix analysis. Imposing $\mathrm{SNR} \geq 1$, we identify the accessible PBH parameter space and propagate these uncertainties to estimate the corresponding uncertainties in $H_0$. For $δθ_i/θ_i \leq 0.1$, with $θ_i \equiv M_{\rm PBH}(f_{\rm PBH})$, we find $δH_0 \lesssim 2~{\rm km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$ in a conservative approach, improving to $δH_0 \lesssim \mathcal{O}(0.1)~{\rm km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$ for $δθ_i/θ_i \leq 0.01$ for an optimistic approach of precision measurement. The results are further found to be largely insensitive to the fiducial choice of the $H_0$, with only moderate dependence on the PBH collapse efficiency. These findings demonstrate that multi-band GW observations provide an independent and complementary approach to constraining the uncertainties in $H_0$, with the potential to provide a novel, cosmic distance ladder-independent measure of the Hubble parameter.

### [51] [Simple sign epistasis and evolutionary detours in fitness landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22611)
*Paolo Ribeca,Alejandro Castro,Alejandro Lage-Castellanos,Alisa Sergeeva,Sebastian Matuszewski,Ruben Gustavo Paccosi,Vitaly Belik,Mahan Ghafari,Joachim Krug,Guillaume Achaz,Luca Ferretti*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文证明了简单符号上位性（simple sign epistasis）与进化绕行（evolutionary detours）——即包含回复突变（back-mutations）的更长、适应度递增的路径——之间的关联，并指出在弱上位性（weakly epistatic）景观中，简单符号上位性比互惠符号上位性（reciprocal sign epistasis）更常见，表明绕行是弱上位性景观中进化轨迹的一般特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然互惠符号上位性已被广泛研究与适应度景观（fitness landscapes）的多峰性和崎岖性（ruggedness）相关联，但简单符号上位性在适应度景观中的作用及其相对频率尚未被系统性地探究。

Method: 通过理论证明建立简单符号上位性与进化绕行之间的形式化联系，并基于实验解析的弱上位性景观数据统计两种符号上位性的发生频率，同时推导了多数景观模型的理论预测进行比较。

Result: 简单符号上位性在实验解析的弱上位性景观中远多于互惠符号上位性；这一结果与除区块模型（block model）和由配对等位基因不相容性（pairwise allelic incompatibilities）主导的景观（如RNA稳定性景观）之外的大多数景观模型的理论预测一致。

Conclusion: 在弱上位性适应度景观中，绕行是进化轨迹的普遍特征，而简单符号上位性是驱动这一现象的关键因素。

Abstract: In epistatic fitness landscapes, the fitness effect of a mutation depends on the genetic background and may even switch between deleterious and beneficial depending on the presence of another mutation. Epistatic interactions may cause both mutations to change the sign of each other's fitness effects (reciprocal sign epistasis) or only one mutation to do so (simple sign epistasis). Both these forms of epistasis influence evolutionary trajectories. While reciprocal sign epistasis has been associated with multi-peaked landscapes and their ruggedness, the role and relative frequency of simple sign epistasis in fitness landscapes have not been systematically investigated. Here, we prove that the presence of simple sign epistasis is associated with evolutionary detours, i.e., indirect, longer fitness-increasing paths to fitness peaks that include back-mutations. We also show that in experimentally resolved, weakly epistatic landscapes, simple sign epistasis occurs much more frequently than reciprocal sign epistasis. This result is consistent with the theoretical predictions we derive for most landscape models, with the exception of the block model and of landscapes dominated by pairwise allelic incompatibilities, such as RNA stability landscapes. Our results suggest that detours represent a general feature of evolutionary trajectories in weakly epistatic landscapes.

### [52] [A high order accurate and energy stable continuous Galerkin framework on summation-by-parts form for the incompressible Navier-Stokes equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22253)
*Mrityunjoy Mandal,Arnaud G Malan,Prince Nchupang,Jan Nordström*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于求和-分部（SBP）形式的连续迦辽金有限元法（CGFEM），结合同时逼近项（SAT）技术，用于高阶精确求解不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯（INS）方程。该SBP-SAT配方保证能量稳定，数值测试（包括四阶收敛验证、顶盖驱动腔流和后向台阶流）展示了其精确性与振荡自由解的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯方程（incompressible Navier-Stokes equations）的高阶精确、能量稳定的数值离散方法，特别是处理间断边界条件时无需特殊处理。

Method: 采用求和-分部（Summation-By-Parts, SBP）形式的连续迦辽金有限元法（CGFEM）离散INS方程，使用最高四阶拉格朗日多项式（Lagrange polynomials），并通过同时逼近项（Simultaneous Approximation Term, SAT）技术弱施加边界条件，形成能量稳定的SBP-SAT离散格式。

Result: 制造解方法（Method of Manufactured Solutions, MMS）验证了四阶收敛性；顶盖驱动腔流（lid-driven cavity flow）在宽雷诺数范围内实现了间断角边界附近的精确、无振荡解；后向台阶流（backward-facing step flow）问题验证了方法的准确性和效率。

Conclusion: 所提出的CGFEM-SBP-SAT框架能够以高阶精度稳定求解不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯方程的初边值问题，特别适用于包含间断边界条件的复杂流动场景。

Abstract: This paper presents a high-order accurate Continuous Galerkin Finite Element Method (CGFEM) for solving the initial boundary value problems governed by the Incompressible Navier-Stokes (INS) equations. We discretize the INS equations using the CGFEM approach in Summation-By-Parts (SBP) form. Lagrange polynomials of up to 4th order are employed. The boundary conditions are imposed weakly using the Simultaneous Approximation Term (SAT) technique, which accommodates discontinuous boundary data without special treatment. The resulting SBP-SAT formulation guarantees an energy stable discretization. The efficiency of the proposed framework is demonstrated by solving a series of numerical tests. Initially, the Method of Manufactured Solutions (MMS) is employed to demonstrate 4th order convergence. Subsequently, the 4th order accurate scheme is applied to a classical benchmark problem featuring discontinuous boundary conditions: the lid-driven cavity flow over a wide range of Reynolds numbers. Accurate and oscillation-free solutions are achieved even in the vicinity of the discontinuous top corner boundaries. Lastly, a canonical backward-facing step flow problem is solved, where accuracy and efficiency are demonstrated.

</details>

### [53] [Sign-balance of random Laplace eigenfunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22567)
*Stephen Muirhead,Igor Wigman*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种强符号平衡（sign-balance）概念，证明随机拉普拉斯本征函数（Laplace eigenfunctions）在精确确定的尺度以上以几乎全概率是符号平衡的，并证明了该尺度在能量对数幂次意义下最优。结果涵盖了随机球谐函数（random spherical harmonics）及光滑黎曼流形上的带限随机波（band-limited random waves），并推广到任意水平，确定了随机本征函数关于非零水平达到体积平衡（volume-balanced）的最优尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究源于拉普拉斯本征函数在小尺度上符号分布的问题（the small-scale sign distribution of Laplace eigenfunctions），旨在建立本征函数符号平衡的严格定量理论，并为确定性本征函数的符号平衡最优尺度猜想提供模型支撑。

Method: 引入了一种强符号平衡（sign-balance）的新定义，将其推广至任意非零水平以定义体积平衡（volume-balanced）。采用概率方法分析随机本征函数（包括随机球谐函数和一般黎曼流形上的带限随机波），研究其在不同尺度上的平衡性质。

Result: 证明了随机本征函数在精确确定的尺度以上以几乎全概率是符号平衡的；该尺度在能量对数幂次（a logarithmic power of the energy）意义下是最优的。对于非零水平，同样确定了随机本征函数达到体积平衡的最优尺度。

Conclusion: 本文的结果不仅具有内在理论价值，还为确定性拉普拉斯本征函数在何种最优尺度下实现符号平衡提供了一个自然猜想（natural conjecture）的模型。

Abstract: Motivated by the problem of the small-scale sign distribution of Laplace eigenfunctions, we introduce a strong notion of sign-balance for (eigen)functions, and prove that random eigenfunctions are sign-balanced above a precisely determined scale with almost full probability. The scale is proven to be optimal up to a logarithmic power of the energy. Our results include the important case of random spherical harmonics, as well as more general band-limited random waves on smooth Riemannian manifolds. Extending the notion of balance to arbitrary levels, we determine the precise optimum scale above which random eigenfunctions are volume-balanced with respect to non-zero levels. Beyond their intrinsic interest, our results serve as a model for a natural conjecture on the optimal scale at which deterministic Laplace eigenfunctions are sign-balanced.

</details>

### [54] [Non-volatile superconducting tunnelling magnetoresistance memory enabled by exchange-field gap engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22214)
*Sonam Bhakat,Pushpak Banerjee,Ahmedullah Aziz,Jackson Miller,Avradeep Pal*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于超导隧穿磁阻效应（superconducting tunnelling magnetoresistance）的非易失性低温存储器件，可在整个超导温度范围内工作，具备毫伏偏压、纳瓦级读取功耗和零待机功耗，并与超导逻辑电路兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导与量子计算系统需要工作于4 K以下的可扩展、低耗散存储技术，但现有低温存储方案（如CMOS衍生或混合架构）存在泄漏电流、刷新开销或与超导逻辑兼容性差等问题。

Method: 通过将de Gennes自旋阀（de Gennes spin valve）与超导隧道结（superconducting tunnel junction）集成于垂直电流平面（current perpendicular-to-plane）几何结构中，实现对超导能隙（superconducting energy gap）的交换场控制，从而产生两个可磁力切换的能隙电压及鲁棒的超导隧穿磁阻效应。

Result: 该器件在低至0.25 K的温度下仍能维持可开关的隧穿磁阻效应，工作偏压为毫伏（mV）量级，读取功耗为纳瓦（nW）量级，且具备零待机功耗。垂直结架构与铌（Nb）基材料平台使其可扩展并与超导逻辑兼容。

Conclusion: 该超导隧穿磁阻器件作为非易失性低温存储单元，在功耗、兼容性和可扩展性方面优于现有低温存储方案，有望推动超导与量子计算系统中存储技术的发展。

Abstract: Scalable, low-dissipation memory operating below 4 K is a critical requirement for superconducting and quantum computing systems. Existing cryogenic memory technologies rely on CMOS derivatives or hybrid architectures that incur leakage, refresh overhead or limited compatibility with superconducting logic. Here we demonstrate a superconducting tunnelling magnetoresistance device that functions as a non-volatile cryogenic memory element across the full superconducting temperature range. By integrating a de Gennes spin valve with a superconducting tunnel junction in a current perpendicular-to-plane geometry, we realise exchange-field control of the superconducting energy gap. This produces two magnetically switchable gap voltages and robust quasiparticle tunnelling magnetoresistance down to 0.25 K.The device operates at millivolt bias with nanowatt-level read power and zero standby dissipation. Its vertical junction architecture and Nb-based materials platform enable compatibility with superconducting logic and scalable cryogenic memory arrays.

</details>


### [55] [Theoretical prediction of strong-coupling superconductivity in a hypothetical NaAlH3 phase at ambient pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22300)
*Izabela A. Wrona,Yinwei Li,Radoslaw Szczesniak,Artur P. Durajski*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算，研究了假想立方相三元氢化物NaAlH₃（空间群Pm-3m）的晶格动力学、电子结构及电子-声子介导的超导特性，在常压下预测其超导转变温度可达73.7 K，且表现出强耦合超导特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索三元氢化物（ternary hydride）在常压下的超导潜力，系统评估假想立方Pm-3m相NaAlH₃的晶格稳定性与电子-声子耦合超导机制，为发现新型中等温度超导体提供理论依据。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与Migdal-Eliashberg形式论（Migdal-Eliashberg formalism）进行第一性原理计算；声子色散计算辅以从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）模拟验证动态与热稳定性。

Result: 电子-声子耦合常数（electron-phonon coupling constant）$λ=2.23$，库仑赝势（Coulomb pseudopotential）$μ^*=0.1$时超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）高达73.7 K；超导能隙比（superconducting gap ratio）$2Δ(0)/k_B T_c ≈ 4.8$，比热跳变（specific heat jump）$ΔC/γT_c ≈ 2.2$，均显著超出BCS弱耦合预言。

Conclusion: 假想立方Pm-3m相NaAlH₃在所采用的理论框架下具有动态和热稳定性，金属性电子结构以Al和Na贡献态为主，其超导电性呈现强耦合（strong-coupling）特征，表明该假想相是一种有潜力的中等温度超导体候选材料。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive first-principles investigation of a hypothetical cubic Pm-3m phase of the ternary hydride NaAlH3, focusing on its lattice dynamics, electronic structure, and electron-phonon-mediated superconducting properties at ambient pressure. Using density functional theory and the Migdal-Eliashberg formalism, we find an exceptionally strong electron-phonon coupling ($λ=2.23$), resulting in a superconducting critical temperature of up to 73.7 K for a Coulomb pseudopotential $μ^* = 0.1$. Phonon dispersion calculations, complemented by ab initio molecular dynamics simulations, indicate dynamic and thermal stability within the adopted theoretical framework. The electronic structure exhibits a metallic character with substantial contributions from Al- and Na-derived states at the Fermi level. The resulting superconducting gap ratio ($2Δ(0)/k_B T_c \approx 4.8$) and specific heat jump ($ΔC/γT_c \approx 2.2$) significantly exceed BCS weak-coupling predictions, highlighting the strong-coupling nature of superconductivity in this hypothetical phase.

</details>


### [56] [Resonance Frequency Shift Measurements of SRF Cavities at DESY](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22596)
*Rezvan Ghanbari,Thorsten Buettner,Wolfgang Hillert,Karol Kasprzak,Tom Krokotsch,Ricardo Monroy-Villa,Detlef Reschke,Lea Steder,Alexey Sulimov,Hans Weise,Marc Wenskat,Mateusz Wiencek,Jonas Wolff*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一套专用频移测量装置，用于分析超导射频腔（superconducting radio-frequency cavities）在超导态-正常态转变过程中的共振频率和内禀品质因数变化，以探究铌（niobium）腔中因间隙原子（interstitial atoms）引入而产生的新奇现象及其背后的超导机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导射频腔在超导-正常态转变过程中的共振频率与内禀品质因数变化，是理解腔体材料基本超导性质的重要窗口。特别是经过氧、氮等间隙原子（interstitial atoms）表面修饰的铌腔中出现了若干尚未完全理解的新奇行为，因此需要建立精准的测量手段来研究这些转变动力学。

Method: 本文开发并调试了一套专用的频移测量装置（frequency-shift measurement setup）。初始版本建立了精确的框架，可用于确定超导穿透深度（superconducting penetration depth）和正常态趋肤深度（normal-conducting skin depth）内的电子平均自由程（electron mean free path）。近期升级版本（处于最终验证阶段）显著提升了测量精度和可重复性。

Result: 该装置能够测量含间隙原子的铌腔在临界温度附近频移温度依赖关系中的一个反常凹陷（anomalous dip），该现象此前已在文献中被报道。升级后的装置可在7 K以上全温区范围内对频移和品质因数进行综合测量。

Conclusion: 该频移测量装置为研究间隙原子修饰铌腔中超导-正常态转变动力学提供了有效工具，有助于深入理解相关超导性质。

Abstract: The variation of the resonance frequency and intrinsic quality factor of superconducting radio-frequency cavities during the transition from the superconducting to the normal-conducting state provides essential insight into the fundamental superconducting properties of the cavity material. Investigating these transition dynamics is crucial for the continued advancement of niobium cavities whose near-surface regions are intentionally modified through the controlled introduction of interstitial atoms, such as oxygen and nitrogen, leading to the emergence of several novel behaviors whose underlying mechanisms are not yet fully understood. This work reports on the development and commissioning of a dedicated frequency-shift measurement setup. In its initial implementation, the system establishes a precise framework for determining the electron mean free path within both the superconducting penetration depth and the normal-conducting skin depth. It further enables investigation of an anomalous dip in the temperature dependence of the frequency shift near the critical temperature in cavities containing interstitial atoms in the near-surface lattice, a novel phenomenon previously reported in the literature. A recent upgrade, currently in the final stage of validation, significantly improves measurement accuracy and reproducibility. The improved setup enables comprehensive studies of the frequency shift and quality factor over the full temperature range above 7 K, contributing to a deeper understanding of the superconducting properties.

### [57] [Floquet mobility edges and transport in a periodically driven generalized Aubry-André model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21992)
*Jayashis Das,Vatsana Tiwari,Manish Kumar,Auditya Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究周期电场驱动对广义Aubry-André模型（GPD模型）Floquet谱的影响，发现了两种不同的Floquet迁移率边（bounded区的退定域-定域边和unbounded区的多分形-定域边），并展示了通过驱动参数调控这些迁移率边及相应输运行为的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义Aubry-André模型（GPD模型）已知存在迁移率边（mobility edges），但周期性电场驱动对该模型迁移率边和输运行为的影响尚不清楚，亟需系统研究。

Method: 采用Avila全局理论（Avila's global theory）对高频有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）进行解析分析，并结合分形维数（fractal dimension）和逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）等数值诊断手段。

Result: 发现了两种Floquet迁移率边：bounded regime中的退定域-定域（DL）边和unbounded regime中的多分形-定域（ML）边；这些迁移率边可通过驱动的振幅和频率进行有效调控；在特定驱动参数下观察到驱动诱导的定域化；bounded regime对应超扩散到准弹道输运，unbounded regime对应次扩散输运；低频驱动下观察到与高频有效描述显著且反直觉的偏离。

Conclusion: 准周期势与周期电场驱动的相互作用为工程化迁移率边和控制具有丰富谱特征的系统中的输运提供了有力机制。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of a periodic electric field drive on the generalized Aubry-André model, also known as the Ganeshan-Pixley-Das Sarma (GPD) model, which is well known as a host of mobility edges. Our study of the Floquet spectrum of the driven GPD model uncovers the emergence of two distinct Floquet mobility edges, a delocalized--localized (DL) edge in the bounded regime, and a multifractal--localized (ML) edge in the unbounded regime. Using analytical results derived from Avila's global theory applied to the high frequency effective Hamiltonian, together with numerical diagnostics such as the fractal dimension and inverse participation ratio, we demonstrate that these mobility edges can be effectively controlled by the amplitude and frequency of the electric field drive. We also identify drive-induced localization at specific values of the driving parameters, corresponding to dynamical localization points in the absence of quasiperiodic potential. Furthermore, the dynamical study of the periodically driven GPD model demonstrates superdiffusive to almost ballistic transport in the bounded regime corresponding to the DL edges, whereas subdiffusive transport is observed in the unbounded regime associated with the ML edges. We also analyze deviations from the high-frequency effective description by explicitly examining the low-frequency driving regime, where significant and counterintuitive deviations in both spectral properties and transport behavior are observed. Our study highlights the interplay of a quasiperiodic potential and a periodically varying electric field drive as a powerful mechanism to engineer mobility edges and control transport in systems with rich spectral features.

</details>

### [58] [Algebraic methods in periodic singular Liouville equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22175)
*Chin-Lung Wang*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文利用代数几何（algebraic geometry）研究平坦环面（flat torus）上具有多个奇点的非线性平均场Liouville方程，通过推广的Lamé方程的单值性理论（monodromy theory），给出了奇点权重之和为奇数情形下的代数度数（algebraic degree）精确计数公式，并为偶数情形提出了广义Lamé曲线的存在性猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将单奇点（N=1）情形的丰富代数几何结构（涉及Lamé曲线与预模形式（pre-modular forms））推广到多奇点（general N）情形，以系统理解非线性平均场方程解空间的结构。

Method: 以广义Lamé方程（generalized Lamé equations）的单值性理论（monodromy theory）为基本工具，分别处理奇点权重之和为奇数和偶数两种情形：奇数情形证明精确计数公式；偶数情形提出广义Lamé曲线的存在性命题。

Result: （1）当ℓ为奇数时，证明了代数度数（algebraic degree）的精确计数公式；（2）当ℓ为偶数时，提出了存在参数化无对数解（logarithmic-free solutions）的广义Lamé曲线（generalized Lamé curves）的猜想。

Conclusion: 多奇点情形下代数几何结构与单奇点情形具有深刻的类比关系，广义Lamé方程的单值性理论是建立这种联系的核心工具；奇偶性不同的ℓ导致解空间结构存在本质差异。

Abstract: We explain how algebraic geometry comes into play in the study of non-linear mean field (singular Liouville) equations $$ \triangle u + e^u = 4π\sum_{i = 1}^N \ell_i δ_{p_i} $$ on a flat torus $E = \Bbb C/Λ$, where $N, \ell_1, \ldots, \ell_N \in \Bbb N$, $p_i \in E$ are distinct points, and $δ_{p_i}$ is the Dirac measure at $p_i$.
  The case with one singular source ($N = 1$) had been studied extensively in recent years. We start with a survey of this case with emphasizes on the constructions of Lamé curves $\overline X_n$ and pre-modular forms $Z_n(σ, τ)$ which encodes the structure of solutions of the PDE.
  We then discuss extensions to the case of general $N$. The basic tool is the monodromy theory for generalized Lamé equations. Two aspects are discussed: (1) For $\ell := \sum_{i = 1}^N \ell_i$ being odd, an exact counting formula of \emph{algebraic degree} is proved. (2) For $\ell$ being even, the existence of generalized Lamé curves parametrizing logarithmic-free solutions is proposed.

### [59] [A variational formulation of stochastic thermodynamics: Spatially extended systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22298)
*Héctor Vaquero del Pino,François Gay-Balmaz,Hiroaki Yoshimura,Lock Yue Chew*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展经典场论的哈密顿原理，建立了热力学一致的随机场论（stochastic field theories）的变分形式，以局部细致平衡（local detailed balance）和熵产生（entropy production）为核心，实现了与标准随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）在轨迹层次和涨落定理（fluctuation theorems）上的对应，并基于广义拉格朗日-达朗贝尔原理（generalized Lagrange-d'Alembert principle）统一几何框架构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机场论通常基于唯象（phenomenological）构建，缺乏对热力学一致性（thermodynamic consistency）和局部细致平衡的系统评估，这阻碍了在场论层次上对不可逆性（irreversibility）进行超越标准随机热力学的物理描述。

Method: 通过将热力学第二定律作为公理引入，扩展经典场论的哈密顿原理（Hamilton's principle），构建热力学一致的随机场论变分形式；在扩展相空间（extended phase space）中同时包含构型变量（configurational variables）和热变量（thermal variables），并基于广义拉格朗日-达朗贝尔原理建立统一的几何框架。

Result: 该方法自然地涌现出新型涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relations），确保局部细致平衡；所得熵产生形式与标准随机热力学一致，并推广了单个轨迹层次热力学（trajectory-level thermodynamics）和涨落定理等关键结论。

Conclusion: 该构造在唯象建模与热力学一致性之间建立了自上而下的联系，潜在应用包括复杂流体（complex fluids）的热力学一致建模、连续体系统中的对称性约化（Lagrangian reduction by symmetry）以及随机偏微分方程（stochastic partial differential equations）的保结构数值格式（structure-preserving numerical schemes）。

Abstract: Stochastic field theories are often constructed phenomenologically, without a systematic assessment of thermodynamic consistency or local detailed balance. This may hinder a physical description of irreversibility at the field-theoretic level beyond the standard statistical formulation of stochastic thermodynamics. Here, we develop a variational formulation for thermodynamically consistent stochastic field theories by extending Hamilton's principle of classical field theory. Introducing the second law as an axiom yields a consistent local thermodynamic structure in which novel fluctuationdissipation relations emerge naturally, ensuring local detailed balance. Remarkably, the resulting entropy production takes the same form as in standard stochastic thermodynamics, up to a reformulation in an extended phase space incorporating both configurational and thermal variables. This correspondence extends key results, including individual trajectory-level thermodynamics and fluctuation theorems. The construction is formulated within a unified geometric framework based on a generalized Lagrange-d'Alembert principle, providing a top-down connection between phenomenological modeling and thermodynamic consistency. Potential applications include thermodynamically consistent modeling of complex fluids, Lagrangian reduction by symmetry in continuum systems, and structure-preserving numerical schemes for stochastic partial differential equations.

</details>


### [60] [Long-Range Correlated Random Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22447)
*Abbas Ali Saberi,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究通过长程关联逾渗模型引入矩阵元之间的代数相关性对随机矩阵本征值统计与谱密度的影响，发现在阈值 H_c = 3/4 处出现高斯统计，过剩峰度符号反转标志着从肥尾广义 t-分布到半圆律的转变，基于标度分析与数值模拟给出了新的谱区间预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机矩阵（random matrices）在多个学科中被广泛用于建模，而矩阵元之间的相关性对本征值统计的影响尚未被充分理解。本文旨在系统揭示代数相关性如何改变本征值分布与谱密度。

Method: 通过长程相关逾渗模型（long-range correlated percolation model）引入矩阵元之间的幂律衰减相关性 $\propto r^{-2H}$（$H > 0$），结合标度分析（scaling analysis）与大规模数值模拟进行分析。

Result: 当 H 变化时，本征值分布与过剩峰度（excess kurtosis）均发生定性改变；在阈值 H_c = 3/4 处出现高斯统计（Gaussian statistics），过剩峰度符号反转标志着从肥尾广义 t-分布（fat-tailed generalized t-distribution）到标准半圆律（semicircle law）的过渡。

Conclusion: 分析结果提供了清晰的预测，揭示了随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）中新的谱区间；将统计物理（statistical physics）、逾渗理论（percolation theory）与随机矩阵分析的技术联系起来，为相关系综（correlated ensembles）的普适性提供了新视角。

Abstract: Motivated by the importance ascribed to correlations in random matrices used to model phenomena in various scientific disciplines, we report how algebraic correlations between matrix elements affect the eigenvalue statistics and spectral density of random matrices. These correlations, introduced through a long-range correlated percolation model, decay as a power law $\propto r^{-2H}$, with exponent $H > 0$. As $H$ varies, both the eigenvalue distribution and excess kurtosis undergo qualitative changes. At the threshold $H_c = 3/4$, characterized by emergent Gaussian statistics, a sign change in excess kurtosis marks a transition from a fat-tailed generalized $t$-distribution to one that gradually approaches the standard semicircle law for $H \gg H_c$. Our analytical results, based on scaling analysis and supported by extensive numerical simulations, provide clear predictions and uncover novel spectral regimes in random matrix theory. Our results connect techniques from statistical physics, percolation theory, and random matrix analysis, offering a new perspective on universality in correlated ensembles.

</details>


### [61] [Long-Range Order in Coupled $D$-dimensional Kuramoto Oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22151)
*Zhongpu Qiu,Tianyi Wu,Linkai Zhang,Sheng Fang,Jun Meng,Jingfang Fan,Hugues Chaté*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现，在低维晶格（d=1,2）上的局域耦合矢量库拉托振荡器（vector Kuramoto oscillators）系统中，长程序（LRO）仅在奇数维 D 时意外出现。这一奇偶依赖效应源于双振荡器动力学的根本不同：奇数 D 的单元在任何耦合下都能同步，而偶数 D 对需要有限阈值。通过重整化群（RG）分析，奇数 D 系统在弱耦合不动点下映射为铁磁模型，形成有序的“半球”相，而偶数 D 系统保持无序。此外，取向长程序在 d=1 和 d=2 中均出现，但频率长程序仅出现在 d=2 中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究低维晶格上局域耦合矢量 Kuramoto 振荡器中的长程序涌现，尤其是奇偶维数 D 对相行为的影响，并对比连续对称性模型的已知行为，揭示淬火无序（quenched disorder）提供了一种根本性的有序化新途径。

Method: 采用双振荡器动力学分析、数值模拟以及重整化群（renormalization group, RG）分析，研究低维晶格（d=1,2）上 D 维矢量 Kuramoto 模型的相变与有序相。

Result: 长程序仅在奇数 D 时出现；奇数 D 的振荡器对在任何耦合下同步，偶数 D 对需要有限阈值；RG 分析显示 d ≤ 2 时存在弱耦合不动点，奇数 D 系统映射为铁磁模型的“半球”有序相；取向 LRO 在 d=1 和 d=2 中均存在，频率 LRO 仅存在于 d=2。

Conclusion: 低维矢量 Kuramoto 系统中奇偶维数 D 决定了长程序的涌现能力，淬火无序为有序化提供了不同于连续对称性模型的新机制。

Abstract: We show that the long-range order (LRO) strikingly emerges in systems of locally coupled $D$-dimensional vector Kuramoto oscillators on low-dimensional lattices ($d=1,2$), but only for odd $D$. This parity-dependent effect is traced to two-oscillator dynamics, where odd-$D$ units synchronize for any coupling, while even-$D$ pairs require a finite threshold. This fundamental difference selectively seeds collective order in large-scale systems, a phenomenon demonstrated by our numerical simulations. A renormalization group analysis reveals a RG flow to a weak-coupling fixed point for $d \le 2$. In this limit, odd-$D$ systems effectively map to a ferromagnetic model, developing an ordered ``hemisphere" phase, whereas even-$D$ systems remain disordered. Our findings further reveal orientational LRO emerges in both $d=1$ and $d=2$, but frequency LRO requires $d=2$. We contrast these results with the established behavior of models possessing continuous symmetry, highlighting how quenched disorder provides a fundamentally new route to order.

</details>


### [62] [The quantum harmonic oscillator in a dissipative bath of anyon pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22342)
*Nils-Henrik Meyer,Michael Thorwart,Axel Pelster*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文将开放量子系统（open quantum systems）的形式论推广至任意子（anyon）浴，通过将一维Grundberg-Hansson谐波束缚任意子对映射为具有重新标度频率的玻色子浴，利用虚时路径积分（imaginary-time path integral）和推广的Wick定理的涂抹公式（smearing formula）近似计算了任意子浴的谱密度（spectral density），揭示了中间温度区间任意子特征最为显著的现象，并给出了耗散谐振子（dissipative harmonic oscillator）在任意子浴中的弛豫动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放量子系统的研究主要针对玻色子或费米子环境，任意子作为满足分数统计（fractional statistics）的准粒子尚未被纳入浴的构建框架。该工作旨在将开放量子系统形式论推广至任意子浴，探索任意子统计特性对量子耗散过程的影响。

Method: 研究采用由一维Grundberg-Hansson谐波束缚任意子对构成的耗散任意子浴，该浴由一个统计参数（statistical parameter）表征。通过将任意子映射为具有重新标度谐振子频率的玻色子浴（bosonic bath），原始双线性系统-浴耦合（bilinear system-bath coupling）呈现非多项式形式。利用虚时路径积分形式和推广的Wick定理（涂抹公式）近似计算任意子浴的谱密度。

Result: 任意子浴的谱密度具有非平凡的温度依赖性（nontrivial temperature dependence）。求得了耗散谐振子在任意子浴中的弛豫动力学，在低温和高温极限下分别呈现良好定义的行为，而任意子特征在中间温度区间最为显著。

Conclusion: 任意子浴所引入的分数统计效应在中等温度区域产生最明显的耗散特征，为理解任意子作为环境时的量子耗散（quantum dissipation）行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We generalize the formalism of open quantum systems to introduce anyon baths. In particular, we work out a dissipative anyon bath composed of independent pairs of one-dimensional Grundberg-Hansson harmonically bound anyons, which are characterized by one statistical parameter. Using a mapping of these anyons to a bosonic bath with rescaled oscillator frequencies, we show that the original bilinear system-bath coupling assumes a particular non-polynomial form. To determine the relaxation properties, we use the imaginary-time path integral formalism together with a generalization of Wick's theorem in the form of a smearing formula. The latter allows to approximately calculate the anyon bath spectral density, which acquires a nontrivial temperature dependence. The corresponding relaxation dynamics of the dissipative harmonic oscillator in an anyon bath is found. Well defined limits are revealed for both low and high temperatures. Anyonic features turn out to be most pronounced in the regime of intermediate temperatures.

</details>


### [63] [Spiral, target, stripe, and disordered waves in active six-state Potts models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22353)
*Hiroshi Noguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）在方形和六边形格点上研究了活性六态Potts模型（active six-state Potts model）中的多种波动模式，揭示了无序波、螺旋波、靶波和条纹波的形成条件、共存与粗化行为，以及偶数/奇数态波之间的相变特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波动传播普遍存在于各类非平衡系统（nonequilibrium systems）中，本研究旨在通过活性六态Potts模型系统性地探索不同波动模式的形成条件与动态行为。

Method: 采用蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）在方形格点（square lattice）和六边形格点（hexagonal lattice）上研究活性六态Potts模型（active six-state Potts model）的波动性质。

Result: 弱排斥下形成无序波（disordered wave），强排斥下形成螺旋波（spiral wave, SP），更强排斥下出现靶波（target wave, TG）和条纹波（stripe wave, ST）。在小体系中三种波可共存，大体系则不共存。粗化过程中SP波作为中间态出现。偶数/奇数态SP波在对角排斥+非翻转吸引条件下形成，且两种条件下波类型不同，分为前向波和后向波，其相变为一级相变（first-order transition）。

Conclusion: 活性六态Potts模型中波动模式的种类和转变依赖于排斥强度与接触规则；偶数/奇数态波并非如先前认为的相同，而是存在前向与后向两种不同类型的传播机制，且它们之间的转变具有一级相变特征。

Abstract: Wave propagation can be observed in various nonequilibrium systems. In this study, we investigated the properties of several wave modes in active six-state Potts models using Monte Carlo simulations of square and hexagonal lattices. Disordered and spiral (SP) waves of six states are formed under weak and strong repulsions at nonflip contacts, respectively. The target (TG) and stripe (ST) waves were found to emerge under stronger repulsion. These three wave modes (SP, TG, and ST) can temporally coexist in small systems near the transition points but they do not switch in large systems or far from these transition points. During coarsening from randomly mixed states to ST waves, SP waves appear at an intermediate stage. The SP wave modes of three even- or odd-numbered states (states $s=0,2,4$ or $s=1,3,5$) emerge under two conditions: repulsion at the diagonal contact and attraction at nonflip contacts. Previously thought to be identical for both conditions, the wave types were found to differ, comprising forward and backward waves ($s=1\to 3\to 5\to 1$ or $s=1\to 5\to 3\to 1$), whose domain boundaries move by the two-step and four-step forward flips, respectively. The transition between the waves of the even- and odd-numbered states is first-order for both the forward and backward waves.

</details>


### [64] [Mean-Field Theory for the Three-State Active Lattice Gas Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22536)
*Ana L. N. Dias,Ronald Dickman,Tiago Venzel Rosembach*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对 Venzel 等人（2024）提出的三态活性物质模型（three-state active matter model）的简化版本，发展了一种包含空间结构的平均场描述（mean-field description）。通过在密度-噪声平面上数值积分四阶龙格-库塔（Runge-Kutta）方法求解的耦合非线性微分方程三角晶格，并结合蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，揭示了多种高密度有序结构及其间的意外跃迁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究（Venzel et al., 2024）提出了三态活性物质模型，但尚无包含空间结构的平均场描述对其简化版本进行系统分析。本研究旨在填补这一空白，通过平均场理论结合数值积分与蒙特卡洛模拟，揭示该模型在密度-噪声参数空间中的有序结构及其稳定性。

Method: 针对简化版三态活性物质模型，发展了一种包含空间结构的平均场描述，构建了三角晶格上的耦合非线性微分方程组，并采用四阶龙格-库塔（fourth-order Runge-Kutta）格式进行数值积分。同时进行了蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟以作对比。

Result: 从不同的有序初始位形出发探测了相应稳态的稳定性，在密度（ρ）-噪声（η）平面上发现了多种高密度有序结构。与蒙特卡洛模拟的对比显示，在某些情况下存在有序构型类型之间的意外跃迁（unexpected transitions）。

Conclusion: 提出的包含空间结构的平均场描述能够捕捉简化三态活性物质模型的主要特征，但蒙特卡洛模拟揭示的意外有序态跃迁表明该模型在有序-有序转变方面存在更为丰富的动力学行为，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: We develop a mean-field description including spatial structure for a simplified version of the three-state active matter model studied by Venzel et al. (Phys. Rev. E 110, 014109 (2024)). The resulting triangular lattice of coupled nonlinear differential equations are integrated numerically using a fourth-order Runge-Kutta scheme. Starting from various ordered initial configurations, we probe the stability of the corresponding stationary states, revealing the presence of various high-density ordered structures in the density(\r{ho})-noise(η) plane. The results are compared with Monte Carlo simulations of the simplified model, yielding, in certain cases, unexpected transitions between ordered configuration types.

</details>

# math.NT [[Back]](#toc)

### [65] [Non-linear geometry of multiple zeta values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22735)
*Francis Brown*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文综述了多重zeta值（multiple zeta values）的两种几何表示：传统的线性几何（linear geometry，基于黎曼球面上三穿孔的迭代积分）以及新兴的非线性几何（non-linear geometry，涉及被积函数分母中的矩阵行列式）。文章追溯了非线性几何的起源，并围绕热带几何（tropical geometry）、热带曲线模空间、量子场论中的费曼积分（Feynman integrals）、整数矩阵的一般线性群以及二次型约化理论等主题，提出了一个基于行列式表示的多重zeta值几何框架，并列出若干开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多重zeta值自1990年代被重新发现以来，在数学与物理学中广泛应用；其标准表示（线性几何）已被充分研究，但存在另一类同样重要但性质截然不同的行列式表示（非线性几何），尚缺乏系统的几何框架。本文旨在追溯非线性几何的起源，整合相关数学与物理工具，并推动该方向的研究。

Method: 本文采用综述与概念整合的方法，通过介绍热带几何、热带曲线模空间、费曼积分、整数矩阵的一般线性群及二次型约化理论等主题，系统阐述多重zeta值的非线性几何表示及其几何框架。

Result: 文章识别并梳理了多重zeta值的非线性几何表示（即被积函数分母中出现矩阵行列式的积分表示），将其与热带几何、模空间、费曼积分、一般线性群及二次型约化理论联系起来，并提出了一个统一的几何框架。

Conclusion: 该综述提出了一个基于非线性行列式表示的多重zeta值几何框架，并列出若干有待进一步研究的开放问题，为后续研究提供了方向。

Abstract: Since their rediscovery in the 1990s, multiple zeta values have become ubiquitous in many areas of mathematics and physics. Their standard integral and sum representations can usually be traced back to a single source, namely the iterated integrals on the Riemann sphere with three punctures. We refer to such representations as the \emph{linear} geometry of multiple zeta values, since the denominators of the corresponding integrands factor completely into linear terms.
  However, there also exist equally important and entirely distinct integral representations for multiple zeta values arising in mathematics and physics, in which matrix determinants appear in the denominator of the integrand. We call this the \emph{non-linear} geometry of multiple zeta values. These lectures trace the origins of this non-linear geometry and provide an introductory journey through a range of topics including tropical geometry, the moduli spaces of tropical curves, Feynman integrals in quantum field theory, the general linear group of integer matrices, and the reduction theory of quadratic forms. In doing so, we propose a geometric framework for multiple zeta values based on such non-linear, determinantal representations and set out a number of open questions for future research.

</details>

Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次测量了$B^+\toπ^+μ^+μ^-$衰变角分布的前后不对称性$A_{\rm FB}$和平坦项$F_{H}$，基于LHCb实验在2011至2018年间采集的9 fb$^{-1}$质子-质子对撞数据。分析在双缪子质量平方的两个区间（高/低于窄粲偶素共振区）进行，标准模型预言均落在测量获得置信区间内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验标准模型（Standard Model）在稀有重味衰变$B^+\toπ^+μ^+μ^-$中的角分布预言，为寻找超出标准模型的新物理（new physics）提供约束。

Method: 利用LHCb实验在2011-2018年采集的9 fb$^{-1}$质子-质子对撞数据，测量$B^+\toπ^+μ^+μ^-$衰变的角分布参数$A_{\rm FB}$和$F_{H}$。分析在双缪子质量平方（dimuon mass squared）的两个区间独立进行：一个高于、一个低于包含$J/\psi$和$\psi(2S)$窄粲偶素共振的区域。

Result: 在高质量区间，标准模型预言落在测量所得68%置信水平（confidence level）区间内；在低质量区间，标准模型预言落在99%置信水平区间内。

Conclusion: 测量结果与标准模型预言一致，未发现显著偏离，从而为相关新物理场景提供了实验约束。

Abstract: This paper presents the first measurement of the forward-backward asymmetry, $A_{\rm FB}$, and the flat term, $F_{H}$, that parameterise the angular distribution of the $B^+\toπ^+μ^+μ^-$ decay. The proton-proton collision dataset used in the analysis corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 9 fb$^{-1}$, collected with the LHCb experiment between 2011 and 2018. The analysis is performed in two intervals of dimuon mass squared, one above and one below the region containing the $J\mskip -3mu/\mskip -2muψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ narrow charmonium resonances. The Standard Model predictions lie within the obtained $68\%$ confidence level interval in the high-mass and within the $99\%$ interval in the low-mass region.

</details>


### [67] [$b\to s\ell^+\ell^- (\ell = e, μ, τ)$ and $b\to sν\barν$ at Belle and Belle II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22079)
*Meihong Liu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于 Belle 与 Belle~II 实验累积的总积分亮度为 1.2 ab⁻¹ 的 e⁺e⁻ → BB̅ 对撞数据，利用 Υ(4S) 共振态提供的干净事件环境和精确初始运动学约束，系统研究了涉及中微子（neutrino）能量缺失的 B 介子稀有衰变过程，包括 B⁺ → K⁺νν̅ 的重新解读、首次对 B → X_s νν̅ 的遍举测量，以及涉及 τ 轻子衰变能量缺失的 B → K⁽*⁾τ⁺τ⁻ 等稀有衰变搜寻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Belle 与 Belle~II 实验累积的大量 B 介子对撞数据为研究涉及中微子能量缺失的稀有衰变过程提供了独特机遇，这些过程对标准模型（Standard Model）之外的物理信号（即新物理，new physics）敏感。特别是 B⁺ → K⁺νν̅ 和 B → X_s νν̅ 等过程的精确测量，以及 B → K⁽*⁾τ⁺τ⁻ 这类味改变中性流（flavor-changing neutral current, FCNC）过程的搜寻，有助于检验标准模型并寻找新物理迹象。

Method: 利用 Υ(4S) 共振态处 e⁺e⁻ → BB̅ 对撞产生的干净事件环境与良好约束的初态运动学（initial-state kinematics），通过直接重建 B 介子衰变中的缺失能量（missing energy）来识别中微子信号。对 B⁺ → K⁺νν̅ 采用重新解读（reinterpretation）方法，对 B → X_s νν̅ 实施首次遍举（inclusive）测量，对 B⁰ → K*⁰τ⁺τ⁻、B⁰ → K_S⁰τ⁺τ⁻ 和 B⁺ → K⁺τ⁺τ⁻ 等过程则通过 τ 轻子衰变产生的能量缺失进行搜寻。

Result: 累积总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）达到 1.2 ab⁻¹ 的 e⁺e⁻ → BB̅ 对撞数据被用于上述多项稀有衰变过程的分析，涵盖了中微子直接产生于 B 介子衰变和产生于 τ 轻子衰变两种能量缺失来源的情形。

Conclusion: 该联合数据分析表明，Belle 与 Belle~II 实验的大数据量和对撞环境优势使其特别适用于中微子能量缺失通道的精确测量和新物理搜寻，为后续 B 介子稀有衰变的系统学研究提供了重要基础。

Abstract: The Belle and Belle~II experiments have accumulated a combined data set of $1.2~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$ of $e^+e^- \to B\bar{B}$ collisions at the $Υ(4S)$ resonance. Owing to the clean event environment and the well-constrained initial-state kinematics, these data are particularly well suited for studying channels involving missing energy from neutrinos. This includes the reinterpretation of $B^+\to K^+ν\barν$ and the first inclusive measurement of $B\to X_sν\barν$ with the missing energy directly from $B$ decays, as well as searches involving missing energy from $τ$ decays, such as $B^0\to K^{*0}τ^+τ^-$, $B^0\to K_S^{0}τ^+τ^-$, and $B^+\to K^{+}τ^+τ^-$.

</details>


### [68] [Cryogenic pure CsI as a probe for neutrino electromagnetic interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22485)
*C. M. Lewis*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出基于低温纯碘化铯（cryogenic undoped CsI）晶体的反应堆中微子探测器概念设计，利用其低阈值和低本底特性，通过抑制核反冲信号使反中微子-电子散射成为主导观测道，有望将中微子磁矩和毫电荷的实验上限提高一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在反应堆位点搜索中微子电磁相互作用（electromagnetic interactions）需要同时具备超低能量阈值（ultra-low threshold）和稳定的低本底环境，而现有探测器难以同时满足这些条件。

Method: 提出一种基于低温纯碘化铯晶体的概念设计，将CsI晶体浸入有源氙掺杂液氩反符合探测器（active xenon-doped liquid argon veto）中，并在现实的内源和环境本底下进行评估。

Result: 低温CsI在低能区对MeV量级反应堆反中微子产生的核反冲信号有效“失明”，从而使反中微子-电子散射成为主导可观测道；基于现有探测器能力，可将中微子磁矩（neutrino magnetic moment）和毫电荷（millicharge）的当前反应堆上限提高一个数量级（order-of-magnitude improvement）。

Conclusion: 低温纯CsI提供了一条独特且可扩展的途径，可用于引领反中微子-电子散射物理的前沿研究。

Abstract: Searches for neutrino electromagnetic interactions at reactor sites require an unusual combination of ultra-low thresholds and a stable low-background environment. It is shown here that cryogenic undoped cesium iodide (CsI) naturally satisfies these conditions in a way prior detectors have not. Although suppression of nuclear recoil ionization efficiency at low energies limits the use of this scintillator for coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering, that same property renders the detector effectively blind to those nuclear recoils from MeV-scale reactor antineutrinos. This leaves the low-energy regime free to expose neutrino-electron ($\barν_{e} -e^{-}$) scattering as the dominant observable channel and converts cryogenic CsI into a targeted probe of electromagnetic couplings. This work presents a conceptual design based on pure CsI crystals immersed in an active xenon-doped liquid argon veto evaluated under realistic intrinsic and environmental backgrounds. Under present detector capabilities, order-of-magnitude improvements over current reactor limits on the neutrino magnetic moment and millicharge are achievable. Cryogenic pure CsI therefore offers a distinctive and scalable route to leading studies of $\barν_{e} -e^{-}$ physics.

</details>


### [69] [Dr.Sai: An agentic AI for real-world physics analysis at BESIII](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22541)
*Mingfeng He,Fayu Jiang,Junkun Jiao,Mingrun Li,Ke Li,Yipu Liao,Beijiang Liu,Tong Liu,Fazhi Qi,Zijie Shang,Weimin Song,Yue Sun,Xiongfei Wang,Hong Wang,Dongbo Xiong,Changzheng Yuan,Bolun Zhang,Zhengde Zhang,Xuliang Zhu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出 Dr.Sai，一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统，能够将自然语言自动转化为高能物理（HEP）分析工作流，并在 BESIII 实验的 J/ψ 衰变分支比大规模重测量中验证了其有效性，结果与已有基准一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理实验（如 BESIII）产生的 PB 级数据需要复杂的分析工作流（模拟、重建、统计分析等），传统人工方法耗时数月甚至数年，劳动密集且易引入偏差，限制了大规模系统性扫描。随着数据量增长，这一范式严重拖慢科学发现速度。

Method: Dr.Sai 是一个基于大语言模型（Large Language Model, LLM）的多智能体系统（multi-agent system）。该系统利用 LLM 的自然语言理解与代码生成能力，将自然语言科学任务翻译为严格的物理分析工作流，并能集成高能物理工具（如 ROOT、BOSS），在真实的 BESIII 计算环境中自主执行。

Result: Dr.Sai 成功完成了 J/ψ 衰变中十个分支比（branching fraction）的大规模重测量，无需人工编码。所有结果与已有基准（established benchmarks）一致，验证了系统在实际高能物理环境中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作为自主科学发现（autonomous discovery）提供了蓝图，并且其方法可推广至其他数据密集型领域，如天文学（astronomy）和基因组学（genomics）。

Abstract: High Energy Physics (HEP) experiments like BESIII produce petabyte-scale data. Extracting physics results requires complex workflows (simulation, reconstruction, statistical analysis, etc.) that traditionally take experts months or years. Current manual methods are labor-intensive, prone to bias, and limit large-scale systematic scans. As data grows, this paradigm slows discovery. Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a solution. Their natural language understanding and code generation capabilities allow them to interpret scientific tasks and integrate with HEP tools (e.g., ROOT, BOSS) to act as an "AI partner" for autonomous analysis. We present Dr.Sai, an LLM-powered multi-agent system that translates natural language into rigorous physics workflows. As validation, Dr.Sai performed large-scale re-measurements of ten J/psi decay branching fractions - without manual coding. It successfully navigated the real BESIII computing environment and produced results matching established benchmarks. The article details Dr.Sai's architecture, the validation results, and performance evaluation. This work provides a blueprint for autonomous discovery, with relevance to other data-intensive fields like astronomy and genomics.

</details>


### [70] [Searches for light exotic scalar decays at the e$^+$e$^-$ Higgs factory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22572)
*Bartłomiej Brudnowski,Kamil Zembaczyński,Aleksander Filip Żarnecki*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本论文基于国际直线对撞机（ILC）250 GeV运行方案，利用国际大型探测器（ILD）的全模拟和Delphes框架的快模拟，研究了在Higgs-strahlung过程中寻找轻标量粒子（scalar-strahlung）的预期截面限制和灵敏度，涵盖b b̅、τ⁺τ⁻和不可见衰变道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对于b b̅衰变道，使用了国际大型探测器（ILD）的全模拟（full simulation）；对于τ⁺τ⁻和不可见衰变道，则基于Delphes框架的快模拟（fast simulation）。所有分析均假设ILC在250 GeV能量下的运行场景。

Result: 给出了在b b̅衰变道中通过全模拟获得的预期截面限制（cross section limits），以及在τ⁺τ⁻和不可见衰变道中通过快模拟获得的预期灵敏度（expected sensitivity）。

Conclusion: 该研究为排除或限制轻标量粒子在ILC上的产生提供了定量预期，有助于指导未来Higgs工厂的物理搜索策略。

Abstract: The physics program of the Higgs factory will focus on measurements of the 125 GeV Higgs boson, with the Higgs-strahlung process being the dominant production channel at 250 GeV. However, similar production of exotic light scalars, in a scalar-strahlug process, is still not excluded by the existing experimental data, provided their coupling to the SM gauge bosons is sufficiently suppressed. This was selected as one of the focus topics of the ECFA Higgs/Top/EW factory study. Presented are the expected cross section limits from the search in the $b\,\bar{b}$ decay channel, based on a full simulation of the International Large Detector (ILD), as well as the expected sensitivity in $τ^+τ^-$ and invisible decay channels, based on the fast simulation in the Delphes framework, assuming 250 GeV ILC running scenario.

### [71] [Hydrodynamics and Energy Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21971)
*João Barata,Matvey V. Kuzmin,Ian Moult,Andrey V. Sadofyev,João M. Silva*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究多体量子态（尤其是重离子碰撞后产生的物质）中的能量-能量关联函数（EEC），在共线极限下识别出一系列动力学区域：从大角度的经典集体流标度、中等角度的集体流体动力学模式、到小角度的光锥算符乘积展开（light-ray OPE）以及最小角度的稀薄强子物质行为，从而为多体QCD态中EEC的角度结构提供统一图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解重离子碰撞后产生的高温高密量子多体物质（夸克-胶子等离子体）的内部结构是强相互作用物质研究的重要问题。现有研究缺乏对能量-能量关联函数（EEC）在多体QCD态中完整角度结构的系统理解，本文旨在通过EEC揭示从集体流体动力学到强子化等不同动力学区域之间的关联。

Method: 在共线极限下对EEC进行角度结构分析，区分断开贡献（disconnected contributions）与连通贡献（connected contributions）。具体地，对于大角度区域的断开贡献，采用具有boost不变性的Gubser流体力学流场解析计算EEC的角度依赖关系，并引入方位角扰动以探测各向异性初始态。对于较小角度区域，利用集体流体动力学模式描述连通贡献，并与共形场论（CFT）中重荷态EEC的结果进行类比。

Result: 大角度区域EEC由断开贡献主导，产生由介质集体流决定的经典标度行为，并在Gubser流模型下获得解析表达式。中等角度区域连通贡献主导，EEC由集体流体动力学模式控制，其角度行为与共形场论中重荷态EEC类似。更小角度区域匹配光锥算符乘积展开（light-ray OPE）结构，最终交叉到稀薄强子物质区域。

Conclusion: 上述结果建立了多体QCD态中EEC角度结构的统一图像，表明EEC可以作为探测重离子碰撞中物质性质（如集体流动、初始态各向异性、流体动力学模式）的新观测量。

Abstract: We study energy-energy correlators (EECs) in many-body quantum states, focusing on the matter produced in the aftermath of heavy-ion collisions. We analyze the angular structure of EECs in the collinear limit and identify a sequence of dynamical regimes. At the largest angular separations within the small-angle regime, the observable is dominated by disconnected contributions, leading to a classical scaling determined by the collective flow of the medium. We explicitly construct this contribution for hadrons produced from a hydrodynamic medium described by boost-invariant Gubser flow, obtaining the angular dependence of the EEC analytically. We further consider azimuthal perturbations to this flow, illustrating how EECs can be used to probe anisotropies in the initial state. At smaller angular separations, connected contributions become increasingly important. We argue that in this regime the EEC is controlled by collective hydrodynamic modes. The resulting angular behavior is similar to the one identified in the EECs of heavy and large-charge states of conformal field theories. At even smaller angles, this regime is expected to match onto the structure determined by the light-ray operator product expansion, before eventually crossing over to the smallest-angle behavior characteristic of dilute hadronic matter. Altogether, these results provide a unified picture of the angular structure of EECs in many-body QCD states and suggest new observables sensitive to the properties of matter in heavy-ion collisions.

</details>


### [72] [Solar Reflection of Inelastic Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21996)
*Haipeng An,Haoming Nie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出太阳反射非弹性暗物质（SR iDM）模型，通过太阳内部高能电子散射使暗物质粒子获得高速尾巴，并在探测器内通过退激释放质量劈裂能，从而增强MeV量级暗物质的直接探测信号。基于蒙特卡洛模拟生成速度与能量分布，计算氙和半导体实验中的事件率，给出新的参数空间约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统直接探测实验对MeV量级暗物质灵敏度有限，因能量沉积低于探测阈值。该研究旨在利用太阳反射机制与非弹性暗物质（inelastic dark matter, iDM）模型，提升低质量暗物质的可探测性。

Method: 采用非弹性暗物质模型：太阳内的高能电子将基态暗物质粒子散射激发至激发态；当激发态粒子到达地球探测器后发生退激，释放质量劈裂能（mass-splitting energy）Δ。利用详细蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）生成太阳反射iDM在不同暗物质质量mχ和质量劈裂Δ下的速度与能量分布，并计算当前氙（xenon）实验与半导体（semiconductor）实验中的事件率与能量沉积。

Result: 模拟结果显示，MeV量级iDM的太阳反射可产生足够高的能量沉积，超出探测器阈值。当前氙与半导体实验能够对Mχ-Δ参数空间施加新的约束。

Conclusion: 太阳反射非弹性暗物质模型为探索MeV尺度暗物质提供了有效途径，现有实验数据可用于排除此前未约束的参数区域。

Abstract: Solar-reflected dark matter (SRDM) consists of dark-matter particles up-scattered and accelerated by energetic electrons in the solar interior, producing a high-velocity tail that can enhance signals in direct-detection experiments, especially for MeV-scale masses. We consider an inelastic dark matter (iDM) model, in which solar scattering populates the excited state; subsequent de-excitation in terrestrial detectors releases the mass-splitting energy, substantially helping the energy release of the collision to be larger than the detector threshold. Using detailed Monte Carlo simulations, we generate the velocity and energy distributions of solar-reflected iDM over a range of dark-matter masses $m_χ$ and mass splittings $Δ$. We then compute event rates and energy depositions for current xenon and semiconductor experiments. Our results show that these experiments can place new constraints on the parameter space of MeV-scale iDM.

</details>

*Motoo Suzuki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了拓扑通量扇区之间的动力学混合（kinetic mixing）能够有效移动QCD的$\barθ$角，从而诱导CP破坏效应；通过(1+1)维$U(1)\times U(1)$规范理论和四维三形式场描述两种途径进行分析，并讨论了该机制对强CP问题（strong CP problem）及现有解决方案的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨动力学混合是否能够改变QCD的$\barθ$角并产生CP破坏效应，进而评估这一机制对强CP问题及其标准解决方案（如轴子机制或CP/宇称机制）的可行性与鲁棒性。

Method: 首先在(1+1)维$U(1)\times U(1)$规范理论中进行分析，作为一种受控设定，展示动力学混合如何导致电通量可观测的偏移；随后将分析推广到四维，使用三形式场（three-form field）描述耦合了额外$U(1)$三形式规范场的QCD。

Result: 动力学混合使隐藏扇区通量（hidden-sector fluxes）偏移QCD的有效$\theta$参数，并诱导出$\langle G\tilde{G}\rangle$的非零期望值。

Conclusion: 该机制对强CP问题具有重要含义；标准解决方案（如轴子机制或基于CP/宇称的机制）在特定条件下可能被破坏，但在其他条件下仍保持鲁棒性。

Abstract: We argue that kinetic mixing between topological flux sectors generates an effective shift of the QCD $\barθ$ angle, thereby inducing CP-violating effects. To demonstrate this mechanism, we analyze a $(1+1)$-dimensional $U(1)\times U(1)$ gauge theory as a controlled setting, where kinetic mixing leads to observable shifts in electric fluxes. We then extend the analysis to four dimensions using a three-form field description of QCD coupled to an additional $U(1)$ three-form gauge field. We find that hidden-sector fluxes, through kinetic mixing, shift the effective $θ$ parameter of QCD and induce a nonzero expectation value of $\langle G\tilde{G}\rangle$. We discuss the implications for the strong CP problem and clarify under which conditions standard solutions, such as axion or CP/parity-based mechanisms, are compromised or remain robust.

</details>


### [74] [Quark hierarchies and CP violation from the Siegel modular group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21979)
*M. Carducci,D. Meloni,M. Parriciatu,J. T. Penedo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于亏格 g=2 模不变性（modular invariance）研究味理论（flavour theory），提出了一种在模空间（moduli space）不变点或区域附近通过残余对称性产生费米子质量层级（mass hierarchies）的机制。该机制被应用于解释夸克质量层级、CP 破坏及混合现象，通过模的真空期望值（vacuum expectation values）自发性破缺味对称性和 CP 对称性。一个基准模型（benchmark model）表明，在对称极限下质量比消失，且模的值趋近于特殊点（如 τ₁≃ω, τ₂≃ω, i）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于利用更高亏格（genus g=2）的模不变性构建味理论，探索费米子质量层级在模空间不变点或区域附近的生成机制，以解释夸克质量层级、CP 破坏及混合现象，并避免引入额外的标量场（scalar fields）。

Method: 方法基于亏格 g=2 模不变性及其模空间中的不变点或区域，在此处保留残余对称性（residual symmetry），从而诱导出费米子质量层级（modular proximity-induced hierarchies）。模的真空期望值作为味对称性和 CP 对称性自发破缺的唯一来源。

Result: 基准模型成功解释了夸克质量层级和 CP 破坏，质量比在对称极限（symmetric limit）下消失，夸克混合也被复现。模的值趋近于特殊值，如 τ₁≃ω 和 τ₂≃ω, i（ω 为三次单位根，i 为虚数单位）。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了基于亏格 g=2 模不变性的味理论能够有效产生费米子质量层级，为解释夸克质量结构、CP 破坏及混合提供了新的框架，且模的真空期望值是唯一的对称性破缺来源。

Abstract: We investigate theories of flavour based on genus $g=2$ modular invariance and analyze how fermion mass hierarchies can be generated in this context, in the vicinity of invariant points or regions in moduli space where a residual symmetry is preserved. We apply this mechanism of modular proximity-induced hierarchies to the quark sector, with the vacuum expectation values of the moduli being the only sources of spontaneous breaking of the flavour and CP symmetries. We present a benchmark model where quark mass hierarchies and CP violation are explained, with mass ratios vanishing in the symmetric limit, and quark mixing is reproduced. In this model, the values of the moduli turn out to be close to special values such as $τ_1 \simeq ω$ and $τ_2 \simeq ω, i$.
