### [75] [Super-Heisenberg protocol for dark matter and high-frequency gravitational wave search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22336)
*Wakutaka Nakano,Ryoto Takai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于彭宁阱（Penning trap）中二维离子晶体的量子增强传感方案，用于探测类波暗物质（wave-like dark matter）和高频引力波（high-frequency gravitational waves）。该协议利用自旋-运动压缩态（spin-motion squeezed states）提升信噪比，并实现相对于离子数的超海森堡标度（super-Heisenberg scaling）。在考虑离子自旋的退相干（decoherence）和退相移（dephasing）情况下，分析了方案对轴子类粒子（axion-like particle）、暗光子（dark photon）以及高频引力波的灵敏度。结果表明，该方案为探索光暗物质和高频引力波中此前未涉及的参数空间提供了有前景的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探测手段难以覆盖类波暗物质（如轴子类粒子和暗光子）以及高频引力波的某些未探索参数空间，需要发展新传感方案以突破海森堡极限（Heisenberg limit）并获得更高灵敏度。

Method: 基于彭宁阱中的二维离子晶体，通过制备自旋-运动压缩态实现量子增强，利用该压缩态提升信噪比并实现超海森堡标度；同时建模并纳入了离子自旋的退相干与退相移效应。

Result: 量子增强方案使探测灵敏度实现超海森堡标度，优于传统方法；在考虑退相干和退相移后，仍能有效覆盖此前未涉及的参数空间。

Conclusion: 二维离子晶体结合该量子增强协议为推进光暗物质和高频引力波的实验搜索提供了有前景的技术平台。

Abstract: We propose a quantum-enhanced sensing scheme for the detection of wave-like dark matter and high-frequency gravitational waves using two-dimensional ion crystals in a Penning trap. The protocol employs spin-motion squeezed states to improve the signal-to-noise ratio and enable a super-Heisenberg scaling with respect to the number of ions over a broad parameter range. We analyze the sensitivity of the protocol to representative wave-like dark matter candidates, including the axion-like particle and the dark photon, as well as to high-frequency gravitational waves, taking into account the decoherence and dephasing of the ion spins. Our results indicate that two-dimensional ion crystals and this new protocol provide a promising platform for probing previously unexplored parameter space in searches for light dark matter and high-frequency gravitational waves.

</details>


### [76] [The possible $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ molecular state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22359)
*Yin Huang,Dan Jiang,Feng Zhang,Bo Nan Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于单玻色子交换模型（one-boson-exchange model），系统研究了矢量介子 $K^{*}$ 与重子 $Σ^{*}$ 之间的相互作用，探讨了形成强子分子态（hadronic molecular states）的可能性。通过求解包含 $ρ$、$ω$、$π$ 介子交换的薛定谔方程，发现不同自旋宇称 $J^{P}$ 和同位旋通道下存在束缚态，并将实验观测到的 $N(2250)$ 和 $Δ(2200)$ 态解释为 $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ 分子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索矢量介子 $K^{*}$ 与重子 $Σ^{*}$ 之间是否存在足够强的吸引力以形成强子分子态（hadronic molecular states），从而为实验上观测到的某些奇特强子态提供理论解释。

Method: 在单玻色子交换模型（one-boson-exchange model）框架下，通过 $ρ$、$ω$ 和 $π$ 介子交换构建 $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ 相互作用势；采用高斯展开法（Gaussian expansion method）求解非相对论薛定谔方程（nonrelativistic Schrödinger equation），计算不同总角动量 $J^{P}$ 和同位旋（isospin）通道 $I=1/2$ 与 $I=3/2$ 中的结合能。

Result: $S$--$D$ 波混合的 $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ 分子态仅在 $I=3/2$、$J^{P}=1/2^{-}$ 通道中形成；$J^{P}=3/2^{-}$ 和 $J^{P}=5/2^{-}$ 的 $S$--$D$ 波混合态也存在束缚态解；$J^{P}=1/2^{+}$ 通道因相互作用主要为排斥而无束缚态；$I=1/2$ 通道中因同位旋空间的干涉相消（destructive interference）而无束缚态。实验观测的 $N(2250)$ 和 $Δ(2200)$ 可分别对应 $I=1/2,\ J^{P}=9/2^{-}$ 和 $I=3/2,\ J^{P}=7/2^{-}$ 的 $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ 分子态。

Conclusion: $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ 体系可在特定同位旋和自旋宇称通道中形成强子分子态，部分波混合、张量力（tensor forces）和自旋-轨道相互作用（spin–orbit interactions）共同主导高分波态的结合机制。该研究支持了 $N(2250)$ 和 $Δ(2200)$ 作为 $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ 分子态的实验解释。

Abstract: Within the framework of the one-boson-exchange model, we systematically investigate the interaction between the vector meson $K^{*}$ and the baryon $Σ^{*}$ with the aim of exploring the possibility of forming hadronic molecular states. The $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ interaction potential is constructed from $ρ$, $ω$, and $π$ meson exchanges, and the nonrelativistic Schrödinger equation is solved using the Gaussian expansion method. The binding energies are calculated for different total angular momenta $J^{P}$ and isospin channels $I=1/2$ and $I=3/2$. Our results show that $S$--$D$ wave mixed $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ molecular states with $J^{P}=1/2^{-}$ can be formed only in the $I=3/2$ channel, while no bound state appears in the $I=1/2$ channel due to destructive interference of the interaction potentials in isospin space. In addition, the $S$--$D$ wave mixed states with $J^{P}=3/2^{-}$ and $J^{P}=5/2^{-}$ are also found to support bound-state solutions. For higher partial-wave states, the binding mechanism is governed by the interplay of partial-wave mixing, tensor forces, and spin--orbit interactions. In particular, the $J^{P}=1/2^{+}$ channel does not support a bound state because the meson-exchange interaction is predominantly repulsive. Our analysis further supports the interpretation of the experimentally observed $N(2250)$ and $Δ(2200)$ states as $K^{*}Σ^{*}$ molecular states, corresponding to $I=1/2,\ J^{P}=9/2^{-}$ and $I=3/2,\ J^{P}=7/2^{-}$, respectively.

</details>


### [77] [The exact column texture: tree-level Yukawa universality in heterotic $Z_3 \times Z_3$ orbifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22403)
*Navid Ardakanian*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在 $T^6/(Z_3 \times Z_3)$ 杂化轨形（heterotic orbifold）上，领先阶树级汤川振幅（leading-order tree-level Yukawa amplitude）精确地具有列纹理（column texture）$Y_{\rm lead}(i,j) = c\,\varepsilon^{q_R[j]}$，并给出五条独立证据；超出领先阶的贡献才是非平庸 $O(1)$ 系数的唯一来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦论唯象学中，汤川矩阵（Yukawa matrix）的结构直接决定了标准模型中的夸克质量与混合角。已有研究表明弗罗盖特-尼尔森（Froggatt-Nielsen）机制可导出层级结构，但领先阶弦振幅是否精确具有列纹理、以及非平庸 $O(1)$ 系数的起源尚不明确。本文旨在从弦论第一原理出发，严格证明列纹理是领先阶的精确性质，并指出修正来源。

Method: 本文在 $T^6/(Z_3 \times Z_3)$ 杂化轨形上，基于世界瞬子（worldsheet instanton）在 $SU(3)$ 根格点（root lattice）上的几何、威尔逊线（Wilson line）的规范等同性质、$\Delta(54)$ 表示论、以及包含 534 个三线性超势耦合的弗罗盖特-尼尔森链计算，从五个独立角度给出证据。此外，通过在 Mini-Landscape 分类（77 个类 MSSM 模型）与 Parr-Vaudrevange-Wimmer 分类（3337 个 $Z_3 \times Z_3$ MSSM 模型）上的系统验证，排除了威尔逊线打破规范盲性的可能。

Result: 领先阶树级汤川振幅严格满足列纹理，其中几何 $O(1)$ 系数恰好为 $1$；所有三代生成（generation）因威尔逊线平凡而具有规范等同性；卡勒度规（Kähler metric）在 $\Delta(54)$ 表示论下是代际普适的；弗罗盖特-尼尔森链计算给出左循环汤川矩阵（left-circulant Yukawa matrices），其本征结构也是代际普适的。非平庸 $O(1)$ 系数只可能来自积出的重中介传播子、真空对位效应、多瞬子修正或圈修正等超出领先阶的贡献。

Conclusion: 弗罗盖特-尼尔森列纹理并非近似，而是领先阶弦振幅的精确性质。要解释超出沃尔芬斯坦层级（Wolfenstein hierarchy）的 CKM 混合角，必须依赖超出领先阶的贡献，这为后续在弦论框架下计算完整汤川矩阵指明了修正方向。

Abstract: On $T^6/(Z_3 \times Z_3)$ heterotic orbifolds where three quark generations arise from $Z_3$ fixed-point triplication, we prove that the leading-order tree-level Yukawa amplitude -- the three-point coupling among massless string states -- has an exact column texture: $Y_{\rm lead}(i,j) = c\,\varepsilon^{q_R[j]}$, with the $O(1)$ coefficient $c$ universal across all left-handed generations $i$. Five independent lines of evidence are given: (1) the worldsheet instanton geometry on the $SU(3)$ root lattice gives identical areas for all non-degenerate triangles, making the geometric $O(1)$ coefficient exactly $1$; (2) the generation direction necessarily has trivial Wilson line, rendering all three generations gauge-identical, as verified across all 77 MSSM-like models in the Mini-Landscape classification; (3) an extension to two-Wilson-line models, verified on the complete Parr-Vaudrevange-Wimmer classification of 3,337 $Z_3 \times Z_3$ MSSM models, confirms that no Wilson line configuration can break gauge blindness; (4) the Kähler metric is generation-universal by $Δ(54)$ representation theory; (5) the full Froggatt-Nielsen chain computation with 534 trilinear superpotential couplings and vacuum-aligned singlet VEVs produces left-circulant Yukawa matrices whose eigenstructure is generation-universal. The Froggatt-Nielsen column texture is therefore not an approximation but an exact property of the leading-order string amplitude. Non-trivial $O(1)$ coefficients, which are required for CKM mixing angles beyond the Wolfenstein hierarchy, must originate from beyond-leading-order contributions: integrated-out heavy messenger propagators (tree-level in the low-energy effective theory), vacuum-alignment effects, multi-instanton corrections, or loop corrections.

</details>


### [78] [Machine Learning for Multi-messenger Probes of New Physics and Cosmology: A Review and Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22462)

Conclusion: 跨领域交叉融合（cross-fertilizing approach）是提取基础物理学重大未解问题信息的关键路径；本文工作建立在前人多信使观测探索暗物质候选者的基础之上，聚焦机器学习在异构数据整合中的角色。

Abstract: The multi-messenger exploration of dark matter and physics beyond the Standard Model has emerged as a central direction in modern astro-particle physics, particularly following the discovery of gravitational waves. In this work, we present a comprehensive review and forward-looking perspective on machine-learning-enhanced multi-messenger approaches, combining information from gravitational waves, cosmic rays, gamma rays, neutrinos, and collider experiments. We summarize the current state of the field, discuss recent methodological developments, and outline a coherent research program aimed at integrating heterogeneous datasets within a unified inference framework. Our collaboration proposes here a plan for forthcoming analyses aiming at extracting information on the properties and interactions of dark matter, and finally on its genesis, combining multi-messenger astronomy techniques and inputs from laboratory physics. The main objectives planned in this line of research comprise: i) the multi-messenger analysis of new physics in cosmology, including mainly, but not only, several different models of dark matter; ii) the phenomenology of new physics signatures in ground-based cosmic rays experiments, with cross-correlation to the corresponding physical, astrophysical and cosmological observations; iii) the development of machine learning methods for data analysis in ground-based cosmic rays experiments, in light of the new physics signatures. We note that several groups have explored the use of multi-messenger observations, including gravitational waves, to probe alternative dark matter candidates. The present work builds on these developments by focusing on the role of machine learning in integrating heterogeneous datasets. We foresee that such a cross-fertilizing approach will represent the right path to extract information about the main questions left in fundamental physics.

### [79] [The potential of directional neutrino detection to observe neutrino spin oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22681)
*Konstantin A. Kouzakov,Fedor M. Lazarev,Alexander I. Studenikin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了入射中微子任意自旋-味态对低能中微子散射过程的影响，发现左右手螺旋性中微子态的叠加会导致反冲动量角分布出现方位角不对称，并通过电子、质子及40Ar、132Xe核上的弹性散射数值计算，展示了定向中微子探测在观测中微子自旋振荡方面的独特潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于作者此前发展的方法，研究任意自旋-味态（spin-flavor state）的入射中微子对低能中微子与探测器内不同粒子散射过程的影响。通过分析左右手螺旋性（helicity）中微子态的叠加效应，推导反冲动量角分布的方位角不对称性（azimuthal asymmetry），并对电子、质子、40Ar和132Xe核上的弹性散射进行数值计算。

Result: 左右手螺旋性中微子态的叠加会导致反冲动量角分布出现方位角不对称。针对电子、质子、40Ar及132Xe核的弹性散射数值计算均验证了该方位角不对称效应的存在。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，定向中微子探测（directional neutrino detection）在观测中微子自旋振荡方面具有独特的潜力，该效应可通过低能弹性散射的方位角不对称特征被实验检验。

Abstract: A nonzero neutrino magnetic moment arises already in the minimally extended Standard Model with right-handed massive Dirac neutrinos. The well-known consequence of the neutrino magnetic moment is the phenomenon of neutrino spin oscillations in a magnetic field. It can manifest itself not only as a lack in the flux of active cosmic neutrinos arriving on Earth but also as characteristic features in low-energy neutrino elastic scattering processes. Following our approach developed earlier, in this work we study the influence of arbitrary spin-flavor state of incoming neutrino on low-energy neutrino scattering off different particles in a detector. We demonstrate that superposition of left- and right-handed helicity neutrino states gives rise to an azimuthal asymmetry in the angular distribution of the recoil momenta. We present numerical calculations for elastic neutrino scattering on electrons, protons and 40Ar and 132Xe nuclei, demonstrating the azimuthal-asymmetry effect. Our results indicate the unique potential of directional neutrino detection to observe the neutrino spin oscillations.

### [80] [Extended Haldane Model in The Dice Lattice: Multiple Flat-Band-Induced topological Transitions Revealed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22131)
*Othmane Benhaida,Lalla Btissam Drissi,El Hassan Saidi*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本研究将Haldane模型引入dice晶格，通过改变次近邻位点之间的通量打破晶格的反演对称性和时间反演对称性。在临界通量φ^c=π/6和5π/6处发现了点电荷粒子对称性，并推导出准能量的解析表达式。通过贝里曲率、轨道磁矩和陈数的拓扑分析，揭示了拓扑相变及通量依赖的拓扑不变量变化，并观察到量子化的反常霍尔电导平台和未量子化的倾斜平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索将Haldane模型引入dice晶格的可行性，通过调节次近邻通量来打破对称性，以实现可控的拓扑相变和量子输运优化，为可重构的低耗散拓扑器件提供理论基础。

Method: 改变dice晶格中次近邻位点之间的通量（flux）以打破反演对称性（inversion symmetry）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）；推导准能量（quasi-energy）的解析表达式；计算贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment）；进行拓扑分析以确定不同通量区域的陈数（Chern number）变化。

Result: 在φ^c=π/6和5π/6处存在点电荷粒子对称性，并在这些临界点发生能隙闭合与拓扑相变。当φ^c = φ^a时，陈数在φ^c∈[0, π/6[区域为(2, -2, 0)，在]5π/6, π]区域为(0, 2, -2)；当φ^c ≠ φ^a时，拓扑不变量变为(-1, -1)和(1, 1)。反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）表现出量为2σ₀的量子化平台以及从1.50σ₀变化至1.25σ₀的未量子化倾斜平台。

Conclusion: 通过控制通量可以工程化地实现拓扑相变并优化dice晶格中的量子输运，为构建具有低耗散和鲁棒量子输运特性的可重构拓扑器件提供了有前景的方案。

Abstract: In this study, we examine the introduction of the Haldane model into the dice lattice by altering the flow between the next-nearest-neighbour sites. This breaks the lattice's inversion and time-reversal symmetries. We demonstrate the presence of point-charge particle symmetries at $φ^c=π/6$ and $5π/6$ and derive the analytical expression for quasi-energies. We demonstrate that a gap closure occurs at these critical points, inducing a topological transition. This is confirmed by calculating the Berry curvature and orbital magnetic moment. A topological analysis shows that the Chern numbers of the valence band $(ν=0)$, the flat band $(ν=1)$ and the conduction band $(ν=2)$ depend strongly on the relationship between the fluxes $φ^a $ and $φ^c$. When $φ^c = φ^a$, the Chern numbers are $(C_0, C_1, C_2) = (2, -2, 0)$ in the region $φ^c \in [0, π/6[$, and (0, 2, -2) in the region $φ^c\in ]5π/6, π]$. Conversely, when $φ^c \neq φ^a$, the topological invariants become $ (C_1, C_2) = (-1, -1)$ for $φ^c \in [0, π/6[$, and $(C_0, C_1, )= (1, 1)$ for $φ^c\in ]5π/6, π]$. These variations reflect topological phase transitions at the critical points $φ^c=π/6$ and $5π/6$, affecting all of the system's bands. Furthermore, the anomalous Hall conductivity exhibits a quantized plateau of 2$σ_{0}$, as well as an unquantized tilted plateau evolving from 1.50$σ_{0}$ to 1.25$σ_{0}$ at the same transition points. Controlling the flux allows topological transitions to be engineered and quantum transport in the dice lattice to be optimised, offering promising prospects for reconfigurable topological devices with low dissipation and robust quantum transport.

### [81] [Dynamically Corrected Bethe-Salpeter Equation Solver for Self-consistent $GW$ Reference on the Matsubara Frequency Axis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22187)
*Ming Wen,Gaurav Harsha,Dominika Zgid*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于自洽 $GW$ 参考的 Bethe-Salpeter 方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation, BSE）求解器（BSE@sc$GW$），并通过等离子体激元-极点模型引入动力学修正，从而在保持计算效率的同时显著提升了激发能精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的一步 $GW$ 方法对初始平均场（mean-field）参考较为敏感，且静态 Casida 框架忽略了动力学屏蔽（dynamic screening）效应，限制了激发能计算的精度与鲁棒性。

Method: 采用在 Matsubara 频率轴上评估的自洽 $GW$（self-consistent $GW$, sc$GW$）作为起点，以提供稳健的准粒子描述；随后通过等离子体激元-极点模型（plasmon-pole model）对静态 Casida 公式施加动力学修正，将问题仍保持为有效本征值问题的形式。

Result: 动力学修正后的 BSE@sc$GW$ 方法在小分子的单重态（singlet）和三重态（triplet）激发能计算上，与高水平波函数基准（high-level wavefunction-based benchmarks）结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 动态 BSE@sc$GW$ 的精度源于两方面——充分收敛的单粒子参考以及频率依赖屏蔽效应（frequency-dependent screening effects）的纳入，二者结合使得该方法兼具准确性与计算效率。

Abstract: We present a Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE) solver based on a self-consistent $GW$ reference evaluated on the Matsubara frequency axis, referred to as BSE@sc$GW$. The self-consistent $GW$ starting point provides a robust quasiparticle description and reduces sensitivity to the initial mean-field reference compared to one-shot $GW$-based approaches. We further introduce a dynamical correction to the static Casida formulation via a plasmon-pole model. This scheme incorporates simple dynamical screening effects while retaining the efficiency of an effective eigenvalue problem. The resulting dynamically corrected BSE@sc$GW$ yields excitation energies in close agreement with high-level wavefunction-based benchmarks for both singlet and triplet excitations of small molecules. Overall, the accuracy of the dynamic BSE@sc$GW$ approach arises from the combination of a well-converged single-particle reference and the inclusion of frequency-dependent screening effects.

### [82] [Pressure-Temperature Phase Diagram and $λ$-Transition in Liquid Sulfur](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22696)
*Sonia Salomoni,Frédéric Datchi,A. Marco Saitta,Arthur France-Lanord*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potential）驱动的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，揭示了硫在λ相变（λ-transition）中的聚合机制及其在低压至中压范围内的相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硫的λ相变是一种温度诱导的聚合反应，但其微观机制尚不清楚；现有实验虽观测到热容尖峰等特征，但缺乏原子尺度的相变图像。

Method: 采用机器学习原子间势驱动的分子动力学模拟，在低压至中压范围内系统研究硫的λ相变过程，分析升温轨迹中分子结构的变化。

Result: 模拟再现了热容急剧上升和转变温度对加热速率的强烈依赖等实验特征；发现非S₈环分子充当反应中心触发聚合；聚合温度随压力升高略有下降，最终与熔化线在临界点汇合；超过临界点后，聚合从晶体相直接发生；升温过程中依次形成非S₈环、开链和保留晶体特征的长链聚合物，最终熔化导致无序化。

Conclusion: 聚合在熔化之前就已启动；研究结果提供了硫λ相变在整个相图中的微观图像。

Abstract: Using molecular dynamics simulations driven by a machine-learned interatomic potential, we investigate at low to intermediate pressures the $λ$-transition of sulfur, a temperature-induced polymerization. At ambient pressure, we capture the melting of crystalline cyclo-octasulfur into a liquid of molecular rings. Within this liquid, the concentration of non-S$_8$ rings increases with temperature; we show that these molecules act as reactive centers, which eventually trigger polymerization. We reproduce key experimental signatures of the $λ$-transition, including the sharp increase in heat capacity and the pronounced dependence of the transition temperature on the heating rate. Building on this, we reconstruct a phase diagram of polymerization up to intermediate pressures. Our results reveal a moderate decrease of the polymerization temperature with pressure, culminating with its merging with the melting line at a critical point. Beyond this point, we provide direct evidence of polymerization emerging from the crystalline phase. By analyzing temperature-ramp trajectories, we observe the formation of non-S$_8$ rings, open chains, and extended polymeric structures which retain features of the crystalline arrangement; further heating the system leads to disorder taking over through melting. Polymerization is therefore initiated slightly before melting. Altogether, our findings provide a microscopic picture of the $λ$-transition throughout the sulfur phase diagram.

### [83] [Tetrahedral $L$-operators, tensor Schur polynomials and $q$-deformed loop elementary symmetric functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22141)
*Shinsuke Iwao,Kohei Motegi,Ryo Ohkawa*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究基于四面体L-算子的三维配分函数，分别在q=0和一般q两种情形下分析其结构，并将其与Schur多项式、洗牌公式、Gustafson-Milne恒等式等建立联系，同时应用于多物种完全不对称简单排斥过程的稳态等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在深入分析由Bazhanov-Sergeev和Kuniba-Maruyama-Okado引入的四面体L-算子（tetrahedral L-operator）所构造的三维配分函数（three-dimensional partition functions），探索其代数结构与组合性质，并建立与已知数学恒等式及统计物理模型的联系。

Method: 首先针对q=0情形，在作者前期工作基础上结合Zamolodchikov-Faddeev代数（Zamolodchikov-Faddeev algebra）进一步分析；引入可用张量Schur多项式（tensor Schur polynomials）表达的配分函数类，并通过差商算子（divided difference operators）构造模仿Schbert多项式（Schubert polynomials）的Laurent多项式族。

Result: 导出了Schur多项式的洗牌公式（shuffle formula），该公式在几何上对应Joźefiak-Pragacz-Lascoux的推出公式（pushforward formula）；推导并统一了Gustafson-Milne恒等式与Fehér–Némehi–Rimányi恒等式；将结果应用于多物种完全不对称简单排斥过程（multispecies totally asymmetric simple exclusion process）的稳态。对于一般q情形，确定了若干类配分函数作为初等对称函数（elementary symmetric functions）形变的具体形式，其中之一可视为q-变形圈初等对称函数（q-deformed loop elementary symmetric functions）的推广。

Conclusion: 四面体L-算子构造的三维配分函数在q=0与一般q两种情形下均展现出丰富的代数与组合结构，并与Schur多项式、多种已知恒等式以及排斥过程稳态等主题产生深刻联系，为三维可积系统与代数组合学的交叉提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study three-dimensional partition functions constructed from the tetrahedral $L$-operator introduced and studied by Bazhanov-Sergeev and Kuniba-Maruyama-Okado. First, we explore the $q=0$ case, extending the authors' previous results and giving applications by a further analysis on the Zamolodchikov-Faddeev algebra. We introduce a class of partition functions which can be expressed as the tensor Schur polynomials, a class of products of Schur polynomials. As an application, we derive the shuffle formula for the Schur polynomials which is geometrically the pushforward formula by Joźefiak-Pragacz-Lascoux. We also give a derivation and a unification of the Gustafson-Milne and Feh{é}r--N{é}methi--Rim{á}nyi identities, and introduce a family of Laurent polynomials using divided difference operators which imitates the Schubert polynomials from the perspective of our study. We also present an application to the steady state of the multispecies totally asymmetric simple exclusion process. Second, we investigate several classes of partition functions for the generic $q$ case, and determine the explicit forms as deformations of the elementary symmetric functions. One of them can be regarded as (an extension of) a $q$-deformed loop elementary symmetric functions.

</details>


### [84] [A direct derivation of an effective Hamiltonian in non-relativistic quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22316)
*Yasumichi Matsuzawa*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在不依赖标度极限（scaling limit）的前提下，直接推导了非相对论量子电动力学（non-relativistic quantum electrodynamics）中的Arai有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），并将结果推广至更广泛的势能类别，包括Rollnik类势和约束势（如谐振子势）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有推导Arai有效哈密顿量的方法通常依赖于标度极限（scaling limit），适用范围受限。本文旨在提供一种不依赖标度极限的直接推导路径，并将其适用性扩展至更广泛的势能类别。

Method: 采用直接推导（direct derivation）方法，摆脱了标度极限的约束，从而在更一般的数学框架下处理非相对论量子电动力学中的有效哈密顿量问题。

Result: 成功推导出Arai有效哈密顿量，且该结果适用于Rollnik类势（Rollnik class）以及约束势（confining potentials），例如谐振子势（harmonic potential）。

Conclusion: 该推导方法不依赖标度极限，能够覆盖更广的势能类别，为非相对论量子电动力学中有效哈密顿量的理论研究提供了更通用的分析工具。

Abstract: We present a direct derivation of Arai's effective Hamiltonian in non-relativistic quantum electrodynamics without relying on the scaling limit. Our result applies to a broader class of potentials, including the Rollnik class and confining potentials such as the harmonic potential.

</details>


### [85] [Affine Supertrusses and Superbraces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22381)
*Andrew James Bruce*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文定义了仿射超桁架（affine supertruss）作为从幺结合超交换超代数范畴到桁架范畴的可表示函子，引入“余桁架”（cotruss）新概念，并证明仿射超桁架可构造仿射超括号（affine superbrace），从而将Rump括号推广到超数学领域，最后提出集合论Yang–Baxter方程到仿射超概形（affine superscheme）设定的推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Brzeziński桁架（truss）是“环状”代数结构，其中加法被阿贝尔堆（abelian heap）运算取代，二元乘法满足三元积的自然分配律。本文旨在探讨如何定义桁架的（$\mathbb{Z}_2$-分次）超版本（super-version）。

Method: 受代数超群（algebraic supergroup）理论的启发，将仿射超桁架定义为从幺结合超交换超代数（unital associative supercommutative superalgebra）范畴到桁架范畴的可表示函子（representable functor）。表示超代数配备了一种全新的“余桁架”（cotruss）结构。

Result: 证明了从仿射超桁架可以构造出仿射超括号（affine superbrace），从而将Rump括号（Rump's braces）推广到超数学（supermathematics）领域。

Conclusion: 作为这些构造的应用，本文提出了集合论Yang–Baxter方程（set-theoretic Yang–Baxter equation）到仿射超概形（affine superscheme）设定的推广。

Abstract: Brzeziński's trusses are ``ring-like'' algebraic structures in which the addition is replaced with an abelian heap operation and the binary product satisfies a natural distributivity rule of the ternary product. The question of how to define ($\mathbb{Z}_2$-graded) super-versions of trusses is addressed in this note. Taking our cue from the theory of algebraic supergroups, we define an affine supertruss as a representable functor from the category of unital associative supercommutative superalgebras to the category of trusses. The representing superalgebras are equipped with a `cotruss' structure--a new concept in itself. We show that from an affine supertruss one can construct an affine superbrace, and so generalise Rump's braces to supermathematics. As an application of these constructions, we propose a generalisation of the set-theoretic Yang--Baxter equation to the setting of affine superschemes.

</details>


### [86] [Two-layer sharply stratified Euler fluids in three dimensions: a Hamiltonian setting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22622)
*R. Camassa,G. Falqui,G. Ortenzi,M. Pedroni,E. Sforza*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从哈密顿（Hamiltonian）视角研究三维两层不可压缩欧拉流体，通过哈密顿约化过程导出有效二维模型的自然哈密顿结构，并展示了弱非线性近似下的KBK-B模型与KP方程之间的结构联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为三维两层不可压缩欧拉流体建立系统的哈密顿描述，并探索其约化后有效二维模型（如KBK-B模型和KP方程）之间的哈密顿结构关系。

Method: 从三维泊松结构（Poisson structure）出发，通过哈密顿约化（Hamiltonian reduction）过程得到由场变量界面值描述的有效二维模型的自然哈密顿结构；对KBK-B模型施以狄拉克型约化（Dirac-type reduction）过程，得到KP方程作为2+1维模型的自然哈密顿结构。

Result: 在弱非线性近似下，该约化过程导出了具有“临界”参数的二维Kaup-Broer-Kupershmidt Boussinesq (KBK-B)模型；讨论了弱依赖于一个水平方向的模型，其单向化（unidirectionalization）得到著名的Kadomtsev-Petviashvili (KP)方程。

Conclusion: 通过哈密顿约化和狄拉克型约化过程，建立了KBK-B模型与KP方程之间的哈密顿结构联系，为三维两层欧拉流体的有效二维描述提供了系统化的哈密顿框架。

Abstract: Three-dimensional two-layer incompressible Euler fluids are studied from a Hamiltonian perspective. A natural Hamiltonian structure for the effective 2D model described by the interface-value of the field variables is obtained by means of a Hamiltonian reduction process from the 3D Poisson structure. The problem of expressing the fluid's energy in terms of the reduced variables is considered, and it is shown that in the weakly non linear approximation our procedure gives rise to a so-called 2D Kaup-Broer-Kupershmidt Boussinesq (KBK-B) model with ``critical" parameters. A model weakly dependent on one of the two horizontal directions is also discussed, whose unidirectionalization turns out to be the well-known Kadomtsev-Petviashvili (KP) equation. A Dirac-type reduction process of the Hamiltonian structure of the KBK-B model yields a natural Hamiltonian structure for KP qua 2+1-dimensional model.

</details>

### [87] [Harnessing Plasmonic Heating For Switching In Antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22148)
*H. Y. Yuan,Yizheng Wu,Olena Gomonay*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用等离激元加热（plasmonic heating）在无磁场和电流辅助下，可逆切换反铁磁（AFM）薄膜中两个垂直取向的磁畴的方法，所需开关能量低至约1 nJ，比电流驱动的AFM开关低三到六个数量级。机制源于热致应变场通过磁弹效应（magnetoelastic effect）耦合与操控磁取向，且可通过改变光波偏振选择性地激发纵向和横向等离激元模式来控制应变场方向，实现AFM矢量的可逆切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热能浪费是绿色信息技术发展的瓶颈，电子和自旋电子器件中加热效应通常被视为问题。本文采取替代思路，旨在证明纳米尺度可控加热实际上有益于信息处理，探索利用热效应实现超低能耗的磁操控方案。

Method: 研究一种由金属方框和反铁磁（AFM）薄膜构成的混合纳米结构。通过改变入射光波偏振，选择性地激发纵向和横向等离激元模式（plasmon modes），在金属方框内产生可控的热致应变场（thermal-induced strain fields），进而通过磁弹效应（magnetoelastic effect）耦合与操控AFM磁取向。

Result: 成功实现了两个垂直取向的AFM磁畴的可逆切换，无需外加磁场和电流。所需切换能量约为1 nJ，比电流驱动的AFM开关低三到六个数量级。

Conclusion: 该发现为利用光学手段以超低能耗操控磁性提供了巨大机遇，有望进一步促进光子学（photonics）、声学（acoustics）和自旋电子学（spintronics）的交叉研究。

Abstract: Heat waste is a bottleneck in the development of green information technologies and much effort has been devoted to suppress the heating effect in both electronic and spintronic devices. Here we take an alternative approach and show that controllable heating at the nanoscale can actually benefit information processing. In particular, we study a hybrid nanostructure consisting of a metallic square frame and an antiferromagnetic (AFM) thin film and show that the plasmonic heating can reversibly switch two perpendicularly-oriented AFM domains without the assistance of magnetic fields and electric currents. The required switching energy is at the order 1 nJ, three to six orders of magnitude lower than the current-driven AFM switching. The physical mechanism arises from the thermal-induced strain fields inside the frame, which couple to and manipulate the magnetic orientation via magnetoelastic effect. The strain field direction can be well controlled by selectively exciting the longitudinal and transverse plasmon modes by varying the polarization of the waves, which readily allows for a reversible switching of the AFM vector. Our findings provide tremendous opportunities for optically manipulating the magnetism with ultralow energy consumption and may further promote the interdisciplinary study of photonics, acoustics and spintronics.

</details>


### [88] [Microscopic Modeling of Surface Roughness Scattering in Inversion Layers of MOSFETs Based on Ando's Linear Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22155)
*Nobuyuki Sano*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 基于Ando线性模型，提出了一个体MOSFET反型层中表面粗糙度（surface roughness, SR）散射的微观模型。通过引入粗糙度位置的概率密度函数并采用格林函数方法推导散射率，发现该散射率本质上是非局域的，且在强有效场和低电子能量区域与费米黄金定则结果存在显著偏差，传统模型倾向于低估SR限制的迁移率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表面粗糙度散射模型在粗糙度参数上与实验存在不一致，且传统基于费米黄金定则（Fermi's golden rule）的处理方式可能无法准确描述散射行为，尤其是在强有效场和低电子能量条件下。

Method: 基于Ando线性模型，在半导体/介质界面处考虑静电势和波函数空间导数不连续性导致的粗糙度位置随机性，在每个原子位点引入粗糙度位置的概率密度函数（probability density）。采用格林函数方案（Green's function scheme）推导表面粗糙度散射率。

Result: 所提模型的粗糙度参数与实验一致，消除理论与实验的差异。散射率在子带指标（subband indices）和位置上本质上是非局域的（nonlocal, 非对角化）。在强有效场和低电子能量区域，自洽散射率（self-consistent scattering rate）与费米黄金定则结果存在显著偏差，传统模型倾向于预测更小的SR限制迁移率（SR-limited mobility）。

Conclusion: 提出的微观表面粗糙度散射模型能更好拟合实验参数，且揭示了传统费米黄金定则方法在强场和低能区的局限性，为更准确评估MOSFET中表面粗糙度散射对迁移率的影响提供了理论框架。

Abstract: A microscopic model of surface roughness (SR) scattering in inversion layers of bulk-MOSFETs based on Ando's linear model is proposed. Taking into account the stochastic nature of roughness position induced by discontinuity of the spatial derivatives of electrostatic potential and wave-function at the semiconductor/dielectric interface, a probability density of roughness position is introduced at each atomic site. The roughness parameters in the proposed model are consistent with those from experiments, and thus, there is no discrepancy between theory and experiment. The SR scattering rate is then derived by using the Green's function scheme, and we find that the scattering rate is intrinsically nonlocal (nondiagonal) with respect to subband indices and position. In addition, the self-consistent scattering rate greatly deviates from those obtained by Fermi's golden rule in the regimes of strong effective fields and low electron energies. As a result, the conventional model tends to predict smaller SR-limited mobility.

</details>


### [89] [Electric-Field Control of Quantum Tunneling Regimes in Focused He-Ion-Beam-Irradiated Oxide Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22346)
*Yu Chen,Maria D'Antuono,Robin Hutt,Cesar Magen,Edward Goldobin,Dieter Koelle,Reinhold Kleiner,Marco Salluzzo,Daniela Stornaiuolo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用氦聚焦离子束（He FIB）辐照技术在氧化物界面二维电子系统（2DES）中制备隧道场效应晶体管，通过辐照诱导的局域晶格形变形成纳米尺度势垒，并实现从热电子发射到直接隧穿和Fowler-Nordheim隧穿等多种输运机制的单器件调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂氧化物界面二维电子系统中实现可调控的纳米尺度势垒和隧道器件，以探索门电压可调的量子隧穿现象，并发展一种新的纳米功能工程方法。

Method: 采用氦聚焦离子束（helium focused ion beam）辐照氧化物界面处的二维电子系统（two-dimensional electron system, 2DES），并结合高分辨扫描透射电子显微镜（scanning transmission electron microscopy, STEM）和应变映射（strain mapping）表征局域晶格形变；通过低温静电背栅（electrostatic backgating）连续调控势垒轮廓。

Result: 实验表明，辐照区域形成局域化晶格形变，构成纳米尺度势垒（nanoscale potential barriers）；该势垒轮廓可通过低温静电背栅连续调控，且不劣化2DES电极的电子性能。单个器件中实现了热电子发射（thermionic emission）、直接隧穿（direct tunneling）和Fowler-Nordheim隧穿（Fowler-Nordheim tunneling）的可控访问。

Conclusion: 氦聚焦离子束辐照技术是一种对复杂氧化物界面进行纳米尺度功能工程（nanoscale functional engineering）的有效工具，为探索门电压可调的量子隧穿现象提供了平台。

Abstract: Helium focused ion beam irradiation enables the fabrication of tunnel field-effect transistors based on two-dimensional electron systems (2DESs) at an oxide interface.High resolution scanning transmission electron microscopy and strain mapping reveal localized lattice deformation confined to the irradiated regions, which act as nanoscale potential barriers. The barrier profile can be continuously tuned by electrostatic backgating at low temperature without degrading the electronic properties of the 2DES electrodes. Transport measurements demonstrate controlled access to thermionic emission, direct tunneling, and Fowler-Nordheim tunneling within a single device architecture. These results establish He FIB irradiation as a powerful tool for nanoscale functional engineering of complex-oxide interfaces and provide a platform for exploring gate-tunable quantum tunneling phenomena.

### [90] [Valley enhanced Rabi frequency in n-type planar Silicon-MOS quantum dot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22547)
*Xunyao Luo,Xander Peetroons,Tsung-Yeh Yang,Ruben M. Otxoa,Normann Mertig,Sofie Beyne,Julien Jussot,Yosuke Shimura,Clement Godfrin,Bart Raes,Roy Li,Roger Loo,Sylvain Baudot,Stefan Kubicek,Shuchi Kaushik,Danny Wan,Kristiaan De Greve,Takuma Kuno,Takeru Utsugi,Noriyuki Lee,Itaru Yanagi,Toshiyuki Mine,Satoshi Muraoka,Hideo Arimoto,Shinichi Saito,Digh Hisamoto,Ryuta Tsuchiya,Hiroyuki Mizuno,Charles Smith,Andrew Ramsay*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文报道了在平面硅金属-氧化物-半导体（Si-MOS）量子点中单个电子的电子自旋共振（ESR）实验，特别是在谷能级反交叉附近的现象。通过观测由磁自旋翻转和电谷翻转跃迁混合引起的一个和两个光子共振，重构了包含两个谷态和两个自旋态的四态系统能级图。在反交叉点附近观察到拉比频率的增强，归因于由谷间自旋耦合激活的上能级电偶极跃迁。通过测量g因子各向异性、平均g因子和谷间自旋耦合，表征了导致增强的自旋-谷耦合。谷间自旋耦合受磁场方向强烈调制，在面外磁场中最强，与面内自旋-谷场一致。该强电偶极自旋共振（EDSR）效应原则上可用于小规模器件中的快速全电自旋控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索平面硅量子点中单个电子的自旋行为，特别是在谷能级反交叉附近的自旋-谷耦合机制，为理解硅基量子点中的自旋操控提供基础。

Method: 通过电子自旋共振（ESR）谱学测量单个电子在Si-MOS量子点中的共振信号，观测一个和两个光子共振跃迁，利用磁自旋翻转与电谷翻转的混合效应重构四态（两个谷态、两个自旋态）能级图。测量g因子差异各向异性、平均g因子以及面内和面外磁场下的谷间自旋耦合。

Result: 在谷能级反交叉附近观测到拉比频率增强，归因于谷间自旋耦合激活的上能级电偶极跃迁。谷间自旋耦合受磁场方向强烈调制，在面外磁场中耦合最强，与面内自旋-谷场（in-plane spin-valley field）一致。

Conclusion: 该强电偶极自旋共振（EDSR）效应原则上可用于小规模器件中实现快速全电自旋控制（all-electrical spin control）。

Abstract: Electron spin resonance spectroscopy (ESR) of a single electron in planar Si-MOS quantum dot is reported in the vicinity of a valley level anti-crossing. A number of one and two-photon resonances are observed due to mixing of magnetic spin-flip and electric valley-flip transitions. This allows the reconstruction of the energy-level diagram of a four state system with two valley and two spin states. Near the anti-crossing, an enhancement of the Rabi frequency is observed. This is attributed to an electric-dipole transition activated by admixing of the upper energy level due to inter-valley spin coupling. The electric-dipole transition may be driven via capacitive coupling between the ESR antenna, and the confinement gate. To characterize spin-valley coupling responsible for the enhancement, we measure the anisotropy of the g-factor difference between the two valley states, the mean g-factor and the inter-valley spin coupling for both in and out-of-plane magnetic fields. The inter-valley spin coupling is strongly modulated by the direction of the B-field, and is strongest for out-of-plane B-field, consistent with an in-plane spin-valley field. In principle, this strong Electric dipole spin resonance (EDSR) effect could be utilized for fast all-electrical spin control in small-scale devices.

</details>


### [91] [Corner Majorana states in semi-Dirac](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22553)
*M. García Olmos,Y. Baba,R. A. Molina,M. Amado*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种理论框架，在二维半狄拉克（semi-Dirac）体系的边缘态中利用邻近效应实现马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states），无需依赖纳米结构、涡旋或高阶拓扑，仅通过 Rashba 自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）与塞曼场（Zeeman field）的协同作用，即可在每一边缘独立驱动一维拓扑超导相变，最终在条带四角产生四个零能模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维体系中的邻近诱导超导性（proximity-induced superconductivity）为在原本非超导的系统中构建拓扑超导相（topological superconducting phases）提供了关键途径；这类拓扑超导相因包含零能模（马约拉纳束缚态）而兼具基础物理与技术应用价值。现有方案常依赖刻意的纳米结构、涡旋或高阶拓扑，本研究旨在探索一种更自然的二维平台以实现马约拉纳模（Majorana modes）。

Method: 基于二维半狄拉克体系——一种具有各向异性能带结构的系统——利用其在特定条件下沿特定边缘传播的非手性边缘态（non-chiral edge states）形成分离的一维通道；通过引入 Rashba 自旋-轨道耦合与塞曼场，结合 s 波超导体的邻近效应（proximity effect），在边缘态之间诱导出有效的 p 波配对（p-wave pairing）；在有限几何中，每条边缘可独立发生拓扑相变（topological phase transition），进入一维拓扑超导态；低能有效模型可由耦合的 Kitaev 链（coupled Kitaev chains）描述。

Result: 在有限几何（例如条带结构）中，每条边缘可在 Rashba 自旋-轨道耦合与塞曼场的调控下独立经历拓扑相变，转变为一维拓扑超导体；该过程在条带的四个角点处产生四个零能马约拉纳模。低能下的耦合 Kitaev 链描述清晰揭示了这些角马约拉纳模（corner Majorana modes）的起源、鲁棒性与可调性。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了半狄拉克材料作为在二维体系中实现马约拉纳模的自然平台，无需依赖工程化纳米结构、涡旋或晶体高阶拓扑（crystalline higher-order topology），从而为非手性边缘态诱导拓扑超导提供了一条新路径。

Abstract: Proximity-induced superconductivity in low-dimensional systems offers a powerful pathway to engineer topological superconducting phases in, otherwise, non-superconducting systems. These exotic phases are of fundamental and technological interest due to the presence of robust zero-energy modes, the Majorana bound states. In this work, we propose a theoretical framework to realize Majorana bound states from the edge states of a two-dimensional semi-Dirac system. This anisotropic system, under specific conditions, can host non-chiral edge states that propagate only along particular edges, effectively forming separated one-dimensional channels. We show that the interplay between Rashba spin-orbit coupling and a Zeeman field on this setup provides the right conditions to get an effective p-wave pairing between the edge states by proximity with a s-wave superconductor. In finite geometries, each edge can independently undergo a topological phase transition into a one-dimensional topological superconductor and give rise to four zero-energy modes localized at the strip corners. At low energies, the edge states subspace admits a description in terms of coupled Kitaev chains, providing a clear picture of the origin, robustness, and tunability of the corner Majorana modes. Our results establish semi-Dirac materials as a natural platform for realizing Majorana modes in two dimensions without relying on engineered nanostructures, vortices, or crystalline higher-order topology.

</details>


### [92] [Pulse Shaping to Mitigate the Impact of Device Imperfections in Field-Free Switching Using Combined Spin-Orbit and Spin-Transfer Torques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22574)
*Kuldeep Ray,Jérémie Vigier,Sylvain Martin,Chloé Bouard,Nicolas Lefoulon,Marc Drouard,Gilles Gaudin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过实验和宏自旋模型（macrospin model）研究自旋轨道矩（SOT）与自旋转移矩（STT）联合切换在顶置钉扎（top-pinned）SOT-MRAM器件中的写入错误率（WER），发现STT导致的反跳（backhopping）和切换不对称性，并提出基于STT脉冲整形的缓解策略以降低WER并提高鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SOT与STT联合切换是实现无外磁场翻转（field-free switching）的实用方案，这是SOT-MRAM工业化部署的前提；但联合方案在顶置钉扎结构中易因STT引发反跳等可靠性问题。现有研究缺乏对非STT优化器件中联合切换写入错误率的系统分析。

Method: 实验测量顶置钉扎SOT-MRAM器件的写入错误率（WER）；采用耦合两套Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert（LLG）方程的宏自旋模型，分别描述自由层（free layer）和参考层（reference layer）的磁化动力学。

Result: 实验观测到STT诱导的反跳现象以及AP→P与P→AP切换之间显著的不对称性；宏自旋模型定性再现了该不对称性，并揭示除已知的反跳区域外还存在一个中间失确定性（loss-of-determinism）区间。实验证明STT脉冲整形可有效降低WER并增强器件存在缺陷时的切换鲁棒性。

Conclusion: STT脉冲整形是一种可行的缓解策略，能够在保持无外磁场翻转能力的同时抑制STT引发的反跳和写入错误，提升SOT-MRAM的工业可靠性。

Abstract: Combining spin-orbit (SOT) and spin-transfer torques (STT) provides a practical approach for field-free switching in spin-orbit torque magnetic random-access memory (SOT-MRAM), a prerequisite for industrial deployment, but can compromise reliability through phenomena such as backhopping, especially in top-pinned stacks commonly used for SOT-MRAM. We investigate the write error rate (WER) of combined SOT + STT switching in top-pinned devices that are not optimized for STT switching. Experiments reveal clear indications of STT-induced backhopping and a pronounced field-free SOT switching asymmetry between AP-to-P and P-to-AP transitions. Our macrospin model, using two coupled Landau Lifshitz Gilbert equations for the free and the reference layers, qualitatively reproduces this asymmetry and reveals an intermediate loss-of-determinism regime in addition to the well-known backhopping region. Based on these simulations, we propose mitigation strategies and experimentally demonstrate that STT pulse shaping reduces WER and improves switching robustness in the presence of device imperfections.

</details>


### [93] [Strain engineering of Andreev spin qubits in Germanium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22650)
*Vittorio Coppini,Patrick Del Vecchio,Antonio L. R. Manesco,Anton Akhmerov,Valla Fatemi,Bernard van Heck,Stefano Bosco*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出压缩应变（compressive strain）是抑制锗（germanium）约瑟夫森结中自旋劈裂（spin-splitting）的关键机制，并建议采用无应变或拉伸应变（tensile-strained）异质结构，可将自旋劈裂提升至GHz范围，实现全电控量子门，从而为锗基安德烈夫自旋量子比特（Andreev spin qubit）的构建提供应变工程（strain engineering）这一核心设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面锗异质结构因与超导体兼容、材料无序度低、制备约束宽松，且具有低核自旋密度和强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit interaction），被认为是混合量子器件和相干自旋物理的理想平台。然而，近期微波光谱实验未能分辨出锗约瑟夫森结中束缚态的自旋劈裂，而这正是定义和操控安德烈夫自旋量子比特（Andreev spin qubit）的前提条件，因此亟需阐明抑制自旋劈裂的机制并给出改进方案。

Method: 本文通过理论分析指出压缩应变是抑制自旋劈裂的关键机制，并提出与现有先进生长技术完全兼容的无应变和拉伸应变异质结构。采用弹道约瑟夫森结（ballistic Josephson junction）的数值模拟，定量预测了不同应变条件下的自旋劈裂大小。

Result: 数值模拟结果表明，采用无应变或拉伸应变结构可将自旋劈裂提升至GHz范围，比压缩应变情形高出两个数量级以上，并可在百纳秒（hundred nanoseconds）时间尺度上实现全电控量子门（all-electric quantum gates）。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了应变工程（strain engineering）作为实现锗基器件中安德烈夫自旋量子比特的核心设计原则。

Abstract: Planar germanium heterostructures are promising hosts for hybrid quantum devices due to their compatibility with superconductors, low material disorder, and relaxed fabrication constraints. Also, the potentially low density of nuclear spins and strong spin-orbit interaction make germanium attractive for coherent spin physics. However, recent microwave spectroscopy experiments were unable to resolve a spin-splitting of bound states in germanium Josephson junctions, the prerequisite for defining and controlling Andreev spin qubits. Here, we argue that compressive strain is the key mechanism suppressing spin splitting in current devices. Furthermore, we propose unstrained and tensile-strained heterostructures, fully compatible with state-of-the-art growth technology, that significantly enhance the relevant spin-orbit effect. By numerically simulating ballistic Josephson junctions, we predict spin splittings comfortably in the GHz range, more than 2 orders of magnitude larger than compressively strained cases, and all-electric quantum gates in a hundred nanoseconds. Our results establish strain engineering as a key design principle for realizing Andreev spin qubits in germanium-based devices.

</details>

### [94] [Field-driven phases in a three-dimensional twisted Kitaev model for CoNb$_2$O$_6$: Interplay of frustration and spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21973)
*Tom Drechsler,Matthias Vojta*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CoNb₂O₆原被视为横场伊辛链（Ising chain in a transverse field）——量子相变（quantum phase transition）的范例材料，但后续发现其磁交换耦合更复杂，实际表现为扭曲的Kitaev链（twisted Kitaev chains）。因此需要建立更精确的三维模型来修正原有理解。

Method: 采用零温半经典（semiclassical）技术，构建包含Kitaev物理和受挫链间耦合（frustrated inter-chain coupling）的三维模型，在任意方向外加磁场下系统分析场驱动相序列。

Result: 绘制出任意磁场方向下的场驱动相图（phase diagram），识别出包含公度（commensurate）和非公度（incommensurate）链间有序的多个相。由于自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）效应，相图对磁场角度微小变化极其敏感。计算了各相中的静态可观测量（static observables）和磁激发谱（magnetic excitation spectra）。

Conclusion: 计算结果与现有实验数据吻合，揭示了CoNb₂O₆中Kitaev物理和受挫链间耦合对磁场方向敏感性的关键作用，为理解该材料的复杂磁序和激发提供了更准确的理论框架。

Abstract: The Ising chain in a transverse field stands out as a paradigmatic example for a quantum phase transition. CoNb$_2$O$_6$ has been discussed as a material realization of this physics, but it was later realized that its magnetic exchange couplings are more complicated, taking the form of twisted Kitaev chains. Here we study a three-dimensional model for CoNb$_2$O$_6$, taking into account both Kitaev physics and frustrated inter-chain coupling, in applied magnetic field. Using semiclassical techniques at zero temperature, we map out the sequence of field-driven phases for arbitrary field direction; these include phases with commensurate and incommensurate inter-chain order. As a result of spin-orbit coupling, the phase diagram is extremely sensitive to small changes in the field angle. We compute static observables as well as magnetic excitation spectra in the various phases and connect our results to existing experimental data.

### [95] [Beyond Variational Bias: Resolving Intertwined Orders in the Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21978)
*Luciano Loris Viteritti,Riccardo Rende,Christopher Roth,Anirvan Sengupta,Giuseppe Carleo,Antoine Georges*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比三种不同Transformer反流费米子波函数，发现变分能量（variational energy）本身不足以区分具有竞争序的基态，只有通过对称性恢复和方差缩减（variance reduction）系统改进波函数后，才能揭示超导序（superconducting order）和条带序（stripe order）共存的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限掺杂下的二维Hubbard模型存在竞争或交织序（competing or intertwined orders），不同计算方法对其基态得出相互矛盾的结论，该研究旨在揭示这一分歧的关键来源。

Method: 基于Slater行列式（Slater determinant）、其粒子-空穴对应物（particle-hole counterpart）以及Pfaffian（Pfaffian）构建三种不同的Transformer反流费米子波函数（Transformer backflow fermionic wave functions），初始化时不做任何平均场预训练（mean-field pretraining），并通过对称性恢复（symmetry restoration）和方差缩减逐步提高精度。

Result: 虽然三种变分波函数达到近乎简并的最优变分能量，但各自收敛到具有定性不同自旋、电荷和配对关联（spin, charge, and pairing correlations）的状态。经过对称性恢复和方差缩减改进后，三者均收敛到超导序和条带序共存的同一物理图像。

Conclusion: 变分能量本身不足以在存在竞争相时识别基态；在得出物理结论之前，必须追踪关联函数随波函数系统性改进的演化过程。

Abstract: The two-dimensional Hubbard model at finite doping hosts competing or intertwined orders, resulting in conflicting conclusions from different computational approaches regarding its ground state. We show that a key source of such discrepancies is the bias encoded in the variational ansatz. We consider three different Transformer backflow fermionic wave functions based on a Slater determinant, its particle-hole counterpart, and a Pfaffian, initialized without any mean-field pretraining. We show that, despite achieving nearly degenerate, state-of-the-art variational energies, each ansatz converges to a state with qualitatively different spin, charge, and pairing correlations. Upon improving accuracy via symmetry restoration and variance reduction, however, all three converge to the same physical picture: coexisting superconducting and stripe orders. These results demonstrate that variational energy alone is insufficient to identify the ground state in the presence of competing phases, and highlight the importance of tracking how correlation functions evolve as the wave function is systematically improved before drawing physical conclusions.

</details>


### [96] [Anisotropy of spin waves in the field-polarized phase of Fe-doped MnSi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21985)
*I. N. Khoroshiy,A. Podlesnyak,D. Menzel,M. C. Rahn,D. S. Inosov,A. S. Sukhanov,S. E. Nikitin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过高分辨非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering, INS）测量Fe掺杂Mn$_{0.9}$Fe$_{0.1}$Si在场极化铁磁态中的自旋波（spin waves），发现具有各向异性刚度的非互易自旋波（non-reciprocal spin waves），其抛物线色散随磁场线性移动，且立方材料中显著的刚度各向异性与现有理论模型不一致，表明需要修正理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性磁纹理（chiral magnetic textures）如斯格明子（skyrmions）因新颖输运性质受到凝聚态领域广泛关注，而这类拓扑非平庸磁相（如MnSi中的斯格明子晶格）的稳定化由其底层磁相互作用决定，这些相互作用可通过自旋波激发（spin-wave excitations）测量加以探测。本文旨在通过高分辨非弹性中子散射实验深入研究Fe掺杂MnSi中的自旋波行为。

Method: 采用高分辨非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering, INS）技术，在深场极化铁磁态（field-polarized ferromagnetic state）下对Fe掺杂样品Mn$_{0.9}$Fe$_{0.1}$Si进行自旋波测量。

Result: 观察到非互易自旋波（non-reciprocal spin waves），其抛物线色散（parabolic dispersion）随磁场线性移动。自旋波刚度（spin-wave stiffness）呈现高度各向异性：平行于施加场方向为14.7 meV $\rm{\mathring{A}}$$^2$，垂直于场方向为7.6 meV $\rm{\mathring{A}}$$^2$。

Conclusion: 立方材料中观测到的显著自旋波刚度各向异性不符合MnSi的标准理论模型，表明需要对现有理论理解进行修正。

Abstract: Chiral magnetic textures, such as skyrmions, are of great interest to the condensed matter community due to their novel transport properties. The stabilization of topologically non-trivial magnetic phases, like the skyrmion lattice in MnSi, is governed by underlying magnetic interactions which can be probed via measurements of spin-wave excitations. Here, we report high-resolution inelastic neutron scattering (INS) measurements of the spin waves in Fe-doped Mn$_{0.9}$Fe$_{0.1}$Si deep within its field-polarized ferromagnetic state. We observe non-reciprocal spin waves with a parabolic dispersion that shifts linearly with magnetic field. Crucially, the spin-wave stiffness is highly anisotropic, with values of 14.7 meV $\rm{\mathring{A}}$$^2$ parallel to the applied field and 7.6 meV $\rm{\mathring{A}}$$^2$ perpendicular to it. This pronounced anisotropy in a cubic material is inconsistent with standard theoretical models for MnSi and indicates a necessity to revise our theoretical understanding.

</details>


### [97] [Apparent Planckian scattering from local polaron formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22029)
*Brian Yong-Ho Lee,Chaitanya Murthy*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于局域极化子（local polaron）形成的简单机制，用以解释表观普朗克散射（Planckian scattering）行为，其中输运散射率 Γ_tr = Γ₀ + αk_BT/ℏ 通过准弹性散射（quasielastic scattering）在无需精细调节的条件下自然产生。蒙特卡洛模拟在无序电子-声子耦合的 Holstein 模型中为该机制提供了证据，并发现该机制在耦合强度的一定区间内使斜率 α 近似恒定，且显著违反马西森定则（Matthiessen's rule）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释凝聚态物理中观测到的“普朗克散射”现象（即输运散射率正比于温度且系数 α 量级为 O(1)）的微观起源，因为该现象在高温超导等奇异金属（strange metal）中普遍存在，但其机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用局域极化子形成的物理图像，对具有无序电子-声子耦合的 Holstein 模型在绝热极限（adiabatic limit）下进行蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，系统分析输运散射率 Γ_tr 随温度及耦合强度的行为。

Result: 发现输运散射率呈现 Γ_tr = Γ₀ + αk_BT/ℏ 的形式，且 α 量级为 O(1)。在耦合强度的一个有限区间内，α 近似恒定，该区间与局域极化子形成的起始区域重合。在该区间内，改变耦合强度不改变斜率 α，而是改变截距 Γ₀，即马西森定则被显著违反。

Conclusion: 该机制适用于任何存在主导性无序相互作用且能驱动极化子形成的系统，可能涵盖最近提出的无序-汤川耦合奇异金属模型（disordered-Yukawa-coupling strange metal models）中极化子形成未被抑制的参数区间。

Abstract: We propose a simple mechanism for apparent Planckian scattering based on local polaron formation, in which $Γ_\text{tr} = Γ_0 + αk_BT / \hbar$ with $α\sim O(1)$ emerges from quasielastic scattering without fine tuning. We provide evidence for our proposal in Monte Carlo simulations of the Holstein model with disordered electron-phonon coupling in the adiabatic limit. Our mechanism generates a finite interval of couplings in which the slope $α$ is approximately constant, coinciding with the onset of local polaron formation. In this regime, Matthiessen's rule is dramatically violated (or obeyed, depending on one's point of view) in that changes to the couplings, which in perturbation theory would alter the slope $α$, instead change the intercept $Γ_0$. We conjecture that a version of our mechanism applies to any system with a dominant disordered interaction that can drive polaron formation. This potentially includes regimes of the recently introduced disordered-Yukawa-coupling strange metal models where polaron formation is not suppressed.

</details>


### [98] [Uncovering long-lived relaxation channel and exciton-phonon coupling in \textrm{Ta\textsubscript{2}NiSe\textsubscript{5}} via non-degenerate pump-probe spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22218)
*Poulami Ghosh,Anupama Chauhan,Sidhanta Sahu,Sk Kalimuddin,Mintu Mondal,N. Kamaraju*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用非简并光泵浦-探测光谱（optical pump-probe spectroscopy）研究了窄带隙半导体Ta₂NSi₅（TNSe）中的非平衡动力学，除已建立的亚皮秒弛豫通道外，发现了一个约280-600 ps的异常缓慢恢复过程，归因于激子与非平衡声子之间的增强散射；同时观测到两个相干声子模式（1.0和2.9 THz），其中1.0 THz模式表现出与激子凝聚态（excitonic condensate）强耦合的序参量（order-parameter）式温度依赖行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator）是激子自发凝聚导致新奇多体现象的量子相，TNSe作为层状窄带隙半导体，为探索关联激子相及其动力学提供了模型平台；先前研究未充分揭示长寿命激子-声子动力学过程，因此有必要扩展泵浦-探测时间窗口。

Method: 采用温度依赖的非简并光泵浦-探测光谱技术，泵浦光能量为3.14 eV，探测光能量为1.57 eV，将泵浦-探测延迟窗口延长至500 ps。

Result: 除已知的亚皮秒弛豫通道（约0.7-0.9 ps）外，发现一个约280-600 ps的缓慢恢复过程；观测到1.0和2.9 THz两个相干声子模式，前者呈现序参量式的温度依赖行为，后者无此耦合特征。

Conclusion: TNSe中存在多层级弛豫路径（hierarchy of relaxation pathways），其中长寿命激子-声子动力学需通过扩展时间检测窗口才能完整捕捉；1.0 THz声子模式与激子凝聚态强耦合，2.9 THz模式则与结构相变（structural phase transition）的非谐晶格动力学相关。

Abstract: An excitonic insulator represents a quantum phase in which spontaneous condensation of excitons leads to novel many-body phenomena. Ta$_2$NSi$_5$ (TNSe), a layered narrow-gap semiconductor, has emerged as a model platform to probe these correlated excitonic phases and their underlying dynamics below 327 K. In this work, we investigate the nonequilibrium dynamics of TNSe using temperature-dependent, non-degenerate optical pump-probe spectroscopy with a 3.14 eV pump and a 1.57 eV probe, extending the accessible pump-probe delay window up to 500 ps. In addition to the well-established sub-picosecond relaxation channel ($\sim$ 0.7- 0.9 ps) associated with carrier cooling and recombination, accompanied by exciton reformation, we uncover a much slower recovery process with a decay time of $\sim$ 280-600~ps, significantly longer than previously reported. We attribute this unusually prolonged recovery to enhanced scattering between excitons and nonequilibrium phonons, which delays the re-establishment of equilibrium excitonic correlations. On top of this bi-exponential background, we observe two coherent phonon modes at 1.0 and 2.9 THz with distinctly different coupling behaviors. The 1.0 THz mode exhibits an order-parameter-like temperature dependence, consistent with strong coupling to the excitonic condensate in TNSe. In contrast, the 2.9 THz mode does not exhibit any discernible coupling to the excitonic order parameter, and appears to arise from anharmonic lattice dynamics associated with the structural phase transition. Together, these results elucidate the hierarchy of relaxation pathways in TNSe and highlight the importance of extending the temporal detection window in pump-probe measurements to fully capture long-lived exciton-phonon dynamics.

</details>


### [99] [QAssemble: A Pure Python Package for Quantum Many-Body Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22223)
*Seongjun Mo,Dongming Li,Mancheon Han,Johan Jönsson,Byungkyun Kang,Hoonkyung Lee,Gabriel Kotliar,Sangkook Choi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: QAssemble 是一个纯 Python 量子多体问题软件包，采用面向对象架构统一实现了紧束缚、Hartree-Fock 和 GW 等多种泛函方法，并通过矢量化与离散 Lehmann 表示在纯 Python 环境中实现了高效率计算。在石墨烯电子结构和五轨道 Hund-Hubbard 模型上的验证表明，该方法相比传统基于循环的 Matsubara 实现可获得高达 60 倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体问题（quantum many-body problem）的高效数值模拟长期以来依赖底层语言或混合编程，纯 Python 环境下计算效率往往受限。QAssemble 旨在提供一个兼具代码清晰性、可扩展性与计算效率的纯 Python 解决方案，以降低开发门槛并推动方法学快速迭代。

Method: 采用统一面向对象架构，将晶格结构、哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）、格林函数（Green's function）、自能（self-energy）、极化率（polarizability）、屏蔽库仑相互作用（screened Coulomb interaction）等每个物理概念封装为独立类。性能关键核（如极化率泡泡、Dyson 方程求逆、晶格傅里叶变换）被系统性地矢量化，并结合离散 Lehmann 表示（discrete Lehmann representation，DLR）实现高效数值运算。数值计算依赖 NumPy、SciPy 和 libdlr 库。

Result: 在石墨烯电子结构（含局域与非局域相互作用）上完成验证。在五轨道扩展 Hund-Hubbard 模型上的基准测试显示，该策略相比传统基于循环的 Matsubara 实现可获得高达 60 倍的加速。软件支持批处理执行与交互式工作流两种模式。

Conclusion: QAssemble 证明了纯 Python 环境在量子多体问题模拟中能够同时实现代码清晰性和实际计算效率。其模块化设计与矢量化策略为泛函方法（如 GW 近似）的快速原型开发与生产级计算提供了统一的平台。

Abstract: QAssemble is a pure-Python package for the quantum many-body problem. It implements various functional approaches, such as tight-binding, Hartree-Fock, and GW approximations within a unified object-oriented architecture. Each physical concept--crystal structure, Hamiltonian, Green's function, self-energy, polarizability, screened Coulomb interaction--is represented as a distinct class. The modular design prioritizes code clarity and extensibility, leveraging NumPy, SciPy, and libdlr for numerical operations. Performance-critical kernels, including the polarizability bubble, Dyson equation inversion, and lattice Fourier transforms, are systematically vectorized and combined with the discrete Lehmann representation to achieve practical efficiency within a pure-Python environment. We validate QAssemble on the electronic structure of graphene with local and non-local interactions. Furthermore, benchmarks on a five-orbital extended Hund-Hubbard model demonstrate that this strategy delivers up to a 60x speedup over traditional loop-based Matsubara implementations. QAssemble supports both batch execution for production calculations and interactive workflows for method development.

</details>


### [100] [The antiferromagnetic Chern insulator phase in the Kane-Mele-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22329)
*Bao-Qing Wang,Can Shao,Takami Tohyama,Hong-Gang Luo,Hantao Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，在具有有限子晶格势的Kane-Mele-Hubbard模型中发现了反铁磁陈绝缘体（antiferromagnetic Chern insulator, AFCI）相，并通过激发隙、各向异性反铁磁关联及边界条件依赖的保真度敏感性等证据，确认了该相的存在；进一步揭示出扭角空间中绝热连续性的破坏，并提出了修正计算方案以获得稳健的陈数（Chern number）C=1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁陈绝缘体相（AFCI）以反铁磁关联与量子化霍尔电导共存为特征，但其能否在保持时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry, TRS）的Kane-Mele-Hubbard模型中存在，长期以来是一个未解决问题。本文旨在通过数值方法验证该相的存在性。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，分析激发隙（excitation gap）、沿z轴和xy平面的各向异性反铁磁关联（AFM correlations），以及在扭角边界条件（twisted boundary conditions）下的保真度敏感性（fidelity susceptibility）。此外，对（自旋）陈数（spin Chern number）进行数值评估，并针对绝热连续性破坏问题提出修正计算方案。

Result: 所有分析指标一致证实了AFCI相的存在。数值评估显示，在扭角空间中陈数对应的绝热连续性（adiabatic continuity）遭到破坏，表明Hubbard相互作用诱导的反铁磁扰动驱动了时间反演对称性破缺（TRS breaking）。采用修正方案后，在该相内获得了稳健的量子化陈数C=1。

Conclusion: Kane-Mele-Hubbard模型在有限子晶格势下可以存在AFCI相，且该相的出现与时间反演对称性的自发破缺有关；修正后的陈数计算方案能够有效应对绝热连续性破坏的问题。

Abstract: The emergence of the antiferromagnetic (AFM) Chern insulator (AFCI) phase in the Kane-Mele-Hubbard (KMH) model with a finite sublattice potential is investigated. The AFCI, characterized by AFM correlations coexisting with quantized Hall conductance, has long raised the question of whether it can exist in the KMH model that respects time-reversal symmetry (TRS). Using exact diagonalization, we analyze the excitation gap, anisotropic AFM correlations along the $z$ axis and in the $xy$ plane, and the fidelity susceptibility under twisted boundary conditions, all of which provide consistent evidence for the AFCI phase. In particular, our numerical evaluation on the (spin) Chern number reveals a breakdown of adiabatic continuity in the twist-angle space, indicating an instability toward TRS breaking driven by Hubbard-induced AFM perturbations. A modified computational scheme is further proposed, which yields a robust quantized Chern number $C=1$ within this phase.

</details>


### [101] [Exact relations between the density-density correlators of states in a spin multiplet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22628)
*Ritajit Kundu,Ajit C. Balram*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文推导出自旋多重态（spin multiplet）中态之间对关联函数（pair-correlation functions）和静态结构因子（static structure factors）的精确恒等式，并利用这些恒等式仅从最高权重态（highest-weight state）的关联函数计算出多重态中所有其他成员的密度-密度关联函数。将这些关系应用于分数量子霍尔态（FQH states）的能量计算，包括解析计算Halperin-(1,1,1)态随密度失衡和层间距变化的能量，以及数值评估其他多种FQH态的能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为解决自旋多重态中不同态的密度-密度关联函数需要分别计算的困难，寻找一种利用最高权重态关联函数统一计算整个多重态中所有态关联函数的方法。

Method: 推导出自旋多重态内态的对关联函数与静态结构因子之间的精确恒等式（exact identities），使得仅通过最高权重态的关联函数即可计算多重态所有成员的密度-密度关联函数。

Result: 将所提出的恒等式应用于分数量子霍尔态的能量计算，解析得到了Halperin-(1,1,1)态能量随密度失衡和层间距的函数关系，并对其他多种FQH态的能量进行了数值计算。

Conclusion: 所建立的精确恒等式提供了一种高效计算自旋多重态中所有态关联函数的方法，显著简化了分数量子霍尔态等物理体系的能量计算过程。

Abstract: We present exact identities relating the pair-correlation functions and static structure factors of states in a spin multiplet. This allows us to compute these density-density correlation functions of all members of the multiplet using just these correlation functions of the highest-weight state. We apply these relations to obtain energies for many fractional quantum Hall (FQH) states. In particular, we analytically compute the energies of the Halperin-$(1,1,1)$ state as a function of density imbalance and layer separation, and numerically evaluate these energies for many other FQH states.

### [102] [Replica Tensor Train](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22718)
*Miha Srdinsek,Gabriel Gouraud,Xavier Waintal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“复制张量训练（replica tensor train, RTT）”的变分波函数，融合了张量网络（tensor network）与量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）两种方法，既能捕获体率纠缠（volume-law entanglement），又能通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）计算可观测量，并展示了其在二维横场自旋模型上的低计算成本应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统张量网络方法在处理体率纠缠（volume-law entanglement）体系时面临指数级计算开销；而量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）方法虽能处理大系统，但受限于符号问题（sign problem）。本文旨在构建一种兼具两者优势的数值多体方法，使其既能描述体率纠缠态，又能以代数方式（而非梯度下降）求解基态，并避免直接计算可观测量时的困难。

Method: 该方法的核心变分结构是“复制张量训练（replica tensor train, RTT）”：在标准张量训练（tensor train）基础上施加一组非局域算符（non-local operators），使多个指标被强制映射到同一物理指标。RTT继承了张量网络工具箱中线性组合状态和施加特定算符的能力，从而可通过纯代数方式——如标准张量网络算法——求解局部哈密顿量的基态，无需梯度下降。同时，由于RTT具有体率纠缠体积律结构，无法直接计算可观测量；因此作者采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）进行采样，类似于量子计算中制备态后以采样方式获取结果。此外，该方法可在变分流形内推广构建Krylov子空间（Krylov-subspace）基态方法。

Result: 在二维横场自旋模型（2D spin model with transverse magnetic field）上进行数值实验，结果表明所提出的RTT方法能够以较低计算成本求解该模型。论文展示了RTT结合代数基态求解与MCMC采样的可行性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了张量网络与量子蒙特卡洛的融合策略——RTT变分框架——能够有效处理体率纠缠体系，且无需梯度下降即可通过代数方法获得基态，同时利用MCMC绕过直接计算可观测量的困难。该方法为数值多体问题提供了一种兼具表达能力和计算效率的新路径，并可进一步扩展至Krylov子空间方法。

Abstract: We describe a numerical many-body technique that is based on both tensor networks and quantum Monte Carlo. The variational ansatz is a tensor network that can harvest volume-law entanglement. It is constructed from a tensor train to which one applies a set of non-local operators that force several indices of the tensor train to represent the same physical index, hence its name -- replica tensor train (RTT). From the tensor network toolbox, it inherits the possibility to make linear combinations of these states and apply a certain class of operators. We can therefore find the ground-state of a local Hamiltonian in a purely algebraic way as in standard tensor network algorithms -- i.e. without using gradient descent methods. On the other hand, the volume-law structure forbids calculating physical observables directly. In much the same way as on a quantum computer where one can prepare a state but can only sample it at the end, here we have to use Markov Chain Monte Carlo to compute the observables. We further show that the approach can be extended to build Krylov-subspace ground-state methods within the variational manifold. We illustrate the different algorithms on a two-dimensional spin model with a transverse magnetic field, which can be solved by this approach at low computational cost.

</details>

### [103] [Active Jurin's law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22231)
*Birendra Mandal,Joydip Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过连续体主动向列型（active nematics）理论，将经典毛细上升（capillary rise）规律（Jurin定律）推广至活性流体（active fluids），推导出广义的活性Jurin定律，并通过无量纲形式揭示了活性应力（active stress）与界面排列状态对毛细高度的调控机制，包括增强、抑制乃至双稳态行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典毛细上升问题由Jurin定律描述，但该定律仅适用于平衡被动流体。本研究旨在将毛细上升理论扩展至活性流体——即通过微观能量消耗产生内应力的材料，探索活性效应对毛细现象的影响。

Method: 采用连续体主动向列型理论（continuum theory of active nematics），分析活性流体在毛细上升中的法向应力平衡（normal stress balance），推导出包含活性法向应力贡献的广义Jurin定律，并通过线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）研究平衡态的稳定性与多稳态行为。

Result: 推导出无量纲形式的活性Jurin定律：\(H_{\infty} = 1 - \mathrm{Ja}_a ξ_0\)，其中活性Jurin数（active Jurin number, \(\mathrm{Ja}_a\)）比较活性应力与毛细压力，\(ξ_0\)描述活性组分在弯月面处的排列方向。建立了\((\mathrm{Ja}_a, ξ_0)\)相图，区分活性增强上升、抑制上升及经典毛细态完全抑制三种区域。在取向序受约束与流动影响时，非线性平衡条件可产生多个稳态高度；过阻尼动力学（overdamped dynamics）选择单一稳态，而惯性扩展（inertial extension）允许活性诱导的双稳态（activity-induced bistability）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，内生成应力从根本上重塑了经典的毛细输送问题，活性效应可显著增强或抑制毛细上升，并可导致经典毛细态的完全失稳及多稳态现象。

Abstract: Capillary rise is one of the classical problems in fluid mechanics and is traditionally described by Jurin's law, which balances capillary suction against hydrostatic pressure. Here we extend this classical result to active fluids, materials that generate internal stresses through microscopic energy consumption. Using the continuum theory of active nematics, we show that activity modifies the normal stress balance at the liquid-gas interface through an additional active normal stress contribution. This leads to a generalized active Jurin's law, which can be written in dimensionless form as \(H_{\infty} = 1 - \mathrm{Ja}_a ξ_0\), where \(H_{\infty}\) is the dimensionless active Jurin height at equilibrium, \(\mathrm{Ja}_a\) is an active Jurin number comparing active stress to capillary pressure, and \(ξ_0\) characterizes the alignment of active constituents at the meniscus. The theory predicts that extensile and contractile active fluids can either enhance or suppress capillary rise depending on the magnitude of activity and the interfacial alignment state. From this relation we construct a phase diagram in the \((\mathrm{Ja}_a,ξ_0)\) plane that delineates regimes of activity-enhanced rise, activity-suppressed rise, and complete suppression of the classical capillary state. When orientational order depends on confinement and flow, the coupling between activity and capillarity produces nonlinear equilibrium conditions that may admit multiple steady heights; linear stability analysis reveals that the overdamped dynamics selects a single stable state, whereas the inertial extension allows the possibility of activity-induced bistability. These results show that internally generated stresses fundamentally reshape one of the most classical capillary transport problems.

</details>


### [104] [Covariant Onsager and Onsager-Machlup principles for active and inertial dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22371)
*Kento Yasuda,Bin Zheng,Zhongqiang Xiong,Zhanglin Hou,Kenta Ishimoto,Xinpeng Xu,David Andelman,Shigeyuki Komura*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文为活性系统（active systems）发展了昂萨格原理（Onsager principle）的协变形式，并将其推广到考虑热涨落（thermal fluctuations）的昂萨格-马赫卢普原理（Onsager-Machlup principle），验证了该推广与随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）的一致性，并进一步将惯性效应（inertia）纳入变分框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 昂萨格原理为耗散动力学现象学方程提供了变分路径，但现有理论在活性系统和热涨落存在时的几何一致性尚不明确。本文旨在将昂萨格原理协变地推广至活性系统，并建立包含热涨落和惯性的统一变分框架，同时确保与随机热力学及细致涨落定理（detailed fluctuation theorem）自洽。

Method: 首先，通过最小化瑞利量（Rayleighian）并确保坐标变换下的几何一致性，发展活性系统的昂萨格原理协变形式。其次，引入昂萨格-马赫卢普泛函（Onsager-Machlup functional）和随机轨迹的路径概率（path probability），构建活性系统的昂萨格-马赫卢普原理。最后，在变分过程中固定协变加速度（covariant acceleration），将惯性纳入该变分框架。

Result: 推导出活性系统在协变形式下的昂萨格原理方程；证明了满足细致涨落定理的扩展昂萨格-马赫卢普理论与随机热力学一致；得到了包含惯性效应后的正确协变运动方程。

Conclusion: 本文建立的协变昂萨格原理与扩展昂萨格-马赫卢普理论为活性系统提供了一致且自洽的变分描述，可在几何上兼容坐标变换，在物理上与随机热力学和细致涨落定理相统一，并自然包含惯性贡献。

Abstract: The Onsager principle provides a variational route to the phenomenological equations of dissipative dynamics through the minimization of the Rayleighian. We develop a covariant formulation of the Onsager principle for active systems, ensuring geometric consistency under coordinate transformations. To further incorporate thermal fluctuations, we formulate the Onsager-Machlup principle for active systems by considering the Onsager-Machlup functional and the corresponding path probability for stochastic trajectories. Requiring that the path probability obeys the detailed fluctuation theorem, we show that the extended Onsager-Machlup theory is consistent with stochastic thermodynamics. Moreover, we incorporate inertia into the variational framework and show that the proper covariant equations follow when the covariant acceleration is held fixed during the variation.

</details>


### [105] [Surface coating induced lubrication in flowing granular materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22396)
*Sayali V. Chaudhary,Ashish V. Orpe*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用离散元方法模拟了球形颗粒在倾斜平面上与润滑剂颗粒混合后的流动行为，发现润滑剂含量对流动速率呈现非单调影响：先增加后减小，分别归因于摩擦系数降低和颗粒致密化与阻尼增强。模拟结果与实验定性一致，深化了对粉末润滑现象的理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过离散元法（discrete element method, DEM）模拟研究球形散装颗粒（bulk granular particles）与小型球形润滑剂颗粒在倾斜平面上的混合流动，探索润滑剂含量对整体流动行为的影响机制。

Method: 采用离散元法模拟，在润滑剂颗粒与散装颗粒之间引入预定义的黏附相互作用（predefined cohesive interaction），使前者能够涂覆于后者表面。

Result: 整体流动速率对润滑剂含量呈现非单调依赖性：随润滑剂含量增加先升高，在中等含量时达到最大值，之后下降。上升阶段归因于润滑剂涂覆后颗粒间摩擦系数降低；下降阶段归因于颗粒致密化（densification）和阻尼（damping）增强。

Conclusion: 模拟结果与已有实验结果定性一致，整合了新的计算洞见与先前的实验证据，增强了对粉末润滑现象（powder lubrication phenomena）的理解。

Abstract: We investigate the flow of spherical, bulk granular particles down an inclined plane mixed with small-sized spherical lubricant particles using discrete element method simulations. Predefined cohesive interaction is implemented between lubricant and bulk particles, enabling the coating of the former over the latter. The overall flow rate exhibits non-monotonic dependence on lubricant content. Initially, it increases with lubricant addition, reaches a maximum at an intermediate lubricant content, and decreases for even higher lubricant content. The increase in the flow rate is attributed to a lower inter-particle friction coefficient between lubricant-coated bulk particles. The decrease in the flow rate at higher lubricant content, on the other hand, is attributed to enhanced densification and increased damping between crowded particles. Both these occurrences are examined using various flow level characteristics. The simulation results are found to be in qualitative agreement with previous experimental results. Overall, the outcome integrates novel computational insights and prior experimental results to enhance the understanding of the powder lubrication phenomena.

### [106] [Odd pathways speed up self-assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22408)
*Dawid Dopierała,Luca Cocconi,Robert L. Jack,Anton Souslov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类名为“奇异性相互作用”（odd interactions）的非互易相互作用，这类作用能在保持平衡态玻尔兹曼分布的前提下加速自组装过程，并发现了动力学加速与功率耗散之间存在权衡关系，为构建高保真、高能效的活性自组装系统提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性自组装（active self-assembly）可通过外部能量注入绕过平衡态瓶颈，但通用的驱动方式通常会扭曲目标结构，且组装完成后仍需持续能量输入。因此，亟需一种既能加速组装又不破坏平衡分布的能量高效方案。

Method: 研究了一类非互易相互作用（non-reciprocal interactions），即“奇异性相互作用”。通过分析其诱导的概率流（probability currents）如何重塑基本动力学过程（包括势垒穿越、软模弛豫和亚稳态间跃迁），揭示了该机制通过非互易耦合提高反应坐标（reaction coordinate）的有效迁移率来加速Arrhenius速率。

Result: 奇异性相互作用可在保持平衡态玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）的前提下加速自组装；该加速源自反应坐标有效迁移率的提高；同时发现动力学加速与功率耗散（power dissipation）之间存在权衡关系。

Conclusion: 提出了一种通过“活性催化剂”（active catalysts）实现高能效、高保真自组装的思路：催化剂可瞬时加速系统向平衡态弛豫，并在到达目标状态后失活，从而避免持续的能量消耗。

Abstract: Active self-assembly can bypass equilibrium bottlenecks through external energy injection. However, generic driving typically distorts target structures and requires sustained energy input even after assembly is complete. Here, we investigate a class of non-reciprocal interactions that accelerates assembly while preserving the equilibrium Boltzmann distribution. The probability currents induced by these odd interactions reshape fundamental processes, including activated barrier crossing, soft-mode relaxation, and transitions between metastable states. In particular, these currents enhance Arrhenius rates by driving particles across otherwise inaccessible free-energy barriers. We show that this acceleration arises from an effective increase in the mobility of the reaction coordinate, mediated by non-reciprocal coupling between mechanical modes. In turn, we discover a trade-off between kinetic acceleration and power dissipation when active forces are engaged. Our results suggest a route to energy-efficient, high-fidelity self-assembly via active catalysts that transiently accelerate relaxation toward equilibrium targets and deactivate upon reaching the desired state.

</details>


### [107] [Comparative Silane Surface Functionalization Strategies for Enhanced Bloch Surface Wave Biosensing of Anti-SARS-CoV-2 Antibodies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22444)
*Agostino Occhicone,Alberto Sinibaldi,Paola Di Matteo,Daniele Chiappetta,Riccardo Guadagnoli,Peter Munzert,Francesco Michelotti*

TL;DR: 本文通过比较三种有机硅烷化学修饰（APTES、APDMS、CPTES）在基于布洛赫表面波（BSW）的一维光子晶体生物传感器上的性能，发现CPTES在无标记和荧光增强两种模式下均表现出最佳的信号特异性、重复性和低非特异性吸附，适用于SARS-CoV-2抗体的快速血清学检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: CPTES是三种被研究的修饰策略中最稳健且可重复的BSW生物传感功能化方案，该平台在临床相关抗体的快速、灵敏检测方面具有潜力。

Abstract: Surface functionalization plays a decisive role in the performance of biosensors, as it governs the efficiency and stability of biomolecule immobilization at the sensor interface and, consequently, the overall performance of the biosensing platforms. In this work, we present a comparative study of three organosilane chemistries - APTES, APDMS, and CPTES - applied to a SiO2 terminated 1D photonic crystal able to sustain Bloch surface waves and designed to operate as optical biosensors in both label free and fluorescence enhanced modes. Each chemistry was evaluated through a standardized label-free protocol based on the interaction between immobilized SARS CoV 2 spike protein and its corresponding antibodies, enabling quantitative assessment of binding efficiency, nonspecific adsorption, and signal repeatability. CPTES exhibited the most favorable balance between specific signals, reduced variability, and low nonspecific adsorption. The three chemistries were subsequently tested in fluorescence mode for the detection of anti SARS CoV 2 IgG antibodies in human serum, demonstrating the suitability of BSW enhanced fluorescence for rapid serological analysis. Overall, the study identifies CPTES as the most robust and reproducible functionalization strategy among the three investigated for BSW biosensing and highlights the potential of the platform for fast, sensitive detection of clinically relevant antibodies.

### [108] [Electrostatic-Elastic Softening and Ultraviolet Instability Driven by Non-DLVO Interactions in Charged Colloidal Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22448)
*Hao Wu,Zhong-Can Ou-Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过高斯涨落分析（Gaussian fluctuation analysis）严格推导了带电胶体晶体（colloidal crystal）中静电场与弹性场耦合导致的短波长力学失稳，发现当静电-弹性耦合参数 ξ 超过临界值 1 时，均匀相会在紫外波段（短波长）出现不稳定性，而长波长弹性模量因完美离子屏蔽（perfect ionic screening）保持刚性不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在移动离子渗透的胶体晶体中，静电与弹性自由度之间存在耦合，这种耦合会重整化有效屏蔽长度（effective screening length）并导致波矢依赖的弹性软化。理解该耦合系统的稳定性极限，对于阐明非DLVO相互作用如何驱动带电胶体晶体的局部结构塌缩具有关键意义。

Method: 基于最近提出的连续介质模型（continuum model），采用严格的 Gaussian 涨落分析，通过积分消去静电涨落（electrostatic fluctuations），推导出有效弹性模量 Γ(q) 作为波矢 q 的函数，并分析其在不同波矢范围的稳定性行为。

Result: 长波长模量 Γ(0) 恒等于裸模量 βK，受完美离子屏蔽保护；短波长模量 Γ(q→∞) = βK(1−ξ) 随耦合参数 ξ≡2βn₀v₀²K 增大而软化，当 ξ=1 时降为零。ξ>1 时，涨落谱（fluctuation spectrum）对所有 q > q_c = κ₀/√(ξ−1) 出现负本征值，标志均匀相出现紫外不稳定性（ultraviolet instability）。实际胶体晶体中，离散晶格截断 q_max∼π/a 将物理不稳定性限制在有限能带 q_c < q < q_max 内。

Conclusion: ξ=1 的转变标志着短波长力学失效（short-wavelength mechanical failure）的开始，而宏观弹性刚度（macroscopic elastic stiffness）始终保持稳定。该分析阐明了最小耦合模型（minimal coupling model）的正确物理诠释，并为非DLVO相互作用如何驱动带电胶体晶体局部结构塌缩提供了自洽的图像。

Abstract: Colloidal crystals permeated by mobile ions exhibit a coupling between electrostatic and elastic degrees of freedom that renormalizes the effective screening length and induces wave-vector-dependent elastic softening. Building on a recently proposed continuum model [\textit{Commun. Theor. Phys.} \textbf{77}, 055602 (2025)], we perform a rigorous Gaussian fluctuation analysis to elucidate the stability limits of the homogeneous phase. By integrating out the electrostatic fluctuations, we derive the effective elastic modulus $Γ(q)$ as a function of wave vector $q$. We show that the long-wavelength modulus $Γ(0)$ remains identically equal to the bare modulus $βK$, protected by perfect ionic screening. In contrast, the short-wavelength modulus $Γ(q\to\infty) = βK(1-ξ)$ softens as the electrostatic-elastic coupling $ξ\equiv 2βn_0 v_0^2 K$ increases, vanishing at a critical value $ξ=1$. For $ξ>1$, the fluctuation spectrum exhibits a negative eigenvalue for all wave vectors $q > q_c = κ_0/\sqrt{ξ-1}$, signaling an ultraviolet instability of the uniform phase. In a real colloidal crystal, this divergence is regulated by the discrete lattice cutoff $q_{\max}\simπ/a$, confining the physical instability to a finite band $q_c < q < q_{\max}$. The macroscopic limit $q\to 0$ remains unconditionally stable for all $ξ$. The transition at $ξ=1$ thus marks the onset of short-wavelength mechanical failure, while macroscopic elastic stiffness remains intact. Our analysis clarifies the proper physical interpretation of the minimal coupling model and provides a consistent picture of how non-DLVO interactions can drive local structural collapse in charged colloidal crystals.

</details>


### [109] [Anomalous Mean-Squared Displacement in Quantum Active Matter from a Wigner Phase-Space Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22600)
*Sangyun Lee,Yehor Tuchkov,Alexander P. Antonov,Benno Liebchen,Hartmut Löwen,Giovanna Morigi,Michael te Vrugt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了基于维格纳函数（Wigner function）的量子主动物质（quantum active matter）完整量子描述，通过引入混合维格纳主方程（hybrid Wigner master equation），解析推导了量子均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）的时间依赖关系，揭示了MSD ∼ t⁶及更陡峭的MSD ∼ t⁷标度行为，并考察了初始状态量子涨落对这些行为的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典主动物质（classical active matter）已得到广泛研究，但主动物质概念向量子系统（quantum systems）的拓展则探索甚少。本文旨在填补这一空白，发展主动物质的完整量子描述。

Method: 基于维格纳函数（Wigner function）建立完整的量子描述；引入混合维格纳主方程（hybrid Wigner master equation），将经典主动运动与量子自由度（quantum degrees of freedom）相结合；利用经典主动物质中的成熟技术计算量子均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）。

Result: 解析推导了MSD的时间依赖关系，澄清了特征标度MSD ∼ t⁶出现的条件；进一步发现，在特定参数和初始条件下，MSD可呈现更陡峭的标度行为MSD ∼ t⁷；考察了这些标度行为对初始状态量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文将主动物质概念成功拓展至量子领域，建立了基于维格纳函数的量子主动物质理论框架，揭示了量子主动系统中MSD的多种标度行为及其对初始量子涨落的敏感性，为后续量子主动物质研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Active matter is driven out of equilibrium by a local influx of energy. While classical active matter has been extensively studied, the extension of active matter concepts to quantum systems has been explored far less. In this work we develop a full quantum description based on the Wigner function. By introducing a hybrid Wigner master equation that incorporates classical active motion and quantum degrees of freedom, we compute the quantum mean-squared displacement (MSD) using established techniques from classical active matter. We analytically derive the time dependence of the MSD and clarify the conditions under which the characteristic scaling with time $\mathrm{MSD}\sim t^{6}$ emerges. We further show that, for certain parameter and initial conditions, the MSD can exhibit an even steeper scaling regime $\mathrm{MSD}\sim t^{7}$, and we examine the robustness of these behaviors against quantum fluctuations of the initial state.
