### [110] [Alterations in Conformations of Poly(3-hexylthiophene) on Au(111) Induced by Annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22687)
*Anmol Arya,François Vonau,Solomon L. Joseph,Thomas Pfohl,Silvia Siegenführ,Laurent Simon,Günter Reiter*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用高真空电喷雾沉积和扫描隧道显微镜，探究了单个聚(3-己基噻吩)（P3HT）链在金(111)重构表面的周期性势能景观上的导航行为。研究发现，聚合物的构象由衬底的周期性波纹势能（如调制表面势的深度和规则性）与热能的相互作用决定。在规则重构表面上，退火使链段克服势垒，单体受热力学驱动力趋向低能谷，链构象复制了鱼骨纹图案；在不规则重构表面上，无序的势能景观导致卷曲线团进行二维随机游走和塌缩链的混合。退火迫使聚合物形成多链团簇。结果表明，热能和衬底形貌是改变聚合物构象的控制参数，为分子层面上理性设计聚合物纳米结构提供了机制框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解单个聚合物链在具有周期性势能景观的固体表面上的导航行为，揭示衬底形貌与热能如何协同调控聚合物构象，从而为分子层面上理性设计聚合物纳米结构建立机制框架。

Method: 采用高真空电喷雾沉积（high-vacuum electrospray deposition）和扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM），在重构的Au(111)表面上直接观察单个P3HT链的构象行为。

Result: 在规则重构表面上，退火后P3HT链构象复制了鱼骨纹（herringbone）图案；在不规则重构表面上，形成了卷曲线团的二维随机游走（two-dimensional random walk）和塌缩链的混合；进一步退火迫使聚合物形成多链团簇。

Conclusion: 热能和衬底形貌是控制聚合物构象的关键参数，为在分子层面理性设计聚合物纳米结构提供了机制框架。

Abstract: Employing high-vacuum electrospray deposition and scanning tunneling microscopy, we investigated how individual poly(3-hexylthiophene) (P3HT) chains navigated on the periodic energy landscape of a reconstructed Au(111) surface. The resulting polymer conformations were governed by the interplay between the periodically corrugated substrate, in particular the depth and regularity of the modulated surface potential, and thermal energy. On a regularly reconstructed surface, annealing at °C provided sufficient energy for chain segments to overcome energy barriers of the corrugated surface potential landscape, allowing monomers along the chain to experience a strong thermodynamic driving force toward the low-energy valleys on the surface. The adsorbed polymers adopted a state where the polymer conformations were replicating the herringbone pattern. By contrast, on an irregularly reconstructed surface, the correspondingly disordered potential landscape yielded a diverse mix of coiled polymer chains performing a two-dimensional random walk and collapsed chains located in troughs of the energy landscape. Intriguingly, annealing at °C forced polymers to form clusters of many chains. Our results establish that thermal energy and substrate topography represent control parameters for altering polymer conformations, providing a mechanistic framework for rationally designing polymer nanostructures at the molecular level.

# math.AP [[Back]](#toc)

### [111] [Large time behavior and transition from vanishing to spreading regimes for the generalized Burgers-Fisher-KPP equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22108)
*Razvan Gabriel Iagar,Ariel Sánchez*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义Burgers-Fisher-KPP方程在大时间尺度下的解行为，识别了Heaviside和“反Heaviside”初值对应的临界速度，发现对流项系数k对解的渐近行为具有决定性影响，并给出了临界系数的存在性与估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在理解带有对流项（convection term）和双非线性源项（bistable nonlinear source term）的广义Burgers-Fisher-KPP方程在大时间尺度下的渐近行为，特别关注初值为Heaviside类函数时解是否收敛于行波解（traveling wave solution），以及对流项如何改变解的极限行为。

Method: 通过识别Heaviside初值对应的临界速度（critical velocity）\(\overline{c}\) 和反Heaviside初值对应的临界速度 \(\widetilde{c}=kn+2\sqrt{p-q}\)，分析解 \(H(x,t)\) 和 \(\widetilde{H}(x,t)\) 在 \(t\to\infty\) 时趋近于具有这些临界速度的唯一行波解。对更为一般的初值条件也进行了分析，并给出了阈值系数（threshold coefficient）\(k^*(n,p,q)\) 的尖锐估计（sharp estimates）。

Result: 反Heaviside解 \(\widetilde{H}(x,t)\) 在 \(t\to\infty\) 时一致趋于零。而Heaviside解 \(H(x,t)\) 的极限行为取决于临界速度 \(\overline{c}\) 的符号：当 \(k>k^*(n,p,q)\) 时 \(\overline{c}>0\)，\(H\) 趋于1；当 \(k<k^*(n,p,q)\) 时 \(\overline{c}<0\)，\(H\) 趋于0。临界速度 \(\overline{c}\) 是反常的（anomalous），无法用代数表达式显式给出。

Conclusion: 对流项对解的渐近行为具有显著影响：当 \(k=0\)（无对流项）时，Heaviside解始终趋于零；而当 \(k\neq0\) 时，解的极限可能反转。这一结果表明对流项可以根本上改变系统的大时间行为。研究还推广到了比Heaviside类函数更一般的初值条件。

Abstract: The large time behavior of solutions to the following generalized Burgers-Fisher-KPP equation $$ \partial_tu=u_{xx}+k(u^n)_x+u^p-u^q, \quad (x,t)\in\mathbb{R}\times(0,\infty), $$ with $n\geq2$, $p>q\geq1$ and $k\in\mathbb{R}$, is considered in this work. Denoting by $H(x,t)$, respectively $\widetilde{H}(x,t)$ the solutions having as initial condition the Heaviside, respectively the ``anti-Heaviside" functions $$ H_0(x)=\begin{cases}
  0, & \mbox{if } x<0
  1, & \mbox{if } x\geq0. \end{cases}, \quad \widetilde{H}_0(x)=1-H_0(x), $$ critical velocities $\overline{c}$, respectively $\widetilde{c}=kn+2\sqrt{p-q}$, are identified such that $H(x,t)$, respectively $\widetilde{H}(x,t)$ approach the unique traveling wave solution of the equation with these critical velocities as $t\to\infty$. The critical velocity $\overline{c}$ is \emph{anomalous}, that is, it cannot be made explicit by an algebraic expression. Assuming for simplicity $k>0$, a remarkable fact is that, while $\widetilde{H}(x,t)\to0$ as $t\to\infty$ uniformly on compact subsets of $\mathbb{R}$, the Heaviside solution $H$ might tend either to zero or to one as $t\to\infty$, depending on the sign of the critical velocity $\overline{c}$. This sign vary with respect to the exponents $n$, $p$, $q$ and the coefficient $k$ and, in fact, we prove that given $p$, $q$, $n$, there exists a critical coefficient $k^*(n,p,q)$ such that $\overline{c}>0$ if $k>k^*(n,p,q)$ and $\overline{c}<0$ if $k<k^*(n,p,q)$. The convergence to either zero or one reflects the sharp influence of the convection term, since in the absence of it (that is, $k=0$), $H(x,t)$ would always tend to zero as $t\to\infty$. The results include more general initial conditions than the Heaviside-type functions, and sharp estimates of the threshold coefficient $k^*(n,p,q)$ are also given.

</details>


### [112] [Trace estimates and improved pointwise bounds for joint eigenfunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22197)
*Xianchao Wu,Xiao Xiao*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文在量子可积系统（quantum integrable system）中，针对满足秩k非退化条件（rank k non-degeneracy condition）的点，建立了$h^{\frac{-n+k+1}{2}}$的尖锐界（sharp bound），改进了[GT20]关于$L^2$归一化联合本征函数（joint eigenfunctions）的多项式改进结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子可积系统中，[GT20]已给出典型点上对标准Hömander界的多项式改进，但尚未达到最优；本文旨在进一步改进该结果，建立更精确的最优估计。

Method: 通过引入秩k非退化条件（rank k non-degeneracy condition）对满足条件的点进行分类，并在此类点上推导出尖锐上界$h^{\frac{-n+k+1}{2}}$。

Result: 对于满足秩k非退化条件的点，建立了$h^{\frac{-n+k+1}{2}}$的尖锐界（sharp bound），改进了[GT20]的典型点多项式改进结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立的界是尖锐的（sharp），表明在满足秩k非退化条件的点上，该上界不可进一步改进，从而补充并优化了[GT20]对量子可积系统联合本征函数的研究。

Abstract: For $L^2$-normalized joint eigenfunctions in a quantum integrable system, [GT20] gave polynomial improvements over the standard Hömander bounds for typical points. In this paper, we improve their result by establishing a sharp bound of $h^{\frac{-n+k+1}2}$ for the points satisfying a rank $k$ non-degeneracy condition.

### [113] [Correctness of Biot's model of in situ leaching for incompressible liquid and compressible solid components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22645)
*Anvarbek Meirmanov,Akbota Senkebayeva*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对稀有金属原位浸出（in situ leaching）的数学模型，提出一种基于不动点定理（fixed point theorem）的求解方法。通过引入辅助问题 $\mathbb{B}^{\varepsilon}(r)$ 并应用均质化方法（homogenization method），从微观模型推导出宏观模型 $\mathbb{H}(r)$。利用 Banach 不动点定理证明解的存在唯一性，解决固液界面自由边界（free boundary）的非线性难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有金属原位浸出涉及两种液体的联合渗流，其微观模型 $\mathbb{A}^{\varepsilon}$ 面临一个关键困难：固体与液体组分之间的自由边界 $\Gamma(r)$ 未知，且受附加条件控制，现有标准方法无法直接处理这一非线性问题（nonlinear problem）。

Method: 首先，从充分光滑函数集 $\mathfrak{M}_{(0,T)}$ 中选取描述骨架结构的函数 $r(\boldsymbol{x},t)$，构造辅助问题 $\mathbb{B}^{\varepsilon}(r)$——一个由描述液固位移的椭圆系统（elliptic system）与酸浓度的抛物方程（parabolic equation）耦合构成的边值问题。选取最小光滑性的弱解（weak solution），应用均质化方法完成从微观到宏观尺度的过渡，得到宏观模型 $\mathbb{H}(r)$，其包含一个均质化边界条件（homogenized boundary condition），将法向边界速度 $V_N=\partial r/\partial t$ 表达为酸浓度 $c$ 的线性函数。通过算子 $\mathbb{F}\colon\mathfrak{M}_{(0,T)}\to\mathfrak{M}_{(0,T)}$ 建立 $c$ 与 $r$ 的依赖关系，证明 $\mathbb{F}$ 满足 Lipschitz 连续性（Lipschitz continuity），进而依据 Banach 不动点定理（Banach's fixed point theorem）得出唯一不动点 $r^{*}$，最终得到唯一解 $\mathbb{H}=\mathbb{H}(r^{*})$。

Result: 算子 $\mathbb{F}$ 是 Lipschitz 连续的，因此 Banach 不动点定理适用，存在唯一的不动点 $r^{*}$，从而宏观模型 $\mathbb{H}(r^{*})$ 有唯一解。

Conclusion: 通过不动点定理与均质化方法相结合，成功解决了自由边界非线性问题的求解困难，为稀有金属原位浸出的宏观建模提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: We study a mathematical model of in situ leaching of rare metals, in which the joint filtration of two liquids is governed by the microscopic model $\mathbb{A}^{\varepsilon}$. A key difficulty is the unknown (free) boundary $Γ(r)$ between solid and liquid components, determined by an additional condition on $Γ(r)$; no standard methods exist for this nonlinear problem. To resolve it, we apply the fixed point theorem. For a given function $r(\boldsymbol{x},t)$ from a set $\mathfrak{M}_{(0,T)}$ of sufficiently smooth functions describing the skeleton structure, we consider the auxiliary problem $\mathbb{B}^{\varepsilon}(r)$: an elliptic system for displacements of the liquid and solid components coupled with parabolic equations for the acid concentration. Selecting the weak solution of minimal smoothness, we apply the homogenization method to pass from the microscopic to the macroscopic description. The resulting macroscopic model $\mathbb{H}(r)$ contains a homogenized boundary condition that expresses the normal boundary velocity $V_{N}=\partial r/\partial t$ as a linear function of the acid concentration $c$. Since $c$ depends on $r$ via an operator $\mathbb{F}\colon\mathfrak{M}_{(0,T)}\to\mathfrak{M}_{(0,T)}$, we prove that $\mathbb{F}$ is Lipschitz continuous and, by Banach's theorem, possesses a unique fixed point $r^{*}$, which yields the unique solution $\mathbb{H}=\mathbb{H}(r^{*})$.

</details>

### [114] [How Electrons Become Mobile in a Colossal Dielectric -- Fe$_2$TiO$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22017)
*M. L. McLanahan,A. P. Ramirez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过宽频光谱学测量Fe₂TiO₅单晶的巨介电常数，发现局域偶极子运动的能垒（286.1 meV）与直流输运激活能（288.8 meV）在误差范围内一致，表明巨介电行为源于接近金属性的微观体相现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Fe₂TiO₅单晶中巨介电常数（colossal permittivity）的微观起源，尤其是局域偶极子弛豫与载流子长程输运之间是否存在共同的物理机制。

Method: 采用宽频光谱学（broadband spectroscopy）在20 Hz–1 MHz频率范围内测量单晶Fe₂TiO₅的介电响应，并用含Arrhenius激活形式的德拜类模型（Debye-like model）以两种方式拟合弛豫行为；同时通过直流输运（DC transport）测量提取激活能。

Result: 弛豫分析给出的能垒为286.1 ± 2.8 meV，直流输运激活能为288.8 ± 2.8 meV，两者在误差范围内高度一致。

Conclusion: 局域偶极子运动与可迁移载流子输运的能垒源自相同的原子尺度作用力；巨介电行为是一种微观体相现象（microscopic bulk phenomenon），源于系统处于金属性边缘（brink of metallicity）的状态。

Abstract: We measure the colossal permittivity in single crystal Fe$_2$TiO$_5$ using broadband spectroscopy in the frequency range 20 Hz - 1 MHz. The relaxation response is analyzed using a Debye-like model with Arrhenius activation in two different ways and yields an energy barrier of 286.1 $\pm$ 2.8 meV. DC transport yields an activation energy of 288.8 $\pm$ 2.8 meV. These results strongly imply that the energy barrier for localized dipole motion and itinerant charge transport originate from the same atom-level forces. A further implication is that colossal dielectric behavior is a microscopic bulk phenomenon arising from a system on brink of metallicity.

</details>


### [115] [Carrier scattering considerations and thermoelectric power factors of half-Heuslers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22033)
*Rajeev Dutt,Bhawna Sahni,Yao Zhao,Yuji Go,Saff E Awal Akhtar,Ankit Kumar,Sumit Kukreti,Patrizio Graziosi,Zhen Li,Neophytos Neophytou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过从头算玻尔兹曼输运计算，系统研究了13种半哈斯勒合金的电子和热电输运性质，发现室温下平均峰值功率因子在5–10 mW/mK²之间，且极性光学声子散射与电离杂质散射共同决定了约65%的热电功率因子，揭示了库仑散射过程在半哈斯勒合金热电性能中的主导作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解半哈斯勒合金中影响热电输运的关键散射机制，特别是区分库仑散射（极性光学声子与电离杂质散射）与非极性散射对热电功率因子（power factor, PF）的相对贡献，从而为材料优化提供理论基础。

Method: 采用玻尔兹曼输运（Boltzmann transport）方法，结合从头算（ab initio）提取的参数，完整计入了所有相关声子相互作用与电离杂质散射（ionized impurity scattering, IIS）的电子散射时间（scattering time），对13种n型和p型半哈斯勒合金进行理论计算。

Result: 室温下所有材料的平均峰值热电功率因子在5–10 mW/mK²之间；极性光学声子（polar optical phonon, POP）散射与电离杂质散射（IIS）共同决定了约65%的热电功率因子，其影响显著超过非极性声子相互作用（声学与光学声子输运）。

Conclusion: 库仑散射过程（POP和IIS）在半哈斯勒合金的热电性能中起决定性作用；计算代价较低的POP与IIS可作为功率因子的一阶近似估计，而非极性贡献（需更昂贵的从头算计算）为次要因素。该结论可推广至其他复杂能带结构材料。

Abstract: The electronic and thermoelectric (TE) transport properties of 13 n-type and p-type half-Heusler alloys are computationally examined using Boltzmann transport. The electronic scattering times resulting from all relevant phonon interactions and ionized impurity scattering (IIS) are fully accounted for using ab initio extracted parameters. We find that at room temperature the average peak TE power factors (PF) of all materials we examine reside between 5 and 10 mW/mK$^2$. We also find that IIS in combination with the long range polar optical phonon (POP) scattering are more influential in determining the electronic transport and PF over all other non-polar phonon interactions (acoustic and optical phonon transport). In fact, the combination of POP and IIS determines the thermoelectric power factor of the half-Heuslers examined on average by about 65\%. The results highlight the crucial impact of Coulombic scattering process (POP and IIS) on the TE properties of half-Heusler alloys and provide profound insight for understanding transport, which can be applied widely in other complex bandstructure materials. In terms of computation expense, the computationally cheaper POP and IIS provide an acceptable first-order estimate of the power factor of these materials, while the non-polar contributions, which require more expensive ab initio calculations, could be of secondary importance.

</details>


### [116] [Spin-polarized Energy Density Method from Spin-Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22044)
*Yang Dan,Dallas R. Trinkle*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于自旋密度泛函理论（spin-density functional theory）将能量密度方法推广至包含自旋极化（spin polarization）的情形，提出了一种将总能分解为唯一定义的原子的能量的形式化方法，并在VASP中实现，通过两个应用案例展示了该方法在磁性系统研究中的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有能量密度方法（energy density method）仅适用于非自旋极化系统，缺乏将总能分解为自旋极化原子能量（spin-polarized atomic energies）的通用形式化框架，限制了密度泛函理论（density functional theory，DFT）在磁性材料研究中的信息提取能力。

Method: 该方法包含两步：(1) 将总能（total energy）在实空间中分解为自旋极化能量密度函数；(2) 在选定的规范不变体积（gauge-invariant volumes）上对能量密度积分，得到唯一定义的原子能量，所有原子能量之和与DFT总能相差一个常数。该方法被数值实现在VASP（Vienna ab initio simulation package）中，基于投影缀加波方法（projector augmented-wave method，PAW）。

Result: 在第一个应用中，利用自旋特殊准随机结构（spin special quasirandom structures）对顺磁面心立方Fe进行建模，将自旋能量拟合至自旋团簇展开（spin cluster expansions）和深度神经网络（deep neural network）。在第二个应用中，计算了不同掺杂距离和自旋构型下稀磁半导体Ni掺杂GaN的原子能量分布。

Conclusion: 该方法能够从DFT计算中提取额外有用信息，为研究磁性系统（magnetic systems）提供了一种有效的原子尺度能量分解工具。

Abstract: The energy density method is generalized to include spin polarization with the full formalism derived based on spin-density functional theory, which aims at decomposing the total energy into well-defined atomic energies. The method involves two steps: (1) decomposing the total energy into spin-polarized energy density functions in real space, and (2) integrating these energy densities over chosen gauge-invariant volumes for uniquely defined atomic energies, whose summation over all the atoms restores the DFT total energy up to a constant difference. This method is numerically implemented into the Vienna ab initio simulation package for the projector augmented-wave method, and is showcased with two applications. In the first application, we model the paramagnetic face-centered cubic Fe using spin special quasirandom structures; the spin energies are fit to spin cluster expansions and a deep neural network. In the second application, we calculate the atomic energy distributions of dilute magnetic semiconductor Ni-doped GaN with different dopant distances and spin configurations. This method extracts additional useful information for the study of magnetic systems with density functional theory.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在新鲜刻蚀的钽和硅表面制备自组装有机单分子层（self-assembled organic monolayers）进行分子表面钝化；采用接触角测量、X射线光电子能谱（XPS）、傅里叶变换红外光谱（FTIR）和透射电子显微镜（TEM）进行表面表征；在约5-9 GHz频段进行微波测量。

Result: 表面表征确认形成了有序的纳米级薄膜并抑制了氧化物生成；在100 mK单光子能级下测得内禀品质因子（internal quality factor）高达1.8×10^6，相较原生氧化物的未处理器件提升约140%。功率和温度依赖性测量将该增强归因于TLS诱导演耗的减少。

Conclusion: 分子钝化方法能够有效工程化低损耗界面，为构建高相干超导量子器件提供了一条可扩展的路径。

Abstract: Tantalum is a promising platform for superconducting quantum circuits, yet coherence times remain limited by dielectric losses from interfacial two-level systems (TLS), exacerbated by native oxide regrowth. Here, we implement molecular surface passivation using self-assembled organic monolayers on freshly etched tantalum and silicon in coplanar waveguide resonators. Surface characterization by contact angle, XPS, FTIR and TEM confirm the formation of ordered, nanometer-thick films that suppress oxide formation. Microwave measurements in the ~5-9 GHz range reveal internal quality factors up to 1.8x10^6 in the single-photon regime at 100 mK, representing a ~140% improvement over untreated devices with native oxide. Power and temperature dependent measurements attribute this enhancement to reduced TLS-induced losses. These results demonstrate that molecular passivation effectively engineers low-loss interfaces and provides a scalable route toward high-coherence superconducting quantum devices.

### [118] [Dynamic Moiré Potentials and Robust Wigner Crystallization in Large-Scale Twisted Transition Metal Dichalcogenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22343)
*Yifan Ke,Chuanjing Zeng,Xinming Qin,Wei-Lin Tu,Wei Hu,Jinglong Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种结合DeePMD和DeepH框架与第一性原理计算的机器学习工作流，用于高效研究含3000原子以上的扭转双层过渡金属二硫属化物（TMDs）大尺度莫尔超胞的时间依赖性结构与电子响应。以WS₂为例，发现低温晶格振动与弛豫加深了莫尔势阱、压窄了最低导带并促进强局域电子态形成；基于此的密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）模拟揭示了稳健的维格纳结晶与Kagomé图案的三电子态，与近期实验一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大尺度莫尔体系（moiré systems）的动力学演化对于连接理论预测与实验观测至关重要，但传统方法难以处理含数千原子的实验相关莫尔超胞（moiré supercells）的实时结构-电子响应问题。

Result: 低温下晶格振动与弛豫导致莫尔势阱（moiré potential wells）加深、最低导带收窄，进而形成强局域化电子态（strongly localized electronic states）；DMRG模拟揭示了稳健的维格纳结晶（Wigner crystallization）以及具有Kagomé图案的三电子态（three-electron state），与近期实验观测吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作流为探索超越静态构型的大尺度莫尔超胞提供了实用路径，并为扭转二维材料中晶格动力学、电子局域化与涌现关联态（emergent correlated states）之间的相互作用提供了新见解。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamical evolution of large-scale moiré systems is crucial for connecting theoretical predictions with experimental observations. Here we develop a machine-learning-based workflow, integrating DeePMD and DeepH frameworks with first-principles calculations, to efficiently investigate time-dependent structural and electronic responses in twisted bilayer transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) with experimentally relevant moiré supercells containing over 3000 atoms. Using $\mathrm{WS_2}$ as a representative system, we show that low-temperature lattice vibrations and relaxation deepen the moiré potential wells, narrow the lowest conduction band, and facilitate the formation of strongly localized electronic states. Based on DFT-derived moiré potentials that incorporate these dynamical effects, density-matrix-renormalization-group (DMRG) simulations reveal robust Wigner crystallization and a kagomé-patterned three-electron state, consistent with recent experimental observations. Our workflow provides a practical route for exploring large moiré supercells beyond static configurations and offers new insight into the interplay between lattice dynamics, electronic localization, and emergent correlated states in twisted two-dimensional materials.

### [119] [Nature of point defects in bulk hexagonal diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22393)
*Ling Zhu,Xuanxuan Zhang,Guliqinayi Alimu,Chen-Min Dai,Chunlan Ma,Zenghua Cai*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），对HD中本征缺陷（intrinsic defects）、外掺杂原子（extrinsic dopants）及缺陷复合体（defect complexes）进行了系统研究。

Result: 碳空位（VC）主导本征导电性，间隙碳（Ci）不稳定；硼（B）作为良性受主增强p型导电性，氮（N）和磷（P）作为有效施主实现n型导电性；II族和IV族掺杂原子形成能高或呈中性电荷态，影响有限；VC、MgC及XV缺陷复合体在HD带隙内呈现多自旋与多电荷态，可作为色心用于量子比特。

Conclusion: 上述结果阐明了HD的缺陷物理机制，并展示了其在导电性工程（conductivity engineering）与量子技术（quantum technologies）中的广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Hexagonal diamond (HD), an exotic carbon allotrope recently synthesized in bulk form, exhibits superior mechanical properties compared to cubic diamond (CD) and holds promise for advanced industrial and quantum applications. Using first-principles calcu-lations, we systematically investigate intrinsic defects, extrinsic dopants, and defect complexes in HD. Our study shows that VC dominates intrinsic conductivity, while Ci is unstable. Among extrinsic dopants, boron acts as a benign acceptor enhancing p-type conductivity, whereas nitrogen and phosphorus serve as effective donors for n-type conductivity. Group II and Group IV dopants, however, introduce high formation energies or neutral charge states with limited impact. Furthermore, VC, MgC and XV defect com-plexes display multiple spin and charge states within the HD band gap, highlighting their potential as color centers for hosting qubits. These results not only clarify the defect physics of HD but also demonstrate its broader implications for conductivity engineering and quantum technologies.

### [120] [Accurate Nanoscale Mapping of Electric Fields across Random Grain Boundaries in Polycrystalline Oxides Using Precession-Assisted 4D-STEM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22398)
*Sangjun Kang,Hyeyoung Cho,Maximilian Töllner,Anna Rose Nelson,Ziming Ding,Xiaoke Mu,Di Wang,Wolfgang Rheinheimer,Kai Wang,Bai-Xiang Xu,Jakob Konstantin Laux,Mahmoud Serour,Karsten Albe,Andreas Klein,Christian Kübel*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合电子束旋进（electron beam precession）与先进后处理技术（Sobel滤波边缘检测与奇异值分解（singular value decomposition, SVD））的新方法，用于在扫描透射电子显微镜微分相差（STEM-DPC）中精确测量局部电场与电荷分布，有效消除了传统质心（center-of-mass, CoM）分析中由取向对比度和动力学散射引起的伪影。该方法通过精确修正纳米束电子衍射（NBED）图案中中心盘的位置，显著提升了BaTiO₃和SrTiO₃晶界电场测量的准确性与鲁棒性，并结合原子模拟进一步分离了空间电荷层（SCL）电场、平均内势差与元素偏析的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶界处的空间电荷层（space charge layers, SCLs）对局部电场调控及材料功能性质（如氧空位迁移与离子电导率）具有关键影响，但直接通过实验分析这些局域电场及其对应的电荷分布仍面临极大挑战。传统扫描透射电子显微镜微分相差（STEM-DPC）中的质心（center-of-mass, CoM）分析方法受取向依赖对比度与动力学散射（dynamical scattering）的强烈干扰，无法获得可靠结果。

Method: 将电子束旋进（electron beam precession）与先进后处理技术相结合，采用Sobel滤波器进行迭代边缘检测（iterative edge detection），并辅以奇异值分解（singular value decomposition, SVD），实现对纳米束电子衍射（nanobeam electron diffraction, NBED）图案中中心盘位置的精确修正。同时结合原子模拟（atomistic simulations），以分离空间电荷层电场、晶界平均内势差与元素偏析的贡献。

Result: 与传统的质心（CoM）分析方法相比，新方法在BaTiO₃和SrTiO₃随机晶界的测试案例中展现出更高的准确性与鲁棒性，能够实现无偏的衍射位移测量，并显著减少晶体学伪影。原子模拟进一步成功分离了空间电荷层电场、平均内势差与元素偏析三者的贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的方法能够在复杂多晶样品中实现高保真度的电磁场及其电荷分布映射，为利用STEM-DPC进行改进的定量分析奠定了基础。

Abstract: Space charge layers (SCLs) at grain boundaries play a crucial role in modulating local electric fields and influencing the functional properties of materials, such as oxygen vacancy migration and ionic conductivity in oxide ceramics. However, the direct experimental analysis of such localized electric fields and the corresponding charge distribution remains challenging. Conventional center-of-mass (CoM) analysis in scanning transmission electron microscopy differential phase contrast (STEM-DPC) is strongly affected by orientation-dependent contrast and dynamical scattering. Here, we demonstrate that combining electron beam precession with advanced post-processing, employing iterative edge detection via a Sobel filter and singular value decomposition (SVD), enables reliable and accurate, unbiased diffraction shift measurements with minimal crystallographic artefacts. The new method accurately refines the central disk position in nanobeam electron diffraction (NBED) patterns and thus significantly improves the extraction of the local electric field and corresponding charge distribution. Comparative analysis with conventional CoM methods shows superior accuracy and robustness for random grain boundaries in BaTiO3 and SrTiO3 as exemplary case studies. The experimental work is complemented by atomistic simulations to separate the electric field of the SCL from the mean inner potential difference of the grain boundary and the elemental segregation around the grain boundary. The in-depth analysis shows that our approach enables high-fidelity mapping of electromagnetic fields and their charge distribution in complex polycrystalline specimens, laying the groundwork for improved quantitative analysis using STEM-DPC.

TL;DR: 通过分子动力学模拟，研究了注入温度和剂量对4H-SiC中浅层Al注入缺陷演化与掺杂激活的影响，揭示了非单调退火行为、两个激活机制（新Al扩散路径与碳反位踢出机制），并指出可控纳米级非晶化可提升激活效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确Al注入4H-SiC过程中，注入温度与剂量如何影响缺陷演化与掺杂激活，解释实验中观察到的激活窗口（500–900 K），并寻找优化激活效率的动力学路径。

Method: 采用Gao-Weber势与重新参数化的Morse Al-SiC相互作用势（拟合自DFT迁移与踢入/踢出能垒），进行分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，并结合DFT-NEB（nudged elastic band）确认新扩散路径与激活机制。

Result: 较高注入温度减少了Frenkel对产生并抑制扩展非晶区；但在高剂量（>1e20 cm^-3）下，900 K注入比500 K注入形成更大、更稳定的间隙团簇，反而降低了取代位Al比例。退火后出现两个剂量区间：低剂量区以孤立点缺陷和小复合体为主，高剂量区以团簇与面缺陷形成为主且强烈依赖温度。识别出新的Al扩散路径与碳反位踢出激活机制。

Conclusion: 实验观察到的激活窗口可通过温度与剂量的竞争效应解释；可控纳米级非晶化通过再生长辅助掺入提升激活效率，同时限制扩展缺陷，为优化SiC掺杂工艺提供了微观机制指导。

Abstract: We present molecular dynamics simulations of shallow Al implantation in 4H-SiC to clarify how implantation temperature and dose control defect evolution and dopant activation during early annealing. Using the Gao-Weber potential together with a reparameterized Morse Al-SiC interaction fitted to DFT migration and kick-in/out barriers, we find that higher implantation temperature reduces Frenkel-pair production and suppresses extended amorphous pockets. Yet at high doses (>1e20 cm^-3), annealing shows non-monotonic behavior: samples implanted at 900 K form larger, more stable interstitial clusters than those implanted at 500 K. These clusters trap Al and lower substitutional incorporation. Within MD-accessible times, the fraction of lattice-site Al is therefore higher after 500 K implantation despite better as-implanted crystallinity at 900 K. After annealing, two regimes emerge around the Al solubility limit: a low-dose regime dominated by isolated point defects and small complexes, and a high-dose regime with clustering and planar-defect formation that is strongly temperature dependent. The results explain the experimentally observed activation window (500-900 K) and indicate a kinetic route in which controlled nanoscale amorphization improves activation through regrowth-assisted incorporation while limiting extended defects. We also identify a new Al diffusion path and a carbon-antisite kick-out activation mechanism, both confirmed by DFT-NEB.

</details>


### [122] [Classifying magnons in itinerant ferromagnets from linear response TDDFT: Fe, Ni and Co revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22484)
*Thorbjørn Skovhus,Thomas Olsen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过线性响应含时密度泛函理论（LR-TDDFT）框架，对巡游铁磁体的磁激发谱进行第一性原理计算，并基于自增强函数（self-enhancement function）对谱特征进行分类，区分相干与非相干集体激发，揭示了bcc-Fe中相干磁振子分支的共存以及fcc-Ni中近布里渊区边界处主磁振子分支的退相干现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 巡游磁体（itinerant magnets）的磁激发谱具有丰富而复杂的谱特征，包括阻尼、分支乃至完全消失等现象，这些特征往往使得对底层物理机制的解释变得困难。本文旨在通过多体谱函数本征模的细致分析，系统理解上述所有特征的物理起源。

Method: 采用线性响应含时密度泛函理论（linear response time-dependent density functional theory, LR-TDDFT）框架的新实现，对元素巡游铁磁体进行第一性原理（first principles）计算。通过自增强函数（self-enhancement function）——即无相互作用Kohn-Sham磁化率与交换关联核（exchange-correlation kernel）的乘积——对单个谱特征的集体性质进行分类。

Result: 基于自增强函数实部在磁振子谱峰处是否跨越1，区分相干（coherent）与非相干（incoherent）集体激发，并由虚部量化朗道阻尼（Landau damping）。计算表明：bcc-Fe中存在相干磁振子分支的共存；fcc-Ni中，在布里渊区（Brillouin zone, BZ）边界附近的波矢处，主磁振子分支发生退相干（decoherence），而非相干谷磁振子（incoherent valley magnons）承载了显著的谱权重。此外，该分析自然导出了多体Stoner谱（many-body Stoner spectrum）的定义，并允许量化Stoner对激发（Stoner pair excitations）的结合能。

Conclusion: 通过自增强函数对磁激发谱特征的分类，能够统一理解巡游磁体中磁振子谱的阻尼、分支与消失等复杂现象。该方法不仅揭示了相干与非相干集体激发的判据，还提供了多体Stoner谱的定义途径，为量化Stoner对激发结合能奠定了基础。

Abstract: The magnetic excitation spectrum of itinerant magnets exhibits rich and complex spectral features that often complicate interpretation of the underlying physics. For perturbations in the long wavelength limit, one obtains a well defined pole at zero frequency in the spectral function, the Goldstone magnon. However, for optical modes and finite wavevectors, the magnon spectrum may become damped, exhibit branching, or be completely washed out. In the present work, we show how the physical mechanism of all such features can be understood from careful analysis of the eigenmodes of the many-body spectral function. We perform first principles computations of elemental itinerant ferromagnets using a novel implementation of the linear response time-dependent density functional theory (LR-TDDFT) framework and classify the collective nature of individual spectral features based on the self-enhancement function, the product of the noninteracting Kohn-Sham susceptibility and the exchange-correlation kernel. In particular, we distinguish between coherent and incoherent collective excitations, depending on whether the real part of the self-enhancement function crosses unity at the spectral peak of the magnon, which may or may not be subject to Landau damping as quantified by the imaginary part. Classifying the computed magnon spectra accordingly, we observe coexistence of coherent magnon branches in bcc-Fe, as well as decoherence of the primary magnon branch in fcc-Ni for wave vectors near the BZ boundary where incoherent valley magnons instead carry substantial spectral weight. The analysis also naturally leads to a definition of the many-body Stoner spectrum and allows us to quantify the binding energy of the Stoner pair excitations.

### [123] [Magnetoelastic Waves in Ferromagnetic Thin Films Mediated by Dipolar Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22523)
*Hiroki Yoshida,Ryohei Kono,Manato Fujimoto,Motoki Asano,Daiki Hatanaka,Kei Yamamoto,Shuichi Murakami*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索铁磁薄膜中磁偶极相互作用如何介导磁弹耦合（magnetoelastic coupling），并建立相应的理论框架。

Method: 从麦克斯韦方程（Maxwell's equations）出发，在存在弹性形变（elastic deformations）的条件下推导偶极场（dipolar fields），构建耦合运动方程，并在钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜中进行数值计算。

Result: 预测了静磁波（magnetostatic waves）与兰姆波（Lamb waves）之间的杂化（hybridization），色散关系中存在反交叉（anti-crossings），杂化能隙（hybridization gaps）范围为0.1至数MHz。

Conclusion: 磁偶极相互作用（magnetic dipolar interactions）能够有效介导铁磁薄膜中的磁弹耦合，产生可观测的杂化效应。

Abstract: Magnetoelastic coupling mediated by magnetic dipolar interactions is theoretically investigated in ferromagnetic thin films under an in-plane magnetic field. We develop a theoretical description that incorporates dipolar fields derived from Maxwell's equations in the presence of elastic deformations. The resulting coupled equations of motion predict hybridization between magnetostatic and Lamb waves. Numerical calculations for a yttrium iron garnet (YIG) film reveal anti-crossings in the dispersion relations, with hybridization gaps ranging from $0.1$ to several MHz.

### [124] [Micromorphic effects in an octet truss lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22544)
*K. Goyal,R. S. Lakes*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过实验研究八面体桁架格栅（octet truss lattice）和肋及格栅（rib lattice）中的弹性波频散（elastic wave dispersion），发现低频段无频散、高频段出现由肋共振（rib resonance）引起的频散和截止频率（cut-off frequency）现象，并将其解释为微形态连续介质（micromorphic continua）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 比较八面体桁架格栅与已知具有强Cosserat弹性效应（Cosserat elastic effects）的肋及格栅在弹性波频散方面的行为差异，以揭示多孔点阵材料在波动传播中的微观结构效应。

Method: 实验方法：在不同长度的试样中以离散频率激发驻波（standing waves），测量波速随频率的变化规律，从而研究频散特性。

Result: 低频长波长区域呈现经典的无频散（non-dispersive）波动行为；当波长接近肋长度的数倍时，出现频散现象；材料存在截止频率，高于该频率时信号无法传播。

Conclusion: 频散和截止频率的物理起源是肋的共振行为。将多孔固体行为解释为微形态连续介质时，可揭示与单元胞（unit cell）柔度相关的弹性常数，该类常数反映胞元相对于整体材料的柔性。

Abstract: Elastic wave dispersion is studied in an octet truss lattice and compared with a designed rib lattice known to exhibit strong Cosserat elastic effects. Dispersion entails variation of wave speed with frequency. The phenomenon is experimentally investigated by exciting standing waves in specimens of different length at discrete frequencies. At lower frequencies corresponding to long wavelengths, wave propagation is classically non-dispersive. As wavelength approaches a small multiple of the rib length, dispersion is observed. The material exhibited cut-off frequencies above which no signals were propagated. The physical origin of the dispersion and cut-off is resonance of the ribs. Interpreted as micromorphic continua, cellular solid behavior reveals elastic constants associated with flexibility of the unit cell in comparison with that of the overall material.

</details>


### [125] [Influence of Ni Doping on the Structural, Morphological, Optical, and Electrical Properties of Nanocrystalline Cd1-xMnxS Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22561)
*Himanshu Sharma Pathok,Padma Pani Shahu,Himanshu Kalita,Prasanta Kumar Saikia*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Ni作为第二种过渡金属掺杂对Cd1-xMnxS三元体系的影响，利用离子尺寸效应和sp-d交换相互作用（sp-d exchange interactions）来调控晶格应变、缺陷密度和电子结构，从而为光电材料提供额外的性能调控自由度。

Method: 采用成本低廉的化学浴沉积（chemical bath deposition, CBD）法制备Ni掺杂Cd1-xMnxS（x=0.4）薄膜；利用X射线衍射（XRD）和高分辨率透射电子显微镜（HRTEM）表征晶体结构，场发射扫描电子显微镜（FESEM）分析形貌和厚度，紫外-可见光谱测量光学性质，电流-电压（I-V）测量评估电学性能。

Conclusion: Ni掺杂可有效调控Cd1-xMnxS薄膜的结构、光学和电学性能，所得薄膜在薄膜太阳能电池窗口层及相关光电设备中具有良好的应用前景。

Abstract: Ni-doped Cd1-xMnxS (x=0.4) thin films were prepared via a cost-effective chemical bath deposition (CBD) method to investigate their suitability for optoelectronic applications. Incorporation of a secondary transition metal such as Ni is expected to influence lattice strain, defect density, and electronic structure through ionic size effects and sp-d exchange interactions, thereby providing an additional degree of freedom for tuning the properties of Cd1-xMnxS-based ternary systems. X-ray diffraction (XRD) analysis confirmed the cubic zinc blende structure of the Cd1-xMnxS crystal, which was further corroborated by high-resolution transmission electron microscopy (HRTEM). Crystallinity increases where as microstrain and dislocation density found to be decreases as the doping concentration of Ni increases. Field emission scanning electron microscopy (FESEM) analysis revealed uniform, dense, and crack-free films with grain size increasing as a function of Ni content, and the FESEM cross-sectional images indicated a nearly constant thickness in the range of 181.2-189.1 nm. The films exhibited high optical transmittance (75-90%) in the visible and near-infrared (NIR) regions. The optical band gap decreases from 2.72 to 2.62 eV as the Ni concentration increases from 1% to 4%. Current-voltage (I-V) measurements revealed enhanced electrical conductivity, which further increased under illumination, confirming the photoconducting nature of the films. These results demonstrate that Ni doping effectively tunes the properties of Cd1-xMnxS thin films, highlighting their potential as efficient window layer materials for thin-film solar cells and related optoelectronic devices.

### [126] [Accurate calculation of Wannier centers, position matrix, and composite operators using translationally equivariant and higher-order finite differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22614)
*Jae-Mo Lihm,Minsu Ghim,Seung-Ju Hong,Cheol-Hwan Park*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对第一性原理计算中Wannier插值所需的位置算符与复合算符的有限差分计算，提出了两种改进方案：平移等变格式（translationally equivariant scheme）和高阶有限差分方法（higher-order finite-difference approach），并展示其在Wannier中心与展宽、电极化、轨道磁化及自旋霍尔电导等计算中显著降低误差、消除对称性破坏误差、改善k点采样收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动量空间中的Bloch波函数导数对研究量子几何（quantum geometry）以及固体的平衡与响应性质至关重要。在实际第一性原理计算中，这些导数通过Wannier插值获得，而插值所需的矩阵初值依赖于有限差分近似，其精度直接影响结果的收敛性与可靠性。现有有限差分方法存在误差较大且可能破坏系统对称性的问题，亟需改进。

Method: 本文提出两种关键改进：一是设计平移等变格式（translationally equivariant scheme），保持系统的底层对称性，显著减小有限差分误差；二是引入高阶有限差分方法（higher-order finite-difference approach），通过系统提高收敛阶数来更精确地逼近k空间导数。从实空间角度看，这些改进对应于在Wannier函数位置处更精确地近似位置算符（position operator）。此外，还提出了一种有限差分格式的泛化，可在保持精度的同时减少有限差分点数。

Result: 将该方法应用于Wannier中心与展宽（Wannier centers and spreads）、电极化（electric polarization）、非对角位置矩阵元（off-diagonal position matrix elements）、轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）及自旋霍尔电导（spin Hall conductivity）的计算，结果显示有限差分误差显著降低、对称性破坏误差被消除，且k点采样的收敛性得到改善。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法已在开源软件包中实现，并可在其他基于Wannier的代码中以极小的额外计算开销直接采用，具有良好的通用性与实用价值。

Abstract: The momentum-space derivatives of Bloch wavefunctions are essential for studying quantum geometry and the equilibrium and response properties of solids. In practical first-principles calculations, these derivatives are obtained via Wannier interpolation of position and related composite matrices. These matrices are initially evaluated on a coarse k-point grid using finite-difference approximations and then interpolated to a dense grid. The accuracy of the finite-difference approximation directly impacts the convergence and reliability of the result. In this work, we present two key improvements to the finite-difference calculation of position and composite operators for Wannier interpolation. First, we formulate a translationally equivariant scheme that preserves the underlying symmetries of the system and significantly reduces finite-difference errors. Second, we introduce a higher-order finite-difference approach that yields a more accurate approximation of the k-space derivatives by systematically increasing the convergence rate. From a real-space perspective, these improvements correspond to better approximations of the position operator at the locations of the Wannier functions. We also present a generalization of the finite-difference scheme, which may reduce the number of finite-difference points while maintaining accuracy. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our methods by applying them to the calculation of Wannier centers and spreads, electric polarization, off-diagonal position matrix elements, orbital magnetization, and spin Hall conductivity. Our results demonstrate significant reductions in finite-difference errors, elimination of symmetry-violating errors, and improved convergence with respect to k-point sampling. These methods have been implemented in the open-source packages and can be readily adopted in other Wannier-based codes with minimal computational overhead.

</details>


### [127] [Mechanical Scaling Laws and Deformation Behavior of Nanoporous Tantalum Microparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22726)
*J. I. Ramallo,N. Vázquez von Bibow,M. A. Monclús,I. McCue,M. C. Fuertes,C. J. Ruestes*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和模拟发现，液态金属脱合金（liquid metal dealloying, LMD）制备的单晶纳米多孔钽（np-Ta）遵循经典Gibson-Ashby标度律，与电化学脱合金制备的纳米多孔金不同。这种差异归因于CuBi金属浴热力学促进了更高的韧带连通性（ligament connectivity），并指出溶剂化学可作为调控力学响应的可调杠杆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有脱合金纳米多孔金属的力学标度律几乎完全基于电化学脱合金制备的纳米多孔金建立，但这些规律是否适用于其他脱合金方法制备的纳米多孔网络仍是一个悬而未决的问题（outstanding question）。

Method: 采用液态金属脱合金（LMD）法在熔融CuBi中处理TiTa合金，制备单晶纳米多孔钽（np-Ta）。对单个微粒进行纳米压痕（nanoindentation）以测量弹性模量和硬度，并结合分子动力学模拟揭示塑性变形机制。

Result: np-Ta的弹性模量为10-30 GPa，硬度为0.3-1.1 GPa，两者均与固体体积分数（solid volume fraction）呈Gibson-Ashby标度关系。该刚度-密度响应偏离了先前纳米多孔金的报道，归因于CuBi金属浴热力学增强的韧带连通性。分子动力学模拟显示np-Ta压痕过程中以位错主导的塑性（dislocation-dominated plasticity）为主，与扫描电镜观察到的压痕下有限致密化（limited densification）一致。

Conclusion: LMD中的溶剂化学（solvent chemistry）可作为调节韧带连通性的可调杠杆（tunable lever），从而影响纳米多孔金属的力学响应。

Abstract: The mechanical scaling laws of dealloyed nanoporous metals depart from classical Gibson-Ashby predictions for open-cell foams due to a decreased connectivity in their solid network. However, these scaling relations have been established almost exclusively on nanoporous gold produced by electrochemical dealloying, and it is an outstanding question whether the relations apply to nanoporous networks fabricated by other dealloying methods. Here, we investigate the mechanical response of single-crystalline nanoporous tantalum (np-Ta) produced by liquid metal dealloying (LMD) a TiTa alloy in molten CuBi. Nanoindentation of individual microparticles yields an elastic modulus of 10-30 GPa and a hardness of 0.3-1.1 GPa, both scaling with the solid volume fraction in agreement with Gibson-Ashby predictions. This stiffness-density response of np-Ta departs from previous reports on nanoporous gold and is attributed to enhanced ligament connectivity enabled by the thermodynamics of the CuBi metal bath. Molecular dynamics simulations reveal dislocation-dominated plasticity during indentation of np-Ta, consistent with scanning electron microscopy observations of limited densification beneath the indents, ruling out unusual deformation mechanisms as an origin of the observed scaling. These findings identify solvent chemistry in LMD as a tunable lever for ligament connectivity, and thus for the mechanical response of nanoporous metals.

</details>
